# 完善双向编译引擎

**Exported:** 2026-07-20T09:00:01.326Z

**Project:** workspace

---

## 完善双向编译引擎

### **You**

基于当前的项目状态，我建议按以下节奏推进：



第一阶段：补完双向编译引擎（1-2 周）

这是 DESIGN.md 定义的核心护城河，之前被针法库不完整卡住了，现在地基已经打好了。

具体任务：把 Monaco Editor 或 CodeMirror 6 接进来做编织语法编辑器，实现语法高亮和基于 abbrev 字段的自动补全；恢复文字→画布的回写能力（parseTextToGrid 代码还在，只是 UI 被移除了）；把 compileGridToText 的输出接到编辑器里做实时同步；恢复柔性校验的 UI 提示。

这一步做完，产品就从"网格编辑器"质变为"编织编译器"了。

第二阶段：打通 L1 换算闭环（3-5 天）

calculator 弹窗已经有了，但算出来的数字没有回写到画布。把它和 resizeGrid 连起来，实现"输入小样数据→自动调整画布尺寸→实时预览效果"的完整流程。这是从"玩具"到"实用工具"的关键一步，工作量不大但体验提升明显。

第三阶段：导出系统升级（1 周）

当前只有位图回退的 PDF 导出。需要实现矢量导出路径（svg2pdf），让放大 400% 时依然清晰；把三种导出模版（Professional/Draft/Social）的实际内容区分开，而不是只换了个按钮状态；补齐商用版的物料消耗单自动生成。

第四阶段：体验优化穿插进行

透明参考底图、快捷格点菜单（点击空格弹出迷你针法盘）、侧栏左右可调、画布边缘"+"号无限蔓延入口——这些可以穿插在上述阶段的间隙做，每个都是独立的小功能，不会阻塞主线。

第五阶段：AI 功能（远期）

图片识别、Text-to-Pattern、实物渲染这些涉及模型训练和后端服务，周期长、不确定性高，建议等前面四个阶段稳定后再启动。

核心思路是：先把护城河挖深（编译器），再把工具链打通（换算+导出），最后做体验打磨和 AI。

现在：补完双向编译引擎，继续优化双向编译引擎，但是从图解——>文字的逻辑已经是完整的，我希望你不要改变这个方向上的逻辑实现。

## 1. Overall Project Structure

The project lives at `D:\aaa-llx\MyKinttingDesign` with the main application under `MyKinttingDesignApp\`. It is a **React + TypeScript + Vite** single-page application.

**Key directories:**
- `src\components\` -- UI components (Grid, TextEditor, Navigator, SymbolPanel, GridPreview, SaveStatusIndicator, etc.)
- `src\store\` -- Zustand stores: `projectStore.ts` (central state), `canvasStore.ts` (viewport/interaction)
- `src\utils\` -- Core logic: `translator.ts` (bidirectional compiler), `coordinateTransform.ts`, `rowNumbering.ts`
- `src\configs\` -- `stitchRegistry.ts` (100+ stitch definitions), `spanRules.ts` (multi-cell sizing)
- `src\hooks\` -- `useInteractionStateMachine.ts` (keyboard shortcuts/mode switching)
- `src\exports\` -- PDF generation pipeline (`pdfGenerator.ts`, `watermarkEngine.ts`, `types.ts`)
- `src\workers\` -- `pdfWorker.ts` (Web Worker for PDF)
- `src\__tests__\` -- Unit tests for translator
- `public\svg-assets\StitchMasteryDash\` -- Hundreds of SVG stitch symbol files
- `public\fonts\` -- StitchMastery TTF font files
- `public\designs\` -- Reference design images

**Top-level files:** `DESIGN.md` (design blueprint), `package.json`, `vite.config.ts`, `tsconfig.json`, etc.

## 2. DESIGN.md Summary

Located at `D:\aaa-llx\MyKinttingDesign\DESIGN.md`, this is a V2.0 design blueprint defining 6 major modules:

1. **Bidirectional compilation engine** -- Grid-to-text and text-to-grid conversion
2. **Dynamic canvas** -- Konva.js-based grid rendering with virtual viewport
3. **Interaction system** -- Mode-based editing (SELECT/DRAW/ERASE/PAN)
4. **Sizing engine** -- Gauge calculator for stitch/row sizing
5. **AI features** -- Image-to-pattern conversion (placeholder)
6. **Copyright/export** -- PDF export with watermarks

**Notable divergence from design:** The DESIGN.md originally planned **Vue 3 + Pinia + Monaco/Codemirror editor + Python AI backend**. The actual implementation uses **React + Zustand + react-konva** and has **no code editor** (Monaco/Codemirror) integrated yet.

## 5. Files Related to Compile/Parse/Bidirectional/Editor/Monaco/Codemirror

---

## 6. Current State of parseTextToGrid and compileGridToText

Both functions live in `D:\aaa-llx\MyKinttingDesign\MyKinttingDesignApp\src\utils\translator.ts`.

### compileGridToText (Grid -> Text) -- WORKING, ACTIVELY USED

```typescript
export function compileGridToText(grid: CellData[][], options: CompileOptions = {}): string[]
```

- Takes a 2D grid of `CellData` and produces an array of text lines (one per row)
- Supports 3 locale outputs: `'abbr'` (abbreviations like "k", "p", "yo"), `'en'` (English names), `'zh'` (Chinese names)
- Handles row direction (`row1Top` option): when true, bottom row of grid is Row 1; when false, top row is Row 1
- RS rows (odd display numbers) read right-to-left; WS rows (even) read left-to-right
- Skips span children (only the root cell of a multi-cell stitch is emitted)
- Aggregates consecutive identical stitches (e.g., 3 consecutive k -> "3 k")
- Called automatically by `compileToText` in projectStore whenever the grid changes

### parseTextToGrid (Text -> Grid) -- IMPLEMENTED BUT NOT WIRED TO UI

```typescript
export function parseTextToGrid(text: string, cols: number): { grid: CellData[][]; results: ParsedRowResult[] }
```

- Parses text like `"Row 1: 3 k, 2 p."` back into grid cells
- Uses regex `Row\s+(\d+):(.+)` to extract row numbers and content
- Builds reverse lookup maps: abbreviation -> stitchId, Chinese label -> stitchId, English label -> stitchId
- Handles WS row inversion (even-numbered rows are read right-to-left)
- Returns both a reconstructed grid and validation results with `delta` (stitch count vs column width)
- Flexible validation: warns but does not block when stitch count exceeds column width

### Integration gap:

`applyTextToGrid` in `projectStore.ts` calls `parseTextToGrid` and rebuilds the grid, but **no UI component currently invokes it**. The TextEditor is read-only. There is no text input field, no editable textarea, and no Monaco/Codemirror editor connected to this function. The text-to-grid direction is fully implemented at the logic layer but has no user-facing entry point.

---

## 7. Current Editor/UI Components

### TextEditor (`src\components\TextEditor\TextEditor.tsx`)
- **Read-only** instruction display panel
- Shows compiled text lines as clickable buttons
- Clicking a row button highlights that row on the canvas via `setHighlightedRow`
- Locale toggle: Abbr / EN / Chinese
- Row direction toggle: Row 1 top / Row 1 bottom
- Uses `compileGridToText` via `useMemo` for reactive updates
- **Not a code editor** -- cannot accept text input

### Grid Canvas (`src\components\Grid\Grid.tsx`)
- ~480 lines, built on react-konva
- Virtual rendering: only renders cells visible in the current viewport
- Features: background, grid lines, stitch SVG images (via `StitchImage` component), row/column headers with display numbers, highlighted row overlay, selection rectangle (dashed blue), hover highlight (color varies by interaction mode)
- Interactions: Ctrl+wheel zoom, drag/middle-click/right-click pan, draw/erase with pointer events
- Uses `lastDrawPlacementRef` to prevent duplicate stitch placement on span areas

### Navigator / Minimap (`src\components\Navigator\Navigator.tsx`)
- Bird's-eye view using react-konva
- Shows occupied cells, viewport rectangle (red dashed border)
- Click/drag to navigate
- Displays selection details (cell position, stitch name, span info)

### Symbol Panel (`src\components\SymbolPanel\SymbolPanel.tsx`)
- Grid display of stitch symbols grouped by category (knit/crochet subcategories)
- Shows span badge for multi-cell stitches (e.g., "4 cells" for c4f)
- Click to select a stitch for drawing

### App Shell (`src\App.tsx`)
- ~1320 lines, 5 pages: workspace (knitting), library (stitch search), AI (image conversion), crochet, export (PDF)
- Workspace layout: Grid canvas on left + right sidebar with tool palette, TextEditor, progress tracker
- Top bar: page navigation tabs, project switcher dropdown (create/rename/duplicate/delete/recycle), mode toggle (knit/crochet), font status indicator, export button
- Gauge calculator dialog overlay
- PDF export with watermark configuration and 3 presets (professional/draft/social)
- AI page is a mock/placeholder with preset grid application

### State Management
- **projectStore.ts**: Central Zustand store with `persist` middleware (localforage + debounced autosave). Manages projects, grids, undo/redo stacks, text locale, row direction. Key actions: `applyCellChange`, `compileToText`, `applyTextToGrid`, `copySelection/cutSelection/pasteClipboard/moveSelection`, `resizeGrid`, `exportSnapshot`. Multi-project support with recycle bin (10-day soft delete).
- **canvasStore.ts**: Viewport state (offset, size, scale), interaction mode (SELECT/DRAW/ERASE/PAN), selection, hover, highlighted row. Supports temp pan mode via Space key hold.

### Interaction (`src\hooks\useInteractionStateMachine.ts`)
- Keyboard shortcuts: V=SELECT, B=DRAW, E=ERASE, H=PAN, Space=temp PAN
- Ctrl+Z=undo, Ctrl+Shift+Z / Ctrl+Y=redo
- Ctrl+C/X/V for copy/cut/paste
- Skips handling when focus is in input/textarea/contentEditable elements

### Stitch Registry (`src\configs\stitchRegistry.ts`)
- ~1558 lines, 100+ stitch definitions
- Each stitch: id, nameZh, nameEn, abbrev, wsStitchId (wrong-side mapping), svgPath, span, renderOffset, color, category
- Knit categories: basics (k/p/yo), decreases (k2tog/ssk/k3tog/s2kp...), increases (m1l/m1r/kfbl...), slip stitches, twisted stitches, cables (c2f through c10b), special (bobble/nupp/lt/rt), crossed decreases, variants, blanks
- Crochet categories: basics (ch/sc/hdc/dc/slst/tr/dtr), post stitches (fpdc/bpdc...), decreases, increases, special (pop/shell/puff/cluster/picot/bean/spike...), V-stitch/X-stitch/star/suzette

---

## Key Architectural Findings

1. **The bidirectional engine is half-wired.** Grid-to-text works end-to-end (grid change -> compileToText -> TextEditor display). Text-to-grid has full logic (`parseTextToGrid` + `applyTextToGrid`) but no UI trigger -- there is no editable text area connected to it.

2. **No code editor exists.** Despite DESIGN.md planning Monaco or CodeMirror integration, neither is present. The TextEditor is purely a display component.

3. **The compilation pipeline is solid.** The translator handles all the complex edge cases: RS/WS direction, span children, stitch aggregation, multiple locales, flexible validation with delta reporting.

4. **The stitch system is comprehensive.** 100+ stitches with full RS/WS mapping, SVG rendering paths, span rules for multi-cell stitches, and category organization.

5. **The app is feature-rich on the canvas side.** Virtual rendering, zoom/pan, selection, copy/paste, undo/redo, navigator minimap, symbol panel, gauge calculator, PDF export -- all working. The missing piece is the editable text editor that would complete the bidirectional workflow.

1	# 🧶 编织设计平台 (Knit/Crochet Design Platform) 全功能设计蓝图 V2.0 
2	
3	## 一、 图文双向编译引擎 (核心护城河)
4	系统的底层数据不再是单纯的图片，而是一套标准的“编织指令集（JSON）”。
5	* **图形 -> 文字 (Chart to Written)：** 画布上的每一次修改，实时按行（Row/Round）解析并翻译为文字说明；自动合并连续的重复针法（如：下针 10）；支持一键切换多语言（英文缩写、日文习惯、中文习惯）。
6	* **文字 -> 图形 (Written to Chart)：** 提供 IDE 级别的“编织语法编辑器”，支持标准缩写的高亮与自动补全。输入代码，画布实时生成对应格点。
7	* **柔性纠错机制：** 当文字输入的针数与上一行结构不匹配时，系统仅在行侧进行“黄色高亮警告”（如提示针数差值），但不强制拦截，允许高阶用户的异形加减针设计存在。
8	
9	## 二、 动态画布与底层渲染空间
10	* **基础架构：** 基于 HTML5 Canvas 的正方形网格底层。支持用户预设初始尺寸（如 300x300），并引入“坐标原点”概念进行绝对定位。
11	* **无限蔓延逻辑：** 画布边缘自带“+”号，点击即动态增加行列，告别固定死板的画板限制。
12	* **悬浮跨格投影：** 针法组件（如占 4 格的大麻花）通过锚点和跨度属性“悬浮”于网格之上，不破坏底层的 1:1 坐标系。
13	* **边界遮罩 (Masking)：** 支持“半个针法”的存在。当组件移至或粘贴至画布边缘时，溢出部分自动隐藏（不可见），但底层 JSON 数据保持完整，拉回中心即自动复原。
14	
15	## 三、 交互与操作体验
16	* **双模独立空间：** 棒针（Knitting）与钩针（Crochet）模式相互独立。支持在当前模式下，挂载另一个模式（或外部图片）作为**“透明参考底图”**，便于复刻和临摹。
17	* **快捷格点菜单：** 点击画布任意空格弹出迷你针法盘，支持上下滑动快速选针；彻底释放屏幕空间，减少鼠标的长距离移动。
18	* **灵活侧边栏：** 左右可调、支持一键收起的总针法字库。
19	* **智能剪贴板：** 矩形框选多选区，支持跨区域复制粘贴。若粘贴区域不足，触发弹窗（自动扩充画布 vs 按边界截断）。
20	
21	## 四、 尺码换算与结构引擎
22	* **L1 线性换算 (基于小样)：** 用户输入试织小样（Swatch）的 $10\text{cm} \times 10\text{cm}$ 针/行数，系统进行全局基础的针数推算。
23	* **L2 拓扑换算 (基于结构关键点)：** 用户标记图解的关键节点（如腋下起步点、领口最高点），AI 学习非线性的距离逻辑，自动计算大/小码在特定区域的加减针频率。
24	
25	## 五、 AI 智能大脑与生成流
26	* **纸面逆向工程：** 上传清晰的图片或 PDF 图解，AI 识别针法并自动转化为 Canvas 中可直接拖拽编辑的活组件。
27	* **Text-to-Pattern (定制生成流)：**
28	    1. **草图层：** 用户输入需求（如“复古风麻花开衫”）及身体维度，生成静态图解预览。
29	    2. **自然语言微调：** 不设复杂的滑块，用户直接通过对话（如“袖子改瘦一点”）让 AI 迭代草图。
30	    3. **一键组件化：** 确认无误后，将草图“爆破”为 Canvas 上的可编辑活组件，进入精修阶段。
31	* **实物渲染：** 基于当前的二维图解，AI 一键生成 2D/3D 的毛线质感实物模拟图。
32	
33	## 六、 版权确权与分发导出
34	* **强制署名与隔离训练：** 导入外部图解以训练 L2 换算模型时，强制签署版权声明（原创或引用）。用户上传的外部训练数据仅在**本地/当前项目内生效**，项目删除即销毁，绝不上传云端污染大模型或侵权。
35	* **智能裁切：** 导出时系统自动计算有效像素范围，过滤掉未使用的空白网格。
36	* **分级导出模版：**
37	    * **分享预览版：** 实物渲染图 + 局部缩略图解 + 全局防盗水印（适合社交媒体展示）。
38	    * **交流草稿版：** 低清黑白图解 + 底部固定作者署名（适合群内答疑）。
39	    * **商用专业版 (PDF)：** 高清无水印矢量图解 + 自动生成的物料消耗单 + 文字图解说明（适合售卖或个人打印）。
40	
41	
42	
43	# 技术栈限定
44	### 1. 核心前端框架：Vue 3 (Composition API) + Pinia
45	* **理由：**
46	    * **Vue 3** 的响应式系统非常适合处理这种“一处修改、多处同步”的场景。
47	    * **Pinia** 作为状态管理中心，负责存储那套核心的 **JSON 指令集**。无论是 Canvas 还是文字编辑器，都只从 Pinia 中读取数据。
48	* **限定原则：** 强制使用 **TypeScript**。编织针法数据极其复杂，必须通过 `Interface` 严格定义 `Stitch`、`Coordinate`、`ProjectSchema` 等类型，否则后期重构 AI 转换逻辑时会陷入泥潭。
49	
50	### 2. 画布渲染层：Konva.js 或 PixiJS
51	* **理由：**
52	    * **Konva.js：** 它是一个 2D 渲染库，天生支持“对象化”操作。你可以把每一个针法组件当作一个 `Group` 或 `Shape`，非常方便处理**锚点定位**、**拖拽**和**遮罩 (Clip)**。
53	    * **PixiJS：** 如果你追求极致性能（比如同时显示 10000+ 格子），PixiJS 的 WebGL 加速更强。
54	* **限定原则：** 禁止直接操作原生 Canvas API。必须使用具备“层级管理”能力的库，以便实现“背景参考层”与“主绘图层”的自由切换。
55	
56	### 3. 文字编辑器：Monaco Editor 或 CodeMirror 6
57	* **理由：**
58	    * 你希望实现“文字驱动图形”，这本质上是在写代码。
59	    * 这些库支持**自定义语法高亮**和**自动补全**。你可以定义一套编织 DSL（领域特定语言），当用户输入 `K2`（两针下）时，编辑器能变色并提示。
60	* **限定原则：** 必须支持 **LSP (Language Server Protocol)** 思想。将文字解析逻辑独立出来，确保同一套解析代码既能运行在前端，也能在未来迁移到后端。
61	
62	### 4. AI 与算法层：Python (FastAPI) + ONNX Runtime (前端)
63	* **理由：**
64	    * **识别与生成：** 图像识别、PDF 解析、T2P 生成（Text-to-Pattern）目前最成熟的生态在 Python (PyTorch/TensorFlow)。
65	    * **前端落地：** 为了降低服务器压力并保护隐私，简单的针法识别可以转换成 **ONNX 格式**，直接在浏览器里用插件调用用户的显卡进行推理。
66	* **限定原则：** 涉及用户版权图解的训练逻辑，**必须限定在本地内存运行**，绝不进行持久化云端存储。
67	
68	### 5. 文档与导出：jsPDF + Canvas-to-Blob
69	* **理由：**
70	    * 用于生成高清 PDF。通过控制 Canvas 的 `scale`，可以在导出时渲染比屏幕显示高 4 倍的像素，确保打印清晰。
71	* **限定原则：** PDF 导出必须在 **Worker 线程** 处理，避免大规模图解导出时导致 UI 卡顿。
72	
73	---
74	
75	### 总结：技术栈限定清单
76	
77	| 维度 | 推荐技术 | 限制要求 |
78	| :--- | :--- | :--- |
79	| **编程语言** | **TypeScript** | 严禁使用 `any`，所有数据模型必须定义 Type/Interface。 |
80	| **逻辑框架** | **Vue 3 + Pinia** | 状态必须单向流动：UI -> Action -> State -> View。 |
81	| **画布引擎** | **Konva.js** | 必须封装为 Vue 组件，利用其图层 (Layer) 系统实现参考图功能。 |
82	| **样式管理** | **Tailwind CSS** | 保持 UI 清爽，特别是侧边栏折叠和浮动菜单的布局。 |
83	| **通信协议** | **JSON (AST-based)** | 图形与文字的转换必须基于一套中间 AST 结构。 |
84	| **构建工具** | **Vite** | 极速的热更新，对大型 Canvas 项目开发友好。 |
85	
86	
87	# 可参考模块
88	在**Canvas引擎、文本编辑器编译器、以及AI识别**这三个核心维度，有非常优秀的开源基座可以“缝合”并二次开发。
89	
90	以下是针对各模块的开源选型参考：
91	
92	### 1. 画布引擎与网格系统 (模块二、三)
93	由于你需要实现“悬浮跨格”、“无限蔓延”和“遮罩”，以下库最适合作为底层：
94	
95	* **Konva.js (推荐):** * **理由：** 它是最适合做“对象化”Canvas的库。你可以轻松地将每一个针法定义为一个 `Konva.Group`。它自带的 `clip` 功能可以完美解决你的“遮罩 (Masking)”需求。
96	    * **参考代码：** 搜索 “Konva Infinite Grid” 或 “Konva Canvas Editor” 的 GitHub 案例。
97	* **Fabric.js:** * **理由：** 强大的对象选择、缩放、组合功能（Group），适合实现你的“矩形框选多选区”和“智能剪贴板”。
98	* **React-Diagrams / Svelte-Flow (逻辑借鉴):** * 虽然是连线图库，但它们处理“无限画布”和“坐标原点锚点”的逻辑非常成熟，可以参考其 `ViewPort` 的实现。
99	
100	### 2. 图文双向编译引擎 (模块一)
101	这是你的核心护城河，建议借鉴“领域特定语言 (DSL)”的开源工具：
102	
103	* **Antlr4 / Chevrotain:**
104	    * **用途：** 编写编织语法（如 `K2, P2`）的解析器。Chevrotain 是一个极其快速的 JavaScript 解析器构建库，非常适合在浏览器端实现“文字 -> JSON”的实时转换。
105	* **Monaco Editor (VS Code 核心):**
106	    * **用途：** 实现“编织语法编辑器”。你可以通过 `monaco.languages.setMonarchTokensProvider` 自定义编织针法的语法高亮。
107	* **Stitch Fiddle (非开源但可参考):** * 这是目前最接近你的产品，你可以观察其格点数据与描述文字的交互逻辑。
108	
109	### 3. AI 识别与生成 (模块五)
110	将图片转化为可编辑的格点，本质上是图像分割与特征匹配：
111	
112	* **Segment Anything Model (SAM) by Meta:**
113	    * **用途：** 预处理。用户上传图解图片，SAM 可以自动抠出每一个符号的轮廓。
114	* **YOLOv8 / TensorFlow.js:**
115	    * **用途：** 训练一个微型的“针法符号识别模型”。你可以收集常见图解符号（麻花、加针等），在前端使用 TensorFlow.js 进行实时识别。
116	* **ControlNet (Stable Diffusion):**
117	    * **用途：** 实现“图解 -> 实物图”。你可以利用 ControlNet 的 `Canny` 边缘检测功能，将你的 Canvas 线稿作为输入，引导 AI 生成具有毛线质感的实物图。
118	
119	### 4. 尺码换算与结构 (模块四)
120	* **D3.js:** * **用途：** 你的 L2 拓扑换算本质上是“几何变形”。D3 具有强大的数学拓扑和坐标转换函数，适合处理关键点（腋下、领口）标记后的网格拉伸算法。
121	
122	### 总结：你的技术栈“拼图”建议
123	
124	| 蓝图模块 | 核心开源建议 | 备注 |
125	| :--- | :--- | :--- |
126	| **底层画布** | **Konva.js** | 配合 Vue 3 的 `shallowRef` 提升性能。 |
127	| **编译器** | **Chevrotain + Monaco** | 处理文字与 JSON 的同步逻辑。 |
128	| **AI 识别** | **SAM + ONNX Runtime** | 建议在前端完成识别，保护版权隐私。 |
129	| **实物渲染** | **Stable Diffusion API** | 后端接入，生成写实的实物预览。 |
130	| **PDF 导出** | **jsPDF + html2canvas** | 处理裁切与清晰度。 |
131	
```

1	import { stitchRegistry } from '../configs/stitchRegistry';
2	import { CellData } from '../store/projectStore';
3	import { displayRowNumber, type RowNumberDirection } from './rowNumbering';
4	
5	export interface ValidationResult {
6	  valid: boolean;
7	  delta: number;
8	  message: string;
9	}
10	
11	export type TextLocale = 'abbr' | 'en' | 'zh';
12	
13	export interface CompileOptions {
14	  locale?: TextLocale;
15	  rowNumberDirection?: RowNumberDirection;
16	}
17	
18	export interface ParsedRowResult {
19	  rowNumber: number;
20	  cells: CellData[];
21	  validation: ValidationResult;
22	}
23	
24	/**
25	 * 提取连续相同的针法并聚合
26	 */
27	function aggregateStitches(instructions: string[]): string[] {
28	  const aggregated: string[] = [];
29	  let currentStitch = '';
30	  let count = 0;
31	
32	  const flush = () => {
33	    if (count > 0) {
34	      aggregated.push(count === 1 ? currentStitch : `${count} ${currentStitch}`);
35	    }
36	  };
37	
38	  for (const inst of instructions) {
39	    if (inst === currentStitch) {
40	      count++;
41	    } else {
42	      flush();
43	      currentStitch = inst;
44	      count = 1;
45	    }
46	  }
47	  flush();
48	
49	  return aggregated;
50	}
51	
52	function normalizeLabel(label: string) {
53	  return label.trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ').toLowerCase();
54	}
55	
56	function resolveDisplayLabel(stitchId: string, locale: TextLocale, isEvenRow: boolean) {
57	  const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[stitchId];
58	  if (!stitchDef) {
59	    return stitchId;
60	  }
61	
62	  const resolvedId = isEvenRow && stitchDef.wsStitchId ? stitchDef.wsStitchId : stitchId;
63	  const resolvedDef = stitchRegistry[resolvedId] ?? stitchDef;
64	
65	  if (locale === 'zh') {
66	    return resolvedDef.nameZh ?? stitchDef.nameZh ?? stitchId;
67	  }
68	
69	  if (locale === 'en') {
70	    return resolvedDef.nameEn ?? stitchDef.nameEn ?? resolvedDef.nameZh ?? stitchId;
71	  }
72	
73	  return resolvedDef.abbrev ?? stitchDef.abbrev ?? resolvedDef.nameEn ?? resolvedDef.nameZh ?? stitchId;
74	}
75	
76	/**
77	 * 将二维网格编译为自然语言文字说明
78	 */
79	export function compileGridToText(grid: CellData[][], options: CompileOptions = {}): string {
80	  if (!grid || grid.length === 0) return '';
81	  
82	  const locale = options.locale ?? 'abbr';
83	  const rowNumberDirection = options.rowNumberDirection ?? 'row1_top';
84	  const textLines: string[] = [];
85	  const rows = grid.length;
86	  const cols = grid[0].length;
87	
88	  const rowIndices =
89	    rowNumberDirection === 'row1_top'
90	      ? Array.from({ length: rows }, (_, row) => row)
91	      : Array.from({ length: rows }, (_, row) => rows - 1 - row);
92	
93	  for (const r of rowIndices) {
94	    const rowNumber = displayRowNumber(r, rows, rowNumberDirection);
95	    const isEvenRow = rowNumber % 2 === 0;
96	    
97	    // 奇数行（正面 RS）从右向左读图；偶数行（反面 WS）从左向右读图
98	    let colIndices = Array.from({ length: cols }, (_, i) => i);
99	    if (!isEvenRow) {
100	      colIndices = colIndices.reverse();
101	    }
102	    
103	    const rowRawInstructions: string[] = [];
104	    let hasStitchInRow = false;
105	    
106	    for (const c of colIndices) {
107	      const cell = grid[r][c];
108	      
109	      // 跳过没有对应源针法的格子（或是跨格的子节点。因为跨格的主节点通常是在左上或者自身）
110	      // TODO: 此处我们简化，只要是 isSpanChild 就跳过，让 root 单独报告
111	      if (cell.isSpanChild) continue;
112	      
113	      if (!cell.stitchId) {
114	        continue;
115	      }
116	      hasStitchInRow = true;
117	      
118	      const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
119	      if (!stitchDef) continue;
120	      
121	      const displayLabel = resolveDisplayLabel(cell.stitchId, locale, isEvenRow);
122	      
123	      // 针对部分多列针法，比如 c4f 需要占用的针数，这里仅简单视作一个整体指令
124	      rowRawInstructions.push(displayLabel);
125	    }
126	    
127	    if (hasStitchInRow) {
128	      const merged = aggregateStitches(rowRawInstructions);
129	      textLines.push(`Row ${rowNumber}: ${merged.join(', ')}.`);
130	    }
131	  }
132	  
133	  return textLines.join('\n');
134	}
135	
136	/**
137	 * 建立反向字典表，用于将简写映射回 stitchId
138	 */
139	const abbrevToStitchId: Record<string, string> = {};
140	const labelToStitchId: Record<string, string> = {};
141	Object.values(stitchRegistry).forEach(def => {
142	  // 这里我们直接映射为图解符号，因此都是正面视角 (RS) 的原始符号 ID
143	  if (def.abbrev) abbrevToStitchId[normalizeLabel(def.abbrev)] = def.id;
144	  if (def.nameEn) labelToStitchId[normalizeLabel(def.nameEn)] = def.id;
145	  if (def.nameZh) labelToStitchId[normalizeLabel(def.nameZh)] = def.id;
146	});
147	
148	/**
149	 * 解析用户输入的自然语言，转换为对应这行的 Grid Cell 结构。
150	 * Demo 版核心链路：按行解析如 "Row 1: 3 k, 2 p"
151	 */
152	export function parseTextToGrid(text: string, cols: number): ParsedRowResult[] {
153	  const results: ParsedRowResult[] = [];
154	  const lines = text.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim() !== '');
155	  
156	  // Row 匹配正则，例如: "Row 1: 3 k, 2 p." / "Row 1: 3 knit, 2 purl."
157	  const rowRegex = /Row\s+(\d+):(.+)/i;
158	  
159	  for (const line of lines) {
160	    const rowMatch = line.match(rowRegex);
161	    if (!rowMatch) continue;
162	    
163	    const rowNumber = parseInt(rowMatch[1], 10);
164	    const instructionsPart = rowMatch[2];
165	    
166	    // 正面行（奇数行），从右往左布置
167	    // 反面行（偶数行），从左往右布置
168	    const isEvenRow = rowNumber % 2 === 0;
169	    
170	    const cells: CellData[] = [];
171	    let stitchCount = 0; // 这行指令要求的总格子数
172	    
173	    const instructionSegments = instructionsPart.split(',').map(part => part.trim()).filter(Boolean);
174	    for (const segment of instructionSegments) {
175	      const segmentMatch = segment.match(/^(?:(\d+)\s*)?(.+?)\.?$/);
176	      if (!segmentMatch) continue;
177	
178	      const count = segmentMatch[1] ? parseInt(segmentMatch[1], 10) : 1;
179	      const rawLabel = segmentMatch[2].trim();
180	      const normalizedLabel = normalizeLabel(rawLabel);
181	      
182	      // 查反向映射
183	      let targetStitchId = abbrevToStitchId[normalizedLabel] ?? labelToStitchId[normalizedLabel];
184	      
185	      if (!targetStitchId) {
186	        // 如果找不到，直接跳过或者记录个 warning，这里暂跳过
187	        continue;
188	      }
189	      
190	      // 反面行的输入需要反转回去以作为图解在界面上显示。由于图解永远是正面的。
191	      // 如果输入文本说反面(Even Row)要织 p，意味着我们在图纸上它是 k-knit。
192	      if (isEvenRow) {
193	        const potentialTargetStr = Object.values(stitchRegistry).find(
194	          def => def.wsStitchId === targetStitchId
195	        )?.id;
196	        if (potentialTargetStr) targetStitchId = potentialTargetStr;
197	      }
198	      
199	      for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
200	        cells.push({
201	          char: '',
202	          stitchId: targetStitchId
203	        });
204	        
205	        // 简单计算一下针法跨格 (复杂多格针法例如 c4f 可能需要在渲染端另作补全，这里暂按占用首格算)
206	        stitchCount += (stitchRegistry[targetStitchId]?.span?.width || 1);
207	      }
208	    }
209	    
210	    // 柔性校验
211	    let delta = stitchCount - cols;
212	    let valid = delta <= 0; // 只要没超出列宽就算有效，或者你也可以设为严格等于
213	    let message = '✅ 解析成功';
214	    if (delta > 0) {
215	      message = `⚠️ 这行需要 ${stitchCount} 针，但画板宽度仅为 ${cols}，超出了 ${delta} 针。`;
216	    } else if (delta < 0) {
217	      message = `ℹ️ 这行排布后画布剩余 ${Math.abs(delta)} 针空白。`;
218	    }
219	    
220	    results.push({
221	      rowNumber,
222	      cells,
223	      validation: { valid, delta, message }
224	    });
225	  }
226	  
227	  return results;
228	}
229	
```

173	const isPlainObject = (value: unknown): value is Record<string, unknown> =>
174	  typeof value === 'object' && value !== null && !Array.isArray(value);
175	
176	const storageReplacer = (_key: string, value: unknown) => {
177	  if (value instanceof Map) {
178	    return { __type: 'Map', value: Array.from(value.entries()) };
179	  }
180	  if (value instanceof Set) {
181	    return { __type: 'Set', value: Array.from(value.values()) };
182	  }
183	  if (value instanceof Date) {
184	    return { __type: 'Date', value: value.toISOString() };
185	  }
186	  return value;
187	};
188	
189	const storageReviver = (_key: string, value: unknown) => {
190	  if (!isPlainObject(value) || typeof value.__type !== 'string') {
191	    return value;
192	  }
193	
194	  switch (value.__type) {
195	    case 'Map':
196	      return new Map(value.value as Array<[unknown, unknown]>);
197	    case 'Set':
198	      return new Set(value.value as Array<unknown>);
199	    case 'Date':
200	      return new Date(value.value as string);
201	    default:
202	      return value;
203	  }
204	};

206	const normalizeProject = (project: any): Project => ({
207	  id: typeof project.id === 'string' ? project.id : crypto.randomUUID(),
208	  name: typeof project.name === 'string' ? project.name : 'Untitled Project',
209	  lastModified: typeof project.lastModified === 'number' ? project.lastModified : Date.now(),
210	  thumbnail: typeof project.thumbnail === 'string' ? project.thumbnail : undefined,
211	  version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
212	  grids:
213	    project?.grids && typeof project.grids === 'object'
214	      ? {
215	          knit: Array.isArray(project.grids.knit) ? project.grids.knit : [],
216	          crochet: Array.isArray(project.grids.crochet) ? project.grids.crochet : [],
217	        }
218	      : { knit: [], crochet: [] },
219	  currentMode: project.currentMode === 'crochet' ? 'crochet' : 'knit',
220	  description: typeof project.description === 'string' ? project.description : '',
221	  textLocale: normalizeTextLocale(project.textLocale),
222	  rowNumberDirection: normalizeRowNumberDirection(project.rowNumberDirection),
223	  undoStack: Array.isArray(project.undoStack) ? project.undoStack : [],
224	  redoStack: Array.isArray(project.redoStack) ? project.redoStack : [],
225	});

227	const getRootPosition = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number) => {
228	  const cell = grid[row]?.[col];
229	  if (!cell) return null;
230	  if (cell.isSpanChild && cell.parentPos) return cell.parentPos;
231	  return { row, col };
232	};
233	
234	const clearStitchAtRoot = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number) => {
235	  const root = getRootPosition(grid, row, col);
236	  if (!root) return false;
237	  const cell = grid[root.row]?.[root.col];
238	  if (!cell?.stitchId) return false;
239	
240	  const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
241	  const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
242	  const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
243	  let changed = false;
244	
245	  for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
246	    for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
247	      const target = grid[root.row + i]?.[root.col + j];
248	      if (target) {
249	        grid[root.row + i][root.col + j] = {};
250	        changed = true;
251	      }
252	    }
253	  }
254	
255	  return changed;
256	};
257	
258	const placeStitchSnapshot = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number, snapshot: CellData) => {
259	  if (!snapshot.stitchId) return false;
260	  const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[snapshot.stitchId];
261	  const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
262	  const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
263	
264	  if (row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > grid.length || col + spanW > (grid[0]?.length ?? 0)) {
265	    return false;
266	  }
267	
268	  for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
269	    for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
270	      if (i === 0 && j === 0) {
271	        grid[row][col] = {
272	          ...snapshot,
273	          isSpanChild: false,
274	          parentPos: undefined,
275	          svgPath: snapshot.svgPath || stitchDef?.svgPath || '',
276	        };
277	      } else {
278	        grid[row + i][col + j] = {
279	          char: '',
280	          svgPath: '',
281	          stitchId: snapshot.stitchId,
282	          isSpanChild: true,
283	          parentPos: { row, col },
284	        };
285	      }
286	    }
287	  }
288	
289	  return true;
290	};
291	
292	// Config localforage
293	const localforageInstance = (localforage as any).default ?? localforage;
294	const storage = localforageInstance.createInstance({
295	  name: 'kintting-design-db',
296	  storeName: 'projects'
297	});
298	
299	localforageInstance
300	  .setDriver([localforageInstance.INDEXEDDB, localforageInstance.WEBSQL, localforageInstance.LOCALSTORAGE])
301	  .catch(() => {
302	    console.warn('localforage failed to set preferred drivers; falling back to defaults');
303	  });
304	
305	const forageStorage: StateStorage = {
306	  getItem: async (name: string): Promise<string | null> => {
307	    let val = (await storage.getItem(name)) as string | null;
308	    // Legacy migration step from simple localStorage
309	    if (!val && typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.localStorage) {
310	      val = window.localStorage.getItem(name);
311	      if (val) {
312	        try {
313	          await storage.setItem(name, val);
314	        } catch (e) {
315	          console.warn('Failed to migrate item to localforage', e);
316	        }
317	      }
318	    }
319	    return val || null;
320	  },
321	  setItem: async (name: string, value: string): Promise<void> => {
322	    await storage.setItem(name, value);
323	  },
324	  removeItem: async (name: string): Promise<void> => {
325	    await storage.removeItem(name);
326	  },
327	};
328	
329	// Default autosave debounce delay (ms). Increase to reduce save frequency.
330	const DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS = 10000;
331	const AUTOSAVE_DELAY_STORAGE_KEY = 'kintting:autosaveDelayMs';
332	
333	// Create a debounced wrapper around the forage storage so frequent writes
334	// (e.g., during continuous drawing) are coalesced. Exposes the same
335	// StateStorage async API expected by zustand's persistence layer.
336	const createDebouncedForageStorage = (delay = DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS): StateStorage => {
337	  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return forageStorage;
338	
339	  let timeout: number | undefined;
340	  const pending = new Map<string, string>();
341	  let flushing = false;
342	
343	  const flush = async () => {
344	    if (flushing) return;
345	    flushing = true;
346	    for (const [k, v] of pending) {
347	      try {
348	        await storage.setItem(k, v);
349	      } catch (e) {
350	        // ignore individual write errors
351	        console.warn('debounced storage setItem failed', e);
352	      }
353	    }
354	    pending.clear();
355	    if (typeof timeout !== 'undefined') {
356	      clearTimeout(timeout);
357	      timeout = undefined;
358	    }
359	    flushing = false;
360	  };
361	
362	  try {
363	    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
364	      // flush synchronously where possible
365	      if (pending.size) {
366	        // best-effort flush (no await in beforeunload)
367	        void flush();
368	      }
369	    });
370	  } catch (e) {
371	    // ignore
372	  }
373	
374	  return {
375	    getItem: async (name: string) => {
376	      // If we have a pending value for this key, return it first
377	      if (pending.has(name)) return pending.get(name) as string;
378	      return (await storage.getItem(name)) as string | null;
379	    },
380	    setItem: async (name: string, value: string) => {
381	      pending.set(name, value);
382	      // read current configured delay from localStorage if available
383	      let configured = delay;
384	      try {
385	        const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(AUTOSAVE_DELAY_STORAGE_KEY);
386	        const parsed = raw ? Number(raw) : NaN;
387	        if (!Number.isNaN(parsed) && parsed > 0) configured = parsed;
388	      } catch (e) {
389	        // ignore
390	      }
391	      if (typeof timeout !== 'undefined') clearTimeout(timeout);
392	      timeout = window.setTimeout(() => void flush(), configured) as unknown as number;
393	    },
394	    removeItem: async (name: string) => {
395	      pending.delete(name);
396	      try {
397	        await storage.removeItem(name);
398	      } catch (e) {
399	        console.warn('debounced storage removeItem failed', e);
400	      }
401	    },
402	  };
403	};
404	
405	export const useProjectStore = create<ProjectState>()(
406	  persist(
407	    (set, get) => {
408	      const updateActiveProject = (updater: (project: Project) => Partial<Project>) => {
409	        const state = get();
410	        if (!state.activeProjectId) return;
411	        const project = state.projects[state.activeProjectId];
412	        if (!project) return;
413	        const nextProject = {
414	          ...project,
415	          ...updater(project),
416	          lastModified: Date.now()
417	        };
418	        set({
419	          projects: {
420	            ...state.projects,
421	            [state.activeProjectId]: nextProject
422	          },
423	          ...projectView(nextProject)
424	        });
425	      };
426	
427	      return {
428	        projects: {},
429	        deletedProjects: {},
430	        activeProjectId: null,
431	        ...emptyProjectView(),
432	        clipboard: null,
433	        validationResults: [],
434	
435	        createProject: (name, rows = 20, cols = 20) => {
436	          const newProject = createProjectRecord(name, rows, cols);
437	          set((state) => ({
438	            projects: { ...state.projects, [newProject.id]: newProject },
439	            activeProjectId: newProject.id,
440	            ...projectView(newProject)
441	          }));
442	          return newProject.id;
443	        },
444	
445	        switchProject: (id) => {
446	          const project = get().projects[id];
447	          if (!project) return;
448	          set({ activeProjectId: id, ...projectView(project), validationResults: [] });
449	        },
450	
451	        deleteProject: (id) => {
452	          set((state) => {
453	            const nextProjects = { ...state.projects };
454	            const projectToDelete = nextProjects[id];
455	            if (!projectToDelete) return state;
456	
457	            delete nextProjects[id];
458	            const nextDeletedProjects = {
459	              ...state.deletedProjects,
460	              [id]: { ...projectToDelete, deletedAt: Date.now() },
461	            };
462	
463	            const fallback = Object.values(nextProjects).sort((a, b) => b.lastModified - a.lastModified)[0];
464	            return {
465	              projects: nextProjects,
466	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
467	              activeProjectId: state.activeProjectId === id ? fallback?.id ?? null : state.activeProjectId,
468	              ...(state.activeProjectId === id ? (fallback ? projectView(fallback) : emptyProjectView()) : {})
469	            };
470	          });
471	        },
472	
473	        restoreProject: (id) => {
474	          set((state) => {
475	            const deleted = state.deletedProjects[id];
476	            if (!deleted) return state;
477	
478	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
479	            delete nextDeletedProjects[id];
480	
481	            const restoredProject = {
482	              ...deleted,
483	              deletedAt: undefined,
484	              lastModified: Date.now(),
485	            };
486	
487	            return {
488	              projects: { ...state.projects, [id]: restoredProject },
489	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
490	            };
491	          });
492	        },
493	
494	        deleteProjectPermanently: (id) => {
495	          set((state) => {
496	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
497	            delete nextDeletedProjects[id];
498	            return { deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects };
499	          });
500	        },
501	
502	        emptyRecycleBin: () => {
503	          set({ deletedProjects: {} });
504	        },
505	
506	        purgeExpiredProjects: () => {
507	          set((state) => {
508	            const nextProjects = { ...state.projects };
509	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
510	            let changed = false;
511	
512	            Object.entries(state.projects).forEach(([id, project]) => {
513	              if (state.activeProjectId === id) return;
514	              if (Date.now() - project.lastModified > EXPIRY_SOFT_DELETE_MS) {
515	                nextDeletedProjects[id] = { ...project, deletedAt: Date.now() };
516	                delete nextProjects[id];
517	                changed = true;
518	              }
519	            });
520	
521	            if (!changed) return state;
522	
523	            const fallback = Object.values(nextProjects).sort((a, b) => b.lastModified - a.lastModified)[0];
524	            const nextActiveId = state.activeProjectId && nextProjects[state.activeProjectId] ? state.activeProjectId : fallback?.id ?? null;
525	
526	            return {
527	              projects: nextProjects,
528	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
529	              activeProjectId: nextActiveId,
530	              ...(nextActiveId ? projectView(nextProjects[nextActiveId]) : emptyProjectView()),
531	            };
532	          });
533	        },
534	
535	        renameProject: (id, name) => {
536	          const nextName = name.trim();
537	          if (!nextName) return;
538	          set((state) => {
539	            const project = state.projects[id];
540	            if (!project) return state;
541	            const nextProject = { ...project, name: nextName, lastModified: Date.now() };
542	            return {
543	              projects: {
544	                ...state.projects,
545	                [id]: nextProject,
546	              },
547	              ...(state.activeProjectId === id ? projectView(nextProject) : {}),
548	            };
549	          });
550	        },
551	
552	        duplicateProject: (id) => {
553	          const project = get().projects[id];
554	          if (!project) return null;
555	          const nextProject = cloneProject(project, `${project.name} Copy`);
556	          set((state) => ({
557	            projects: { ...state.projects, [nextProject.id]: nextProject },
558	            activeProjectId: nextProject.id,
559	            ...projectView(nextProject),
560	          }));
561	          return nextProject.id;
562	        },
563	
564	        updateProjectThumbnail: (id, thumbnail) => {
565	          set((state) => {
566	            const project = state.projects[id];
567	            if (!project) return state;
568	            return {
569	              projects: {
570	                ...state.projects,
571	                [id]: { ...project, thumbnail, lastModified: Date.now() }
572	              }
573	            };
574	          });
575	        },
576	
577	        replaceModeGrid: (mode, grid, resetHistory = true) => {
578	          const { activeProjectId } = get();
579	          if (!activeProjectId) {
580	            get().createProject('Untitled Project', grid.length, grid[0]?.length ?? 0);
581	          }
582	
583	          updateActiveProject((project) => ({
584	            grids: { ...project.grids, [mode]: cloneGrid(grid) },
585	            currentMode: mode,
586	            ...(resetHistory ? { undoStack: [], redoStack: [] } : {}),
587	          }));
588	        },
589	
590	        setMode: (mode) => {
591	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ currentMode: mode }));
592	        },
593	
594	        setTextLocale: (locale) => {
595	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ textLocale: locale }));
596	          get().compileToText();
597	        },
598	
599	        setRowNumberDirection: (direction) => {
600	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ rowNumberDirection: direction }));
601	          get().compileToText();
602	        },
603	
604	        initGrid: (rows, cols) => {
605	          if (!get().activeProjectId) {
606	            get().createProject('Untitled Project', rows, cols);
607	            return;
608	          }
609	
610	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ 
611	            grids: { 
612	              knit: createEmptyGrid(rows, cols), 
613	              crochet: createEmptyGrid(rows, cols) 
614	            },
615	            description: '',
616	            undoStack: [], 
617	            redoStack: [] 
618	          }));
619	        },
620	
621	        applyCellChange: (row, col, char, svgPath, stitchId) => {
622	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
623	          if (!activeProjectId) return false;
624	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
625	
626	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
627	          if (!currentGrid[row] || !currentGrid[row][col]) return false;
628	        
629	          const isErasing = !stitchId;
630	          const stitchDef = stitchId ? stitchRegistry[stitchId] : null;
631	        
632	          const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
633	          const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
634	
635	          let needsUpdate = false;
636	          const newGrid = currentGrid.map(r => [...r]);
637	
638	          const clearStitchAt = (r: number, c: number) => {
639	            const cell = newGrid[r]?.[c];
640	            if (!cell) return;
641	            if (cell.isSpanChild && cell.parentPos) {
642	              clearStitchAt(cell.parentPos.row, cell.parentPos.col);
643	              return;
644	            }
645	          
646	            const sDef = cell.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId] : null;
647	            const cSpanW = sDef?.span?.width || 1;
648	            const cSpanH = sDef?.span?.height || 1;
649	          
650	            for (let i = 0; i < cSpanH; i++) {
651	              for (let j = 0; j < cSpanW; j++) {
652	                if (newGrid[r + i] && newGrid[r + i][c + j]) {
653	                  newGrid[r + i][c + j] = { ...newGrid[r + i][c + j], char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: '', isSpanChild: false, parentPos: undefined };
654	                  needsUpdate = true;
655	                }
656	              }
657	            }
658	          };
659	
660	          if (isErasing) {
661	            if (newGrid[row][col].stitchId || newGrid[row][col].isSpanChild) {
662	              clearStitchAt(row, col);
663	            }
664	          } else {
665	            if (row + spanH > currentGrid.length || col + spanW > currentGrid[0].length) {
666	              return false; 
667	            }
668	
669	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
670	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
671	                 const tarR = row + i;
672	                 const tarC = col + j;
673	                 if (newGrid[tarR]?.[tarC] && (newGrid[tarR][tarC].stitchId || newGrid[tarR][tarC].isSpanChild)) {
674	                   clearStitchAt(tarR, tarC);
675	                 }
676	              }
677	            }
678	
679	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
680	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
681	                const tarR = row + i;
682	                const tarC = col + j;
683	                if (newGrid[tarR] && newGrid[tarR][tarC]) {
684	                  if (i === 0 && j === 0) {
685	                    newGrid[tarR][tarC] = { ...newGrid[tarR][tarC], char, svgPath, stitchId, isSpanChild: false, parentPos: undefined };
686	                  } else {
687	                    newGrid[tarR][tarC] = { ...newGrid[tarR][tarC], char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: stitchId, isSpanChild: true, parentPos: { row, col } };
688	                  }
689	                  needsUpdate = true;
690	                }
691	              }
692	            }
693	          }
694	
695	          if (needsUpdate) {
696	            get()._saveSnapshot();
697	            updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid } }));
698	            get().compileToText();
699	            return true;
700	          }
701	
702	          return false;
703	        },
704	
705	        copySelection: (roots, anchor) => {
706	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
707	          if (!activeProjectId || !anchor || roots.length === 0) return false;
708	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
709	
710	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
711	          const seen = new Set<string>();
712	          const items: ClipboardItem[] = [];
713	
714	          for (const root of roots) {
715	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
716	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
717	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
718	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
719	            seen.add(key);
720	
721	            const cell = currentGrid[resolvedRoot.row]?.[resolvedRoot.col];
722	            if (!cell?.stitchId || cell.isSpanChild) continue;
723	
724	            items.push({
725	              dr: resolvedRoot.row - anchor.row,
726	              dc: resolvedRoot.col - anchor.col,
727	              cellSnapshot: { ...cell, parentPos: undefined, isSpanChild: false },
728	            });
729	          }
730	
731	          if (!items.length) return false;
732	          set({ clipboard: { anchor, items } });
733	          return true;
734	        },
735	
736	        cutSelection: (roots, anchor) => {
737	          if (!get().copySelection(roots, anchor)) return false;
738	
739	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
740	          if (!activeProjectId) return false;
741	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
742	
743	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
744	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
745	          let changed = false;
746	
747	          const seen = new Set<string>();
748	          for (const root of roots) {
749	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
750	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
751	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
752	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
753	            seen.add(key);
754	            changed = clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col) || changed;
755	          }
756	
757	          if (!changed) return false;
758	          get()._saveSnapshot();
759	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
760	          get().compileToText();
761	          return true;
762	        },
763	
764	        pasteClipboard: (target) => {
765	          const { activeProjectId, projects, clipboard } = get();
766	          if (!activeProjectId || !clipboard?.items.length) return null;
767	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
768	
769	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
770	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
771	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
772	          const placements = clipboard.items.map((item) => ({
773	            row: target.row + item.dr,
774	            col: target.col + item.dc,
775	            item,
776	          }));
777	
778	          const isOutOfBounds = placements.some(({ row, col, item }) => {
779	            const stitchDef = item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
780	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
781	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
782	            return row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > rows || col + spanW > cols;
783	          });
784	
785	          if (isOutOfBounds) return null;
786	
787	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
788	          for (const placement of placements) {
789	            placeStitchSnapshot(nextGrid, placement.row, placement.col, placement.item.cellSnapshot);
790	          }
791	
792	          get()._saveSnapshot();
793	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
794	          get().compileToText();
795	          return placements.map(({ row, col }) => ({ row, col }));
796	        },
797	
798	        exportSnapshot: () => {
799	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
800	          if (!activeProjectId) return { pages: [] };
801	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
802	
803	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
804	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
805	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
806	
807	          const pageWidth = 595.28;
808	          const pageHeight = 841.89;
809	          const cellSize = 16;
810	          const gridWidth = cols * cellSize;
811	          const gridHeight = rows * cellSize;
812	          const pageScale = Math.min(pageWidth / Math.max(gridWidth, 1), pageHeight / Math.max(gridHeight, 1), 1);
813	
814	          const glyphs = [] as Array<{
815	            id: string;
816	            svgPath: string;
817	            transform: { tx: number; ty: number; scale: number };
818	            bounds: { w: number; h: number };
819	          }>;
820	
821	          for (let row = 0; row < rows; row += 1) {
822	            for (let col = 0; col < cols; col += 1) {
823	              const cell = currentGrid[row]?.[col];
824	              if (!cell?.stitchId || cell.isSpanChild) continue;
825	              const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
826	              if (!stitchDef) continue;
827	
828	              const spanW = stitchDef.span.width || 1;
829	              const spanH = stitchDef.span.height || 1;
830	              glyphs.push({
831	                id: `${row}-${col}-${cell.stitchId}`,
832	                svgPath: stitchDef.svgPath,
833	                transform: {
834	                  tx: col * cellSize * pageScale,
835	                  ty: row * cellSize * pageScale,
836	                  scale: pageScale,
837	                },
838	                bounds: {
839	                  w: spanW * cellSize * pageScale,
840	                  h: spanH * cellSize * pageScale,
841	                },
842	              });
843	            }
844	          }
845	
846	          return {
847	            pages: [
848	              {
849	                width: pageWidth,
850	                height: pageHeight,
851	                glyphs,
852	              },
853	            ],
854	          } as ExportSnapshot;
855	        },
856	
857	        moveSelection: (roots, anchor, target) => {
858	          if (!get().copySelection(roots, anchor)) return null;
859	
860	          const { activeProjectId, projects, clipboard } = get();
861	          if (!activeProjectId || !clipboard?.items.length) return null;
862	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
863	
864	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
865	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
866	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
867	          const placements = clipboard.items.map((item) => ({
868	            row: target.row + item.dr,
869	            col: target.col + item.dc,
870	            item,
871	          }));
872	
873	          const isOutOfBounds = placements.some(({ row, col, item }) => {
874	            const stitchDef = item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
875	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
876	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
877	            return row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > rows || col + spanW > cols;
878	          });
879	
880	          if (isOutOfBounds) return null;
881	
882	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
883	
884	          for (const placement of placements) {
885	            const stitchDef = placement.item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[placement.item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
886	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
887	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
888	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
889	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
890	                clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, placement.row + i, placement.col + j);
891	              }
892	            }
893	          }
894	
895	          const seen = new Set<string>();
896	          for (const root of roots) {
897	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
898	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
899	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
900	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
901	            seen.add(key);
902	            clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
903	          }
904	
905	          for (const placement of placements) {
906	            placeStitchSnapshot(nextGrid, placement.row, placement.col, placement.item.cellSnapshot);
907	          }
908	
909	          get()._saveSnapshot();
910	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
911	          get().compileToText();
912	          return placements.map(({ row, col }) => ({ row, col }));
913	        },
914	
915	        compileToText: () => {
916	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
917	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
918	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
919	
920	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
921	          const text = compileGridToText(currentGrid, { locale: project.textLocale, rowNumberDirection: project.rowNumberDirection });
922	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ description: text }));
923	        },
924	
925	        applyTextToGrid: (text: string) => {
926	          const { activeProjectId, projects, _saveSnapshot } = get();
927	          if (!activeProjectId) return [];
928	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
929	
930	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
931	          const rowsInGrid = currentGrid.length;
932	          const colsInGrid = currentGrid.length > 0 ? currentGrid[0].length : 0;
933	
934	          const parsedRows = parseTextToGrid(text, colsInGrid);
935	
936	          set({ validationResults: parsedRows });
937	
938	          const hasInvalidRows = parsedRows.some((r: any) => !r.validation.valid);
939	
940	          if (hasInvalidRows) {
941	            if (text.trim() === '') {
942	              updateActiveProject(() => ({ description: '' }));
943	            } else {
944	              get().compileToText(); 
945	            }
946	            return parsedRows; 
947	          }
948	
949	          _saveSnapshot(); 
950	
951	          let maxColsFromText = colsInGrid;
952	          parsedRows.forEach((pRow: any) => {
953	            if (pRow.validation.delta > 0) {
954	              maxColsFromText = Math.max(maxColsFromText, colsInGrid + pRow.validation.delta);
955	            }
956	          });
957	
958	          let newGrid = createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText);
959	    
960	          if (rowsInGrid === 0 || text.trim() === '') {
961	            newGrid = createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText); 
962	            updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid }, description: '' }));
963	            return parsedRows;
964	          }
965	
966	          parsedRows.forEach((parsed: any) => {
967	            const gridRowIndex = gridRowFromDisplayRow(parsed.rowNumber, rowsInGrid, project.rowNumberDirection);
968	            if (gridRowIndex >= 0 && gridRowIndex < rowsInGrid) {
969	              const isEvenRow = parsed.rowNumber % 2 === 0;
970	              let currentCol = isEvenRow ? 0 : maxColsFromText - 1;
971	
972	              for (const cell of parsed.cells) {
973	                const stitchId = cell.stitchId!;
974	                const spanW = stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.span?.width || 1;
975	                const dir = isEvenRow ? 1 : -1;
976	
977	                const endCol = currentCol + dir * (spanW - 1);
978	                if (dir === 1 && endCol >= maxColsFromText) continue; 
979	                if (dir === -1 && endCol < 0) continue; 
980	
981	                if (currentCol >= 0 && currentCol < maxColsFromText) {
982	                  newGrid[gridRowIndex][currentCol] = {
983	                    ...cell,
984	                    svgPath: stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.svgPath || '',
985	                    isSpanChild: false,
986	                    parentPos: undefined,
987	                  };
988	                }
989	
990	                for (let k = 1; k < spanW; k++) {
991	                  const childCol = currentCol + dir * k;
992	                  if (childCol >= 0 && childCol < maxColsFromText) {
993	                    newGrid[gridRowIndex][childCol] = {
994	                      char: '',
995	                      svgPath: '',
996	                      stitchId,
997	                      isSpanChild: true,
998	                      parentPos: { row: gridRowIndex, col: currentCol },
999	                    };
1000	                  }
1001	                }
1002	                currentCol = currentCol + dir * spanW;
1003	              }
1004	            }
1005	          });
1006	
1007	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid }, description: text }));
1008	          return parsedRows;
1009	        },
1010	
1011	        resizeGrid: (newCols: number) => {
1012	          const { activeProjectId, projects, _saveSnapshot } = get();
1013	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1014	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1015	
1016	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
1017	          const currentRows = currentGrid.length;
1018	          const currentCols = currentGrid.length > 0 ? currentGrid[0].length : 0;
1019	
1020	          if (newCols === currentCols) return; 
1021	
1022	          _saveSnapshot(); 
1023	
1024	          const newGrid = createEmptyGrid(currentRows, newCols);
1025	
1026	          for (let r = 0; r < currentRows; r++) {
1027	            for (let c = 0; c < Math.min(currentCols, newCols); c++) {
1028	              newGrid[r][c] = currentGrid[r][c];
1029	            }
1030	          }
1031	
1032	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid } }));
1033	          get().compileToText(); 
1034	        },
1035	
1036	        undo: () => {
1037	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1038	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1039	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1040	
1041	          if (project.undoStack.length === 0) return;
1042	        
1043	          const previous = project.undoStack[project.undoStack.length - 1];
1044	          const newUndoStack = project.undoStack.slice(0, -1);
1045	        
1046	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1047	            grids: previous.grids,
1048	            currentMode: previous.currentMode,
1049	            description: previous.description || '',
1050	            undoStack: newUndoStack,
1051	            redoStack: [...project.redoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1052	          }));
1053	        },
1054	
1055	        redo: () => {
1056	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1057	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1058	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1059	
1060	          if (project.redoStack.length === 0) return;
1061	        
1062	          const next = project.redoStack[project.redoStack.length - 1];
1063	          const newRedoStack = project.redoStack.slice(0, -1);
1064	        
1065	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1066	            grids: next.grids,
1067	            currentMode: next.currentMode,
1068	            description: next.description || '',
1069	            undoStack: [...project.undoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1070	            redoStack: newRedoStack,
1071	          }));
1072	        },
1073	
1074	        _saveSnapshot: () => {
1075	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1076	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1077	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1078	
1079	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1080	            undoStack: [...project.undoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1081	            redoStack: []
1082	          }));
1083	        }
1084	      };
1085	    },
1086	    {
1087	      name: 'kintting-design-project',
1088	      storage: createJSONStorage(() => createDebouncedForageStorage(DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS), {
1089	        replacer: storageReplacer,
1090	        reviver: storageReviver,
1091	      }),
1092	      version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
1093	      partialize: (state) => ({
1094	        projects: state.projects,
1095	        deletedProjects: state.deletedProjects,
1096	        activeProjectId: state.activeProjectId,
1097	      }),
1098	      merge: (persistedState: any, currentState) => {
1099	        const merged = { ...currentState, ...(persistedState ?? {}) };
1100	        const activeProject = merged.activeProjectId ? merged.projects?.[merged.activeProjectId] : null;
1101	        return {
1102	          ...merged,
1103	          deletedProjects: merged.deletedProjects ?? {},
1104	          ...(activeProject ? projectView(activeProject) : emptyProjectView()),
1105	          clipboard: null,
1106	          validationResults: [],
1107	        };
1108	      },
1109	      migrate: (persistedState: any, version: number) => {
1110	        if (!persistedState || Object.keys(persistedState).length === 0) {
1111	          return {
1112	            projects: {},
1113	            deletedProjects: {},
1114	            activeProjectId: null,
1115	            clipboard: null,
1116	            validationResults: [],
1117	          };
1118	        }
1119	
1120	        if (version === 0 || typeof persistedState.version !== 'number') {
1121	          if (persistedState.projects && typeof persistedState.projects === 'object') {
1122	            const migratedProjects = Object.fromEntries(
1123	              Object.entries(persistedState.projects).map(([id, project]) => [id, normalizeProject(project)])
1124	            );
1125	
1126	            return {
1127	              projects: migratedProjects,
1128	              deletedProjects: {},
1129	              activeProjectId: persistedState.activeProjectId in migratedProjects ? persistedState.activeProjectId : Object.keys(migratedProjects)[0] ?? null,
1130	              clipboard: null,
1131	              validationResults: [],
1132	            };
1133	          }
1134	
1135	          const id = crypto.randomUUID();
1136	          const grids = persistedState.grids || { knit: [], crochet: [] };
1137	          const currentMode = persistedState.currentMode === 'crochet' ? 'crochet' : 'knit';
1138	
1139	          return {
1140	            projects: {
1141	              [id]: {
1142	                id,
1143	                name: 'Migrated Project',
1144	                lastModified: Date.now(),
1145	                deletedAt: undefined,
1146	                thumbnail: undefined,
1147	                version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
1148	                grids,
1149	                currentMode,
1150	                description: '',
1151	                textLocale: 'abbr' as TextLocale,
1152	                rowNumberDirection: 'row1_top' as RowNumberDirection,
1153	                undoStack: [],
1154	                redoStack: [],
1155	              }
1156	            },
1157	            deletedProjects: {},
1158	            activeProjectId: id,
1159	            clipboard: null,
1160	            validationResults: [],
1161	          };
1162	        }
1163	
1164	        if (version < CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION) {
1165	          if (persistedState.projects && typeof persistedState.projects === 'object') {
1166	            const upgradedProjects = Object.fromEntries(
1167	              Object.entries(persistedState.projects).map(([id, project]) => [id, normalizeProject(project)])
1168	            );
1169	
1170	            return {
1171	              projects: upgradedProjects,
1172	              deletedProjects: {},
1173	              activeProjectId: persistedState.activeProjectId in upgradedProjects ? persistedState.activeProjectId : Object.keys(upgradedProjects)[0] ?? null,
1174	              clipboard: null,
1175	              validationResults: [],
1176	            };
1177	          }
1178	        }
1179	
1180	        return persistedState;
1181	      },
1182	    }
1183	  )
1184	);
1185	
```

2	import { useCanvasStore } from '../../store/canvasStore';
3	import { useProjectStore } from '../../store/projectStore';
4	import { compileGridToText, type TextLocale } from '../../utils/translator';
5	import { gridRowFromDisplayRow } from '../../utils/rowNumbering';
6	import './text-editor.css';
7	
8	const LOCALES: Array<{ id: TextLocale; label: string }> = [
9	  { id: 'abbr', label: 'Abbr' },
10	  { id: 'en', label: 'EN' },
11	  { id: 'zh', label: '中文' },
12	];
13	
14	export const TextEditor: React.FC = () => {
15	  const {
16	    grids,
17	    currentMode,
18	    textLocale,
19	    setTextLocale,
20	    rowNumberDirection,
21	    setRowNumberDirection,
22	  } = useProjectStore();
23	  const setHighlightedRow = useCanvasStore((state) => state.setHighlightedRow);
24	
25	  const currentGrid = grids[currentMode];
26	  const rowsInGrid = currentGrid.length;
27	
28	  const instructionLines = useMemo(() => {
29	    const text = compileGridToText(currentGrid, { locale: textLocale, rowNumberDirection });
30	    return text
31	      .split('\n')
32	      .map((line) => line.trim())
33	      .filter(Boolean)
34	      .map((line) => {
35	        const rowNumber = Number(line.match(/^Row\s+(\d+):/i)?.[1] ?? 0);
36	        return { line, rowNumber };
37	      });
38	  }, [currentGrid, rowNumberDirection, textLocale]);
39	
40	  const handleRowClick = (rowNumber: number) => {
41	    const gridRow = gridRowFromDisplayRow(rowNumber, rowsInGrid, rowNumberDirection);
42	    if (gridRow >= 0 && gridRow < rowsInGrid) {
43	      setHighlightedRow(gridRow);
44	    }
45	  };
46	
47	  return (
48	    <div className="text-editor-container instruction-map-panel">
49	      <div className="text-editor-header">
50	        <div>
51	          <span className="text-editor-kicker">Instruction Map</span>
52	          <h3>指令映射</h3>
53	        </div>
54	      </div>
55	
56	      <div className="text-editor-toolbar" role="group" aria-label="行号方向">
57	        <button
58	          type="button"
59	          className={rowNumberDirection === 'row1_top' ? 'locale-chip is-active' : 'locale-chip'}
60	          onClick={() => setRowNumberDirection('row1_top')}
61	        >
62	          Row 1 顶部
63	        </button>
64	        <button
65	          type="button"
66	          className={rowNumberDirection === 'row1_bottom' ? 'locale-chip is-active' : 'locale-chip'}
67	          onClick={() => setRowNumberDirection('row1_bottom')}
68	        >
69	          Row 1 底部
70	        </button>
71	      </div>
72	
73	      <div className="text-editor-toolbar" role="group" aria-label="文本输出语言">
74	        {LOCALES.map((locale) => (
75	          <button
76	            key={locale.id}
77	            type="button"
78	            className={textLocale === locale.id ? 'locale-chip is-active' : 'locale-chip'}
79	            onClick={() => setTextLocale(locale.id)}
80	          >
81	            {locale.label}
82	          </button>
83	        ))}
84	      </div>
85	
86	      <div className="instruction-map-list" aria-label="只读指令映射">
87	        {instructionLines.length ? (
88	          instructionLines.map(({ line, rowNumber }) => (
89	            <button
90	              key={`${rowNumber}-${line}`}
91	              type="button"
92	              className="instruction-map-row"
93	              onClick={() => handleRowClick(rowNumber)}
94	            >
95	              {line}
96	            </button>
97	          ))
98	        ) : (
99	          <p className="instruction-map-empty">画布中暂无可映射的针法。</p>
100	        )}
101	      </div>
102	    </div>
103	  );
104	};
105	
```
