```json
149	  const scale = useCanvasStore((state) => state.scale);
150	  const selectedCell = useCanvasStore((state) => state.selectedCell);
151	  const setInteractionMode = useCanvasStore((state) => state.setInteractionMode);
152	  const setScale = useCanvasStore((state) => state.setScale);
153	  const clearSelection = useCanvasStore((state) => state.clearSelection);
154	
155	  useEffect(() => {
156	    if (!grids.knit.length || !grids.crochet.length) {
157	      initGrid(DEFAULT_GRID_ROWS, DEFAULT_GRID_COLS);
158	    }
159	  }, [grids.crochet.length, grids.knit.length, initGrid]);
160	
161	  useEffect(() => {
162	    if (activePage === 'workspace') {
163	      purgeExpiredProjects();
164	    }
165	  }, [activePage, purgeExpiredProjects]);
166	
167	  useEffect(() => {
168	    const fontSet = (document as unknown as { fonts?: FontFaceSet }).fonts;
169	    if (!fontSet) {
170	      setFontsReady(true);
171	      return;
172	    }
173	
174	    const uniqueFamilies = Array.from(
175	      new Set(Object.values(stitchRegistry).map((definition) => definition.svgPath.split('/')[2] ?? 'StitchMasteryDash'))
176	    );
177	
178	    Promise.all(uniqueFamilies.map((name) => fontSet.load(`16px "${name}"`)))
179	      .then(() => setFontsReady(true))
180	      .catch(() => setFontsReady(true));
181	  }, []);
182	
183	  const availableSymbols = useMemo<StitchDefinition[]>(
184	    () => Object.values(stitchRegistry).filter((definition) => definition.category === currentMode),
185	    [currentMode]
186	  );
187	
188	  const activeSymbol = useMemo(
189	    () => availableSymbols.find((definition) => definition.id === activeSymbolId) ?? null,
190	    [activeSymbolId, availableSymbols]
191	  );
192	
193	  useEffect(() => {
194	    if (!availableSymbols.length) {
195	      setActiveSymbolId(null);
196	      return;
197	    }
198	
199	    if (!activeSymbolId || !availableSymbols.some((definition) => definition.id === activeSymbolId)) {
200	      setActiveSymbolId(availableSymbols[0].id);
201	    }
202	  }, [activeSymbolId, availableSymbols]);
203	
204	  const currentGrid = grids[currentMode];
205	  const gridRows = currentGrid.length;
206	  const gridCols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
207	
208	  const filledCellCount = useMemo(
209	    () => currentGrid.flat().filter((cell) => cell.stitchId && !cell.isSpanChild).length,
210	    [currentGrid]
211	  );
212	
213	  const selectedPosition = selectedCell ? `${displayRowNumber(selectedCell.root.row, gridRows, rowNumberDirection)}, ${selectedCell.root.col + 1}` : '未选择';
214	  const projectCompletion = gridRows && gridCols ? Math.round((filledCellCount / (gridRows * gridCols)) * 100) : 0;
215	
216	  const selectedInfo = useMemo(() => {
217	    if (!selectedCell) {
218	      return null;
219	    }
220	
221	    const cell = currentGrid[selectedCell.root.row]?.[selectedCell.root.col];
222	    if (!cell?.stitchId) {
223	      return {
224	        title: '空单元格',
225	        detail: '可直接点击针法后进入绘制',
226	      };
227	    }
228	
229	    const definition = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
230	    return {
231	      title: definition?.nameZh ?? cell.stitchId,
232	      detail: definition?.nameEn ?? '已放置到主画布。',
233	    };
234	  }, [currentGrid, selectedCell]);
235	
236	  const filteredLibraryCards = useMemo(
237	    () =>
238	      LIBRARY_SHOWCASE.filter((card) => {
239	        if (!libraryQuery.trim()) {
240	          return true;
241	        }
242	
243	        return `${card.title}${card.subtitle}`.includes(libraryQuery.trim());
244	      }),
245	    [libraryQuery]
246	  );
247	
248	  const handleProjectModeChange = (mode: ProjectMode) => {
249	    setMode(mode);
250	    clearSelection();
251	    setNotice(mode === 'knit' ? '已切换到棒针编辑空间。' : '已切换到钩针编辑空间。');
252	    if (mode === 'knit' && activePage === 'crochet') {
253	      setActivePage('workspace');
254	    }
255	    if (mode === 'crochet' && activePage === 'workspace') {
256	      setActivePage('crochet');
257	    }
258	  };
259	
260	
261	
262	  const handlePageChange = (page: ExperiencePage, mode?: ProjectMode) => {
263	    setActivePage(page);
264	    clearSelection();
265	    if (mode) {
266	      setMode(mode);
267	    }
268	
269	    const pageLabel = PAGE_ITEMS.find((item) => item.id === page)?.label ?? '当前页面';
270	    setNotice(`已进入 ${pageLabel}。`);
271	  };
272	
273	  const getProjectAgeLabel = (project: { lastModified: number }) => {
274	    const ms = Date.now() - project.lastModified;
275	    const days = Math.floor(ms / 86400000);
276	    return days <= 1 ? '1天内' : `${days}天前`;
277	  };
278	
279	  const isProjectWarning = (project: { id?: string; lastModified: number }, activeId: string | null) => {
280	    if (project.id && project.id === activeId) return false;
281	    const ms = Date.now() - project.lastModified;
282	    return ms >= 7 * 86400000 && ms < 10 * 86400000;
283	  };
284	
285	  const expiringProjectsCount = useMemo(() => {
286	    return projectList.filter((p) => isProjectWarning(p, activeProjectId)).length;
287	  }, [projectList, activeProjectId]);
288	
289	
290	  const handleSymbolPick = (symbolId: string, symbolMode: ProjectMode = currentMode) => {
291	    if (symbolMode !== currentMode) {
292	      setMode(symbolMode);
293	    }
294	    setActiveSymbolId(symbolId);
295	    setInteractionMode('DRAW');
296	    setNotice(`已选择 ${stitchRegistry[symbolId]?.nameZh ?? symbolId}，可直接在画布中落针。`);
297	  };
298	
299	  const updateScale = (value: number) => {
300	    setScale(Number(clampScale(value).toFixed(2)));
301	  };
302	
303	  const handleGaugeFieldChange = (key: keyof typeof gaugeForm, value: string) => {
304	    setGaugeForm((prev) => ({
305	      ...prev,
306	      [key]: value.replace(/\D/g, ''),
307	    }));
308	  };
309	
310	  const parseGaugeValue = (value: string) => {
311	    const parsed = Number(value);
312	    return Number.isNaN(parsed) ? 0 : parsed;
313	  };
314	
315	  const gaugeTotals = useMemo(
316	    () => ({
317	      stitches: Math.max(0, Math.round((parseGaugeValue(gaugeForm.stitchesPerTenCm) / 10) * parseGaugeValue(gaugeForm.targetWidthCm))),
318	      rows: Math.max(0, Math.round((parseGaugeValue(gaugeForm.rowsPerTenCm) / 10) * parseGaugeValue(gaugeForm.targetHeightCm))),
319	    }),
320	    [gaugeForm]
321	  );
322	
323	  const applyGaugeToProject = () => {
324	    const nextCols = Math.max(12, gaugeTotals.stitches);
325	    const nextRows = Math.max(12, gaugeTotals.rows);
326	    initGrid(nextRows, nextCols);
327	    clearSelection();
328	    setCalculatorOpen(false);
329	    setNotice(`针数换算已应用，项目尺寸更新为 ${nextCols} 列 x ${nextRows} 行。`);
330	  };
331	
332	  const handleCreateProject = () => {
333	    const name = window.prompt('项目名称', `Project ${projectList.length + 1}`);
334	    if (!name?.trim()) {
335	      return;
336	    }
337	
338	    createProject(name.trim(), DEFAULT_GRID_ROWS, DEFAULT_GRID_COLS);
339	    clearSelection();
340	    setScale(1);
341	    setIsProjectPanelOpen(false);
342	    setNotice(`已创建项目：${name.trim()}`);
343	  };
344	
345	  const handleRenameProject = () => {
346	    if (!activeProject) {
347	      return;
348	    }
349	
350	    const name = window.prompt('重命名项目', activeProject.name);
351	    if (!name?.trim()) {
352	      return;
353	    }
354	
355	    renameProject(activeProject.id, name.trim());
356	    setNotice(`项目已重命名为：${name.trim()}`);
357	  };
358	
359	  const handleDuplicateProject = () => {
360	    if (!activeProjectId) {
361	      return;
362	    }
363	
364	    const nextId = duplicateProject(activeProjectId);
365	    if (nextId) {
366	      clearSelection();
367	      setIsProjectPanelOpen(false);
368	      setNotice('项目副本已创建。');
369	    }
370	  };
371	
372	  const handleDeleteProject = (id: string) => {
373	    const project = projects[id];
374	    if (!project || !window.confirm(`删除项目“${project.name}”？`)) {
375	      return;
376	    }
377	
378	    deleteProject(id);
379	    clearSelection();
380	    setNotice(`已删除项目：${project.name}`);
381	  };
382	
383	  const handleSwitchProject = (id: string) => {
384	    switchProject(id);
385	    clearSelection();
386	    setIsProjectPanelOpen(false);
387	    setNotice(`已打开项目：${projects[id]?.name ?? id}`);
388	  };
389	
390	  const applyAiPresetToProject = () => {
391	    const knitPreset = createPresetGrid('knit', 32, 32);
392	    replaceModeGrid('knit', knitPreset);
393	    clearSelection();
394	    setScale(1);
395	    setInteractionMode('DRAW');
396	    setActiveSymbolId('c4f');
397	    setActivePage('workspace');
398	    setNotice('AI 纹样映射已应用到棒针工作区，可继续精修。');
399	  };
400	
401	  const confirmExport = async () => {
402	    if (isExporting) {
403	      return;
404	    }
405	
406	    const presetLabel =
407	      exportPreset === 'professional' ? '商用专业版' : exportPreset === 'draft' ? '交流草稿版' : '社交分享版';
408	    setNotice(`${presetLabel} 导出任务正在进行中，水印内容为“${watermarkText || '未设置'}”。`);
409	    setIsExporting(true);
410	
411	    try {
412	      const snapshot = exportSnapshot();
413	      const pdfBlob = await exportProjectAsPDF(snapshot, {
414	        watermarkText,
415	        scale: 1,
416	      });
417	      const url = URL.createObjectURL(pdfBlob);
418	      const anchor = document.createElement('a');
419	      anchor.href = url;
420	      anchor.download = 'mykintting-design.pdf';
421	      document.body.appendChild(anchor);
422	      anchor.click();
423	      document.body.removeChild(anchor);
424	      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
425	      setNotice(`导出完成：已生成 PDF 并自动下载，水印“${watermarkText || '未设置'}”。`);
426	    } catch (error: any) {
427	      setNotice(`导出失败：${error?.message ?? '未知错误'}`);
428	    } finally {
429	      setIsExporting(false);
430	    }
431	  };
432	
433	  const renderSymbolRail = (symbols: StitchDefinition[]) => (
434	    <div className="studio-list">
435	      {symbols.slice(0, 6).map((symbol) => (
436	        <button
437	          key={symbol.id}
438	          type="button"
439	          className={`symbol-button studio-list-item${activeSymbolId === symbol.id ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
440	          onClick={() => handleSymbolPick(symbol.id)}
441	        >
442	          <span className="studio-list-thumb">
443	            <img src={symbol.svgPath} alt={symbol.nameZh} />
444	          </span>
445	          <span className="studio-list-copy">
446	            <strong>{symbol.nameZh}</strong>
447	            <small>{symbol.nameEn ?? (currentMode === 'knit' ? 'Knitting' : 'Crochet')}</small>
448	          </span>
449	        </button>
450	      ))}
451	    </div>
452	  );
453	
454	  const renderWorkspacePage = () => (
455	    <div className="page-stack">
456	      {expiringProjectsCount > 0 && (
457	        <div className="expiration-banner">
458	          <div className="expiration-banner-content">
459	            <span className="expiration-icon">⚠️</span>
460	            <div className="expiration-text">
461	              <strong>注意：{expiringProjectsCount} 个项目即将回收</strong>
462	              <p>最近 7 天未使用的项目将在 10 天后自动移入回收站。请及时查看项目管理面板。</p>
463	            </div>
464	            <button 
465	              type="button" 
466	              className="expiration-action-btn"
467	              onClick={() => setIsProjectPanelOpen(true)}
468	            >
469	              查看项目
470	            </button>
471	          </div>
472	        </div>
473	      )}
474	      <section className="page-hero">
475	        <div>
476	          <div className="text-base font-bold">复杂提花：北极星图案</div>
477	        </div>
478	        <div className="hero-actions">
479	          <span className="hero-pill">Delta: +2</span>
480	          <span className="hero-pill muted">{Math.round(scale * 100)}%</span>
481	        </div>
482	      </section>
483	
484	      <section className="workspace-layout">
485	        <div className="canvas-column">
486	          <div className="canvas-ruler">
487	            {[0, 8, 16, 24, 32].map((value) => (
488	              <span key={value}>{value}</span>
489	            ))}
490	          </div>
491	          <div className="canvas-stage-card">
492	            <div className="canvas-main-row">
493	              <div className="main-content atelier-grid-shell" style={{ position: 'relative' }}>
494	                <Grid activeSymbolId={activeSymbolId} />
495	              </div>
496	            </div>
497	            <div className="floating-tool-rail">
498	              <button type="button" onClick={() => updateScale(scale + 0.1)}>
499	                +
500	              </button>
501	              <button type="button" onClick={() => updateScale(scale - 0.1)}>
502	                -
503	              </button>
504	              <button type="button" onClick={() => setInteractionMode('SELECT')}>
505	                光标
506	              </button>
507	              <button type="button" onClick={() => setCalculatorOpen(true)}>
508	                换算
509	              </button>
510	            </div>
511	          </div>
512	        </div>
513	
514	        <aside className="workspace-side">
515	          <div className="studio-card compact flush-top">
516	            <div className="studio-card-header">
517	              <div>
518	                <span className="card-kicker">工作台侧栏</span>
519	                <h3>右侧映射面板</h3>
520	              </div>
521	              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
522	                <button
523	                  type="button"
524	                  className="ghost-button"
525	                  onClick={() => {
526	                    const input = window.prompt('设置自动保存间隔（秒）。输入正数，例如 10 表示 10 秒。', String(Math.round(autosaveMs / 1000)));
527	                    if (!input) return;
528	                    const sec = Number(input);
529	                    if (Number.isNaN(sec) || sec <= 0) {
530	                      setNotice('请输入大于 0 的数字。');
531	                      return;
532	                    }
533	                    const ms = Math.round(sec * 1000);
534	                    try {
535	                      window.localStorage.setItem('kintting:autosaveDelayMs', String(ms));
536	                      setAutosaveMs(ms);
537	                      setNotice(`自动保存间隔已设置为 ${sec} 秒。`);
538	                    } catch (e) {
539	                      setNotice('无法保存设置（localStorage 失败）。');
540	                    }
541	                  }}
542	                  title="设置自动保存间隔"
543	                >
544	                  自动保存: {Math.round(autosaveMs / 1000)}s
545	                </button>
546	              </div>
547	            </div>
548	          </div>
549	
550	          <>
551	            {/* Existing right sidebar content */}
552	            <div className="studio-card compact">
553	              <div className="studio-card-header">
554	                <div>
555	                  <span className="card-kicker">当前笔刷</span>
556	                  <h3>{activeSymbol?.nameZh ?? '未选择针法'}</h3>
557	                </div>
558	                <span className="hero-pill muted">{currentMode === 'knit' ? '棒针' : '钩针'}</span>
559	              </div>
560	              <p className="muted-copy">{selectedInfo?.detail ?? '选择任意单元格后，这里会展示当前针法详情。'}</p>
561	              <div className="tool-grid">
562	                {TOOLBAR_TOOLS.map((tool) => (
563	                  <button
564	                    key={tool.id}
565	                    type="button"
566	                    className={`tool-chip${interactionMode === tool.id ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
567	                    data-testid={`tool-${tool.id.toLowerCase()}`}
568	                    onClick={() => setInteractionMode(tool.id)}
569	                  >
570	                    <strong>{tool.short}</strong>
571	                    <span>{tool.label}</span>
572	                  </button>
573	                ))}
574	              </div>
575	              {renderSymbolRail(availableSymbols)}
576	              <div className="studio-range-row">
577	                <label htmlFor="canvas-scale">缩放</label>
578	                <input
579	                  id="canvas-scale"
580	                  type="range"
581	                  min={CANVAS_SCALE_MIN}
582	                  max={CANVAS_SCALE_MAX}
583	                  step={0.05}
584	                  value={scale}
585	                  onChange={(event) => updateScale(Number(event.target.value))}
586	                  aria-label="画布缩放"
587	                />
588	              </div>
589	              <div className="studio-button-row">
590	                <button type="button" className="ghost-button icon-only-button" onClick={undo} disabled={!undoStack.length} aria-label="Undo" title="Undo">
591	                  ↩
592	                </button>
593	                <button type="button" className="ghost-button icon-only-button" onClick={redo} disabled={!redoStack.length} aria-label="Redo" title="Redo">
594	                  ↪
595	                </button>
596	              </div>
597	
598	              <div className="studio-meta-grid">
599	                <span>选择</span>
600	                <strong>{selectedPosition}</strong>
601	                <span>状态</span>
602	                <strong>{previousMode ? `临时 ${interactionMode}` : interactionMode}</strong>
603	              </div>
604	            </div>
605	
606	            <div className="studio-card compact">
607	              <TextEditor />
608	            </div>
609	
610	
611	            <div className="tracker-card">
612	              <span className="card-kicker">进度追踪</span>
613	              <div className="tracker-ring">
614	                <strong>{projectCompletion}%</strong>
615	                <span>已完成</span>
616	              </div>
617	              <div className="tracker-stat">
618	                <strong>
619	                  第 {Math.max(1, Math.ceil(filledCellCount / Math.max(gridCols, 1)))} 行 / 共 {gridRows} 行
620	                </strong>
621	                <span>
622	                  填充 {filledCellCount}/{gridRows * gridCols}
623	                </span>
624	              </div>
625	            </div>
626	          </>
627	        </aside>
628	      </section>
629	    </div>
630	  );
631	
632	  const renderLibraryPage = () => (
633	    <div className="page-stack">
634	      <section className="page-hero">
635	        <div>
636	          <div className="page-eyebrow">针法库 | 搜索与筛选</div>
637	          <h1>针法库搜索与筛选状态</h1>
638	          <p>在您的工作室中寻找最合适的纹理，并将结果直接应用到当前项目。</p>
639	        </div>
640	      </section>
641	
642	      <section className="library-toolbar">
643	        <label className="library-search">
644	          <span>当前搜索</span>
645	          <input value={libraryQuery} onChange={(event) => setLibraryQuery(event.target.value)} placeholder="搜索基础、麻花、钩针…" />
646	        </label>
647	        <button type="button" className="filter-button">
648	          筛选条件 (3)
649	        </button>
650	      </section>
651	
652	      <section className="library-grid">
653	        {filteredLibraryCards.map((card, index) => (
654	          <article
655	            key={card.id}
656	            className={`library-card tone-${card.tone}${index === 0 ? ' is-featured' : ''}`}
657	            onClick={() => handleSymbolPick(card.id, 'knit')}
658	          >
659	            <div className="library-card-media" />
660	            <div className="library-card-copy">
661	              <h3>{card.title}</h3>
662	              <p>{card.subtitle}</p>
663	            </div>
664	            <div className="library-card-actions">
665	              <button type="button" className="icon-button subtle">
666	                收藏
667	              </button>
668	              <button
669	                type="button"
670	                className="icon-button"
671	                onClick={(event) => {
672	                  event.stopPropagation();
673	                  handleSymbolPick(card.id, 'knit');
674	                  handlePageChange('workspace', 'knit');
675	                }}
676	              >
677	                应用
678	              </button>
679	            </div>
680	          </article>
681	        ))}
682	
683	        <article className="library-insight-card">
684	          <span className="card-kicker">库数据分布</span>
685	          <h3>基础分类包含约 24 种常用针法</h3>
686	          <div className="insight-stats">
687	            <div>
688	              <strong>85%</strong>
689	              <span>热度</span>
690	            </div>
691	            <div>
692	              <strong>12</strong>
693	              <span>已收藏</span>
694	            </div>
695	          </div>
696	        </article>
697	      </section>
698	    </div>
699	  );
700	
701	  const renderAiPage = () => (
702	    <div className="page-stack">
703	      <section className="page-hero">
704	        <div>
705	          <div className="page-eyebrow">AI 工坊 | 纹样解析</div>
706	          <h1>AI 图像转换（中文）</h1>
707	          <p>利用纹理网络将视觉灵感转为技术模式，我们的工坊正在分析您的纹理。</p>
708	        </div>
709	      </section>
710	
711	      <section className="ai-layout">
712	        <article className="studio-card ai-parameters">
713	          <div className="studio-card-header">
714	            <div>
715	              <span className="card-kicker">可调参数</span>
716	              <h3>精细优化</h3>
717	            </div>
718	          </div>
719	          <div className="parameter-block">
720	            <span>针脚密度</span>
721	            <strong>24 / 1</strong>
722	          </div>
723	          <div className="parameter-block">
724	            <span>针脚锐度</span>
725	            <strong>12</strong>
726	          </div>
727	          <button type="button" className="primary-button" onClick={applyAiPresetToProject}>
728	            精细优化
729	          </button>
730	          <button type="button" className="ghost-button" onClick={() => setNotice('AI 参数已重置为推荐档位。')}>
731	            重置
732	          </button>
733	          <div className="ai-apply-box">

1280	                </button>
1281	                <button
1282	                  type="button"
1283	                  className="ghost-button"
1284	                  onClick={() =>
1285	                    setGaugeForm({
1286	                      stitchesPerTenCm: '22',
1287	                      rowsPerTenCm: '36',
1288	                      targetWidthCm: '50',
1289	                      targetHeightCm: '50',
1290	                    })
1291	                  }
1292	                >
1293	                  重置
1294	                </button>
1295	              </div>
1296	            </div>
1297	
1298	            <div className="calculator-summary-panel">
1299	              <button type="button" className="dialog-close" onClick={() => setCalculatorOpen(false)}>
1300	                x
1301	              </button>
1302	              <div className="summary-metric">
1303	                <span>计算总计</span>
1304	                <strong>{gaugeTotals.stitches}</strong>
1305	                <small>针</small>
1306	              </div>
1307	              <div className="summary-divider" />
1308	              <div className="summary-metric">
1309	                <span>总行数</span>
1310	                <strong>{gaugeTotals.rows}</strong>
1311	                <small>行</small>
1312	              </div>
1313	            </div>
1314	          </div>
1315	        </div>
1316	      ) : null}
1317	    </div>
1318	  );
1319	}
1320	
1321	export default App;
1322
```

> Read: `D:\aaa-llx\MyKinttingDesign\MyKinttingDesignApp\src\store\canvasStore.ts`

**Output:**

```json
1	import { create } from 'zustand';
2	
3	export type InteractionMode = 'SELECT' | 'DRAW' | 'ERASE' | 'PAN';
4	
5	export interface ViewportSize {
6	  width: number;
7	  height: number;
8	}
9	
10	export interface GridCellPosition {
11	  row: number;
12	  col: number;
13	}
14	
15	export interface SelectedCellState {
16	  anchor: GridCellPosition;
17	  root: GridCellPosition;
18	}
19	
20	interface CanvasState {
21	  viewportOffset: { x: number; y: number };
22	  viewportSize: ViewportSize;
23	  scale: number;
24	  interactionMode: InteractionMode;
25	  previousMode: InteractionMode | null;
26	  selectedCell: SelectedCellState | null;
27	  hoverRoot: GridCellPosition | null;
28	  highlightedRow: number | null;
29	  
30	  setViewportOffset: (offset: { x: number; y: number }) => void;
31	  setViewportSize: (size: ViewportSize) => void;
32	  setScale: (scale: number) => void;
33	  setInteractionMode: (mode: InteractionMode) => void;
34	  selectCell: (selection: SelectedCellState) => void;
35	  clearSelection: () => void;
36	  setHoverRoot: (root: GridCellPosition | null) => void;
37	  setHighlightedRow: (row: number | null) => void;
38	  tempSwitchToPan: () => void;
39	  restorePreviousMode: () => void;
40	}
41	
42	export const useCanvasStore = create<CanvasState>((set) => ({
43	  viewportOffset: { x: 0, y: 0 },
44	  viewportSize: { width: 0, height: 0 },
45	  scale: 1,
46	  interactionMode: 'SELECT',
47	  previousMode: null,
48	  selectedCell: null,
49	  hoverRoot: null,
50	  highlightedRow: null,
51	  
52	  setViewportOffset: (offset) => set({ viewportOffset: offset }),
53	  setViewportSize: (size) => set({ viewportSize: size }),
54	  setScale: (scale) => set({ scale }),
55	  setInteractionMode: (mode) => set({ interactionMode: mode, previousMode: null }),
56	  selectCell: (selection) => set({ selectedCell: selection }),
57	  clearSelection: () => set({ selectedCell: null }),
58	  setHoverRoot: (root) => set({ hoverRoot: root }),
59	  setHighlightedRow: (row) => set({ highlightedRow: row }),
60	  tempSwitchToPan: () => set((state) => {
61	    if (state.interactionMode === 'PAN') {
62	      return state;
63	    }
64	
65	    return { previousMode: state.interactionMode, interactionMode: 'PAN' };
66	  }),
67	  restorePreviousMode: () => set((state) => {
68	    if (!state.previousMode) {
69	      return state;
70	    }
71	
72	    return {
73	      interactionMode: state.previousMode,
74	      previousMode: null,
75	    };
76	  }),
77	}));
78	
```

```json
1	import './testSetup';
2	import { describe, expect, it } from 'vitest';
3	import { compileGridToText, parseTextToGrid } from '../utils/translator';
4	
5	const buildGrid = () => [
6	  [
7	    { stitchId: 'k-knit' },
8	    { stitchId: 'p-purl' },
9	    { stitchId: 'c2f' },
10	    { stitchId: 'c2f', isSpanChild: true, parentPos: { row: 0, col: 2 } },
11	  ],
12	  [
13	    { stitchId: 'p-purl' },
14	    { stitchId: 'k-knit' },
15	    { stitchId: 'yo' },
16	    { stitchId: 'k-knit' },
17	  ],
18	];
19	
20	describe('translator', () => {
21	  it('compiles grid to abbreviated text by default', () => {
22	    const text = compileGridToText(buildGrid() as never);
23	
24	    expect(text).toContain('Row 1:');
25	    expect(text).toContain('k');
26	    expect(text).toContain('c2f');
27	  });
28	
29	  it('can compile with Row 1 at the bottom', () => {
30	    const text = compileGridToText(buildGrid() as never, { rowNumberDirection: 'row1_bottom' });
31	
32	    expect(text.split('\n')[0]).toContain('Row 1:');
33	    expect(text).toContain('c2b');
34	  });
35	
36	  it('compiles grid to english names when locale is en', () => {
37	    const text = compileGridToText(buildGrid() as never, { locale: 'en' });
38	
39	    expect(text).toContain('Row 1:');
40	    expect(text).toMatch(/knit|purl|Cable 2 Front/);
41	  });
42	
43	  it('compiles grid to chinese names when locale is zh', () => {
44	    const text = compileGridToText(buildGrid() as never, { locale: 'zh' });
45	
46	    expect(text).toContain('Row 1:');
47	    expect(text).toMatch(/下针|上针|2针前交叉/);
48	  });
49	
50	  it('parses chinese names back into grid cells', () => {
51	    const parsed = parseTextToGrid('Row 1: 2 下针, 1 上针, 1 左上两针并一针.', 6);
52	
53	    expect(parsed).toHaveLength(1);
54	    expect(parsed[0].rowNumber).toBe(1);
55	    expect(parsed[0].cells.map((cell) => cell.stitchId)).toEqual([
56	      'k-knit',
57	      'k-knit',
58	      'p-purl',
59	      'k2tog',
60	    ]);
61	    expect(parsed[0].validation.valid).toBe(true);
62	  });
63	
64	  it('flags rows that exceed the available width', () => {
65	    const parsed = parseTextToGrid('Row 1: 8 下针.', 6);
66	
67	    expect(parsed[0].validation.valid).toBe(false);
68	    expect(parsed[0].validation.delta).toBeGreaterThan(0);
69	  });
70	});
71
```

#### Tool: Read

> Read: `D:\aaa-llx\MyKinttingDesign\MyKinttingDesignApp\src\components\Grid\Grid.tsx`

**Output:**

```json
1	import { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';
2	import { Group, Image, Layer, Line, Rect, Stage, Text } from 'react-konva';
3	import useImage from 'use-image';
4	import { stitchRegistry } from '../../configs/stitchRegistry';
5	import { useCanvasStore } from '../../store/canvasStore';
6	import { useProjectStore } from '../../store/projectStore';
7	import {
8	  calculateZoomOffset,
9	  clamp,
10	  resolveGridCell,
11	  screenToGrid,
12	  toSelectedCellState,
13	} from '../../utils/coordinateTransform';
14	import { displayRowNumber } from '../../utils/rowNumbering';
15	import { CANVAS_CELL_SIZE, CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE, clampCanvasScale } from '../../constants/canvas';
16	import './grid.css';
17	
18	const StitchImage = ({ svgPath, width, height }: { svgPath: string; width: number; height: number }) => {
19	  const [image] = useImage(svgPath);
20	  if (!image) {
21	    return null;
22	  }
23	
24	  return <Image image={image} x={0} y={0} width={width} height={height} />;
25	};
26	
27	const GridKonva = ({ activeSymbolId }: { activeSymbolId: string | null }) => {
28	  const { grids, currentMode, applyCellChange, rowNumberDirection } = useProjectStore();
29	  const grid = grids[currentMode];
30	  const {
31	    viewportOffset,
32	    setViewportOffset,
33	    setViewportSize,
34	    scale,
35	    setScale,
36	    interactionMode,
37	    selectedCell,
38	    hoverRoot,
39	    highlightedRow,
40	    selectCell,
41	    clearSelection,
42	    setHoverRoot,
43	  } = useCanvasStore();
44	
45	  const stageRef = useRef<any>(null);
46	  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
47	  const lastDrawPlacementRef = useRef<{
48	    row: number;
49	    col: number;
50	    stitchId: string;
51	    spanWidth: number;
52	    spanHeight: number;
53	  } | null>(null);
54	  const [size, setSize] = useState({ width: 800, height: 600 });
55	  const [isPanning, setIsPanning] = useState(false);
56	  const [isDrawing, setIsDrawing] = useState(false);
57	
58	  const gridRows = grid.length;
59	  const gridCols = grid[0]?.length ?? 0;
60	
61	  const clampViewportOffset = (nextOffset: { x: number; y: number }) => {
62	    const contentWidth = size.width - CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE;
63	    const contentHeight = size.height - CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE;
64	
65	    const minContentX = contentWidth - gridCols * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * scale;
66	    const minContentY = contentHeight - gridRows * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * scale;
67	
68	    return {
69	      x: clamp(nextOffset.x, Math.min(0, minContentX), 0),
70	      y: clamp(nextOffset.y, Math.min(0, minContentY), 0),
71	    };
72	  };
73	
74	  const getPointerPosition = (event?: any) => {
75	    const eventStage = event?.target?.getStage?.();
76	    return eventStage?.getPointerPosition?.() ?? stageRef.current?.getPointerPosition?.() ?? null;
77	  };
78	
79	  useEffect(() => {
80	    const handleResize = () => {
81	      if (!containerRef.current) {
82	        return;
83	      }
84	
85	      const nextSize = {
86	        width: containerRef.current.clientWidth,
87	        height: containerRef.current.clientHeight,
88	      };
89	
90	      setSize(nextSize);
91	      setViewportSize(nextSize);
92	    };
93	
94	    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
95	    window.setTimeout(handleResize, 50);
96	
97	    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
98	  }, [setViewportSize]);
99	
100	  useEffect(() => {
101	    setViewportOffset(clampViewportOffset(viewportOffset));
102	  }, [gridCols, gridRows, scale, size.height, size.width]);
103	
104	  const handleWheel = (event: any) => {
105	    event.evt.preventDefault();
106	    const pointer = getPointerPosition(event);
107	    const scaleBy = 1.1;
108	
109	    if (event.evt.ctrlKey) {
110	      if (!pointer) {
111	        return;
112	      }
113	
114	      const oldScale = scale;
115	      const newScale = clampCanvasScale(event.evt.deltaY < 0 ? oldScale * scaleBy : oldScale / scaleBy);
116	      const nextOffset = calculateZoomOffset(viewportOffset, oldScale, newScale, pointer);
117	
118	      setScale(newScale);
119	      setViewportOffset(clampViewportOffset(nextOffset));
120	      return;
121	    }
122	
123	    setViewportOffset(
124	      clampViewportOffset({
125	        x: viewportOffset.x - event.evt.deltaX,
126	        y: viewportOffset.y - event.evt.deltaY,
127	      })
128	    );
129	  };
130	
131	  const resolvePointer = (pointer: { x: number; y: number }) => {
132	    const logical = screenToGrid(pointer, viewportOffset, scale, CANVAS_CELL_SIZE);
133	    return resolveGridCell(grid, logical.row, logical.col);
134	  };
135	
136	  const drawAtPointer = (pointer: { x: number; y: number }) => {
137	    const logical = screenToGrid(pointer, viewportOffset, scale, CANVAS_CELL_SIZE);
138	    let row = logical.row;
139	    let col = logical.col;
140	
141	    if (interactionMode === 'DRAW' && activeSymbolId) {
142	      const symbol = stitchRegistry[activeSymbolId];
143	      if (!symbol) {
144	        return;
145	      }
146	
147	      const lastPlacement = lastDrawPlacementRef.current;
148	      if (
149	        lastPlacement &&
150	        lastPlacement.stitchId === symbol.id &&
151	        logical.row >= lastPlacement.row &&
152	        logical.row < lastPlacement.row + lastPlacement.spanHeight &&
153	        logical.col >= lastPlacement.col &&
154	        logical.col < lastPlacement.col + lastPlacement.spanWidth
155	      ) {
156	        return;
157	      }
158	
159	      if (applyCellChange(row, col, symbol.nameZh, symbol.svgPath, symbol.id)) {
160	        lastDrawPlacementRef.current = {
161	          row,
162	          col,
163	          stitchId: symbol.id,
164	          spanWidth: symbol.span.width,
165	          spanHeight: symbol.span.height,
166	        };
167	        selectCell({
168	          anchor: logical,
169	          root: { row, col },
170	        });
171	      }
172	
173	      return;
174	    }
175	
176	    if (interactionMode === 'ERASE' && applyCellChange(logical.row, logical.col, '', undefined, undefined)) {
177	      clearSelection();
178	    }
179	  };
180	
181	  const handlePointerDown = (event: any) => {
182	    const pointer = getPointerPosition(event);
183	    if (!pointer) return;
184	
185	    const isRightClick = event.evt.button === 2;
186	    const resolved = resolvePointer(pointer);
187	
188	    setHoverRoot(resolved?.root ?? null);
189	
190	    if (interactionMode === 'PAN' || event.evt.button === 1 || isRightClick) {
191	      setIsPanning(true);
192	      return;
193	    }
194	
195	    if (interactionMode === 'SELECT') {
196	      if (!resolved || !resolved.cell?.stitchId) {
197	        clearSelection();
198	        return;
199	      }
200	
201	      selectCell(toSelectedCellState(resolved));
202	      return;
203	    }
204	
205	    if (interactionMode === 'DRAW' || interactionMode === 'ERASE') {
206	      setIsDrawing(true);
207	      drawAtPointer(pointer);
208	    }
209	  };
210	
211	  const handlePointerMove = (event: any) => {
212	    if (isPanning) {
213	      setViewportOffset(
214	        clampViewportOffset({
215	          x: viewportOffset.x + event.evt.movementX,
216	          y: viewportOffset.y + event.evt.movementY,
217	        })
218	      );
219	      return;
220	    }
221	
222	    const hoverPointer = getPointerPosition(event);
223	    if (hoverPointer) {
224	      const hoverResolved = resolvePointer(hoverPointer);
225	      setHoverRoot(hoverResolved?.root ?? null);
226	    }
227	
228	    if (!isDrawing) {
229	      return;
230	    }
231	
232	    const pointer = getPointerPosition(event);
233	    if (!pointer) {
234	      return;
235	    }
236	
237	    drawAtPointer(pointer);
238	  };
239	
240	  const handlePointerUp = () => {
241	    setIsPanning(false);
242	    setIsDrawing(false);
243	    lastDrawPlacementRef.current = null;
244	  };
245	
246	  const selectedHighlights = useMemo(() => {
247	    if (!selectedCell) {
248	      return [];
249	    }
250	
251	    const resolved = resolveGridCell(grid, selectedCell.root.row, selectedCell.root.col);
252	    if (!resolved?.cell) {
253	      return [];
254	    }
255	
256	    const stitchDef = resolved.cell.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[resolved.cell.stitchId] : null;
257	    const spanWidth = stitchDef?.span.width ?? 1;
258	    const spanHeight = stitchDef?.span.height ?? 1;
259	
260	    return [
261	      {
262	        key: `selected-${resolved.root.row}-${resolved.root.col}`,
263	        x: resolved.root.col * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
264	        y: resolved.root.row * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
265	        width: CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * spanWidth,
266	        height: CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * spanHeight,
267	      },
268	    ];
269	  }, [grid, selectedCell]);
270	
271	  const visibleCells = useMemo(() => {
272	    if (!grid.length || !grid[0]?.length) {
273	      return { cells: [] as Array<{ row: number; col: number; cell: (typeof grid)[number][number] }>, gridLines: [] as Array<{ points: number[]; key: string }> };
274	    }
275	
276	    const scaledCellSize = CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * scale;
277	    const startCol = Math.max(0, Math.floor(-viewportOffset.x / scaledCellSize));
278	    const endCol = Math.min(grid[0].length - 1, Math.ceil((size.width - viewportOffset.x) / scaledCellSize));
279	    const startRow = Math.max(0, Math.floor(-viewportOffset.y / scaledCellSize));
280	    const endRow = Math.min(grid.length - 1, Math.ceil((size.height - viewportOffset.y) / scaledCellSize));
281	
282	    const cells = [];
283	    for (let row = startRow; row <= endRow; row += 1) {
284	      for (let col = startCol; col <= endCol; col += 1) {
285	        cells.push({ row, col, cell: grid[row][col] ?? { bg: 'white' } });
286	      }
287	    }
288	
289	    const gridLines = [];
290	    const maxGridCol = grid[0].length;
291	    const maxGridRow = grid.length;
292	
293	    for (let col = startCol; col <= endCol + 1; col += 1) {
294	      if (col > maxGridCol) {
295	        break;
296	      }
297	
298	      gridLines.push({
299	        points: [
300	          col * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
301	          startRow * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
302	          col * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
303	          Math.min(endRow + 1, maxGridRow) * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
304	        ],
305	        key: `v-${col}`,
306	      });
307	    }
308	
309	    for (let row = startRow; row <= endRow + 1; row += 1) {
310	      if (row > maxGridRow) {
311	        break;
312	      }
313	
314	      gridLines.push({
315	        points: [
316	          startCol * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
317	          row * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
318	          Math.min(endCol + 1, maxGridCol) * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
319	          row * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE,
320	        ],
321	        key: `h-${row}`,
322	      });
323	    }
324	
325	    return { cells, gridLines };
326	  }, [grid, scale, size.height, size.width, viewportOffset.x, viewportOffset.y]);
327	
328	  const gridCursor = interactionMode === 'PAN' || isPanning ? 'grab' : interactionMode === 'SELECT' ? 'pointer' : 'crosshair';
329	
330	  return (
331	    <div ref={containerRef} className="grid-container konva-wrapper" data-testid="grid-root" style={{ width: '100%', height: '100%', outline: 'none' }}>
332	      <Stage
333	        ref={stageRef}
334	        width={size.width}
335	        height={size.height}
336	        onWheel={handleWheel}
337	        onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
338	        onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
339	        onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
340	        onMouseLeave={handlePointerUp}
341	        onContextMenu={(event: any) => event.evt.preventDefault()}
342	        style={{ cursor: gridCursor }}
343	      >
344	        <Layer x={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE + viewportOffset.x} y={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE + viewportOffset.y} scaleX={scale} scaleY={scale}>
345	          {visibleCells.cells.map(({ row, col, cell }) => (
346	            <Rect
347	              key={`bg-${row}-${col}`}
348	              x={col * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE}
349	              y={row * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE}
350	              width={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE}
351	              height={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE}
352	              fill={cell.bg || 'white'}
353	              listening={false}
354	            />
355	          ))}
356	
357	          {visibleCells.gridLines.map((line) => (
358	            <Line key={line.key} points={line.points} stroke="#e2e8f0" strokeWidth={1 / scale} listening={false} />
359	          ))}
360	
361	          {visibleCells.cells.map(({ row, col, cell }) => {
362	            if (cell.isSpanChild || !cell.svgPath) {
363	              return null;
364	            }
365	
366	            const stitchDef = cell.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId] : null;
367	            const spanWidth = stitchDef?.span.width ?? 1;
368	            const spanHeight = stitchDef?.span.height ?? 1;
369	
370	            return (
371	              <Group key={`stitch-${row}-${col}`} x={col * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE} y={row * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE}>
372	                <StitchImage svgPath={cell.svgPath} width={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * spanWidth} height={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * spanHeight} />
373	              </Group>
374	            );
375	          })}
376	
377	          {highlightedRow !== null ? (
378	            <Rect
379	              x={0}
380	              y={highlightedRow * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE}
381	              width={gridCols * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE}
382	              height={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE}
383	              fill="rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.14)"
384	              stroke="#f59e0b"
385	              strokeWidth={2 / scale}
386	              listening={false}
387	            />
388	          ) : null}
389	
390	          {selectedHighlights.map((highlight) => (
391	            <Rect
392	              key={`selected-${highlight.key}`}
393	              x={highlight.x}
394	              y={highlight.y}
395	              width={highlight.width}
396	              height={highlight.height}
397	              stroke="#0ea5e9"
398	              strokeWidth={2 / scale}
399	              dash={[6 / scale, 4 / scale]}
400	              fill="rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.12)"
401	              listening={false}
402	            />
403	          ))}
404	
405	          {hoverRoot && (
406	            <Rect
407	              x={hoverRoot.col * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE + 1.5}
408	              y={hoverRoot.row * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE + 1.5}
409	              width={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE - 3}
410	              height={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE - 3}
411	              fill={
412	                interactionMode === 'ERASE'
413	                  ? 'rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.2)'
414	                  : interactionMode === 'SELECT'
415	                  ? 'rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.15)'
416	                  : 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.15)'
417	              }
418	              stroke={
419	                interactionMode === 'ERASE'
420	                  ? '#ef4444'
421	                  : interactionMode === 'SELECT'
422	                  ? '#0ea5e9'
423	                  : '#10b981'
424	              }
425	              strokeWidth={1.5 / scale}
426	              listening={false}
427	            />
428	          )}
429	        </Layer>
430	
431	        <Layer>
432	          <Rect x={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} y={0} width={size.width} height={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} fill="#f8fafc" stroke="#e2e8f0" strokeWidth={1} />
433	          <Rect x={0} y={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} width={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} height={size.height} fill="#f8fafc" stroke="#e2e8f0" strokeWidth={1} />
434	          <Rect x={0} y={0} width={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} height={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} fill="#f1f5f9" stroke="#cbd5e1" strokeWidth={1} />
435	
436	          <Group clipX={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} clipY={0} clipWidth={size.width - CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} clipHeight={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE}>
437	            <Group y={0}>
438	              {Array.from(new Set(visibleCells.cells.map((cell) => cell.col))).map((col) => (
439	                <Text
440	                  key={`col-${col}`}
441	                  text={`${col + 1}`}
442	                  x={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE + col * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * scale + viewportOffset.x}
443	                  y={0}
444	                  width={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * scale}
445	                  height={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE}
446	                  align="center"
447	                  verticalAlign="middle"
448	                  fill="#64748b"
449	                  fontSize={12}
450	                />
451	              ))}
452	            </Group>
453	          </Group>
454	
455	          <Group clipX={0} clipY={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} clipWidth={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE} clipHeight={size.height - CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE}>
456	            <Group x={0}>
457	              {Array.from(new Set(visibleCells.cells.map((cell) => cell.row))).map((row) => (
458	                <Text
459	                  key={`row-${row}`}
460	                  text={`${displayRowNumber(row, gridRows, rowNumberDirection)}`}
461	                  x={0}
462	                  y={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE + row * CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * scale + viewportOffset.y}
463	                  width={CANVAS_HEADER_SIZE}
464	                  height={CANVAS_CELL_SIZE * scale}
465	                  align="center"
466	                  verticalAlign="middle"
467	                  fill="#64748b"
468	                  fontSize={12}
469	                />
470	              ))}
471	            </Group>
472	          </Group>
473	        </Layer>
474	      </Stage>
475	    </div>
476	  );
477	};
478	
479	export default GridKonva;
480	
```

#### Tool: Read

> Read: `D:\aaa-llx\MyKinttingDesign\MyKinttingDesignApp\src\configs\stitchRegistry.ts`

```json
1	import type { GridCellPosition, SelectedCellState, ViewportSize } from '../store/canvasStore';
2	import type { CellData } from '../store/projectStore';
3	
4	export interface Point {
5	  x: number;
6	  y: number;
7	}
8	
9	export interface ResolvedGridCell {
10	  anchor: GridCellPosition;
11	  root: GridCellPosition;
12	  cell: CellData | null;
13	}
14	
15	export interface NavigatorMetrics {
16	  miniCellSize: number;
17	  originX: number;
18	  originY: number;
19	  gridWidth: number;
20	  gridHeight: number;
21	}
22	
23	export const clamp = (value: number, min: number, max: number) => Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max);
24	
25	export function screenToGrid(
26	  screenPoint: Point,
27	  viewportOffset: Point,
28	  scale: number,
29	  cellSize: number
30	): { row: number; col: number } {
31	  const gridX = (screenPoint.x - viewportOffset.x) / scale;
32	  const gridY = (screenPoint.y - viewportOffset.y) / scale;
33	
34	  return {
35	    col: Math.floor(gridX / cellSize),
36	    row: Math.floor(gridY / cellSize),
37	  };
38	}
39	
40	export function gridToScreen(
41	  row: number,
42	  col: number,
43	  viewportOffset: Point,
44	  scale: number,
45	  cellSize: number
46	): Point {
47	  return {
48	    x: col * cellSize * scale + viewportOffset.x,
49	    y: row * cellSize * scale + viewportOffset.y,
50	  };
51	}
52	
53	export function calculateZoomOffset(
54	  currentOffset: Point,
55	  currentScale: number,
56	  newScale: number,
57	  mousePoint: Point
58	): Point {
59	  const logicalX = (mousePoint.x - currentOffset.x) / currentScale;
60	  const logicalY = (mousePoint.y - currentOffset.y) / currentScale;
61	
62	  return {
63	    x: mousePoint.x - logicalX * newScale,
64	    y: mousePoint.y - logicalY * newScale,
65	  };
66	}
67	
68	export function resolveGridCell(
69	  grid: CellData[][],
70	  row: number,
71	  col: number
72	): ResolvedGridCell | null {
73	  if (!grid[row] || !grid[row][col]) {
74	    return null;
75	  }
76	
77	  const anchor = { row, col };
78	  const cell = grid[row][col];
79	
80	  if (cell.isSpanChild && cell.parentPos) {
81	    const root = cell.parentPos;
82	    return {
83	      anchor,
84	      root,
85	      cell: grid[root.row]?.[root.col] ?? null,
86	    };
87	  }
88	
89	  return {
90	    anchor,
91	    root: anchor,
92	    cell,
93	  };
94	}
95	
96	export function toSelectedCellState(resolved: ResolvedGridCell): SelectedCellState {
97	  return {
98	    anchor: resolved.anchor,
99	    root: resolved.root,
100	  };
101	}
102	
103	export function getNavigatorMetrics(
104	  rows: number,
105	  cols: number,
106	  _viewportSize: ViewportSize,
107	  _scale: number,
108	  navigatorSize: number,
109	  _cellSize: number,
110	  padding: number
111	): NavigatorMetrics {
112	  const safeRows = Math.max(rows, 1);
113	  const safeCols = Math.max(cols, 1);
114	  const contentSize = Math.max(1, navigatorSize - padding * 2);
115	  const miniCellSize = Math.min(contentSize / safeCols, contentSize / safeRows);
116	  const gridWidth = cols * miniCellSize;
117	  const gridHeight = rows * miniCellSize;
118	
119	  return {
120	    miniCellSize,
121	    gridWidth,
122	    gridHeight,
123	    originX: (navigatorSize - gridWidth) / 2,
124	    originY: (navigatorSize - gridHeight) / 2,
125	  };
126	}
127	
128	export function getNavigatorViewportRect(
129	  rows: number,
130	  cols: number,
131	  viewportOffset: Point,
132	  viewportSize: ViewportSize,
133	  scale: number,
134	  cellSize: number,
135	  metrics: NavigatorMetrics
136	) {
137	  if (rows <= 0 || cols <= 0 || viewportSize.width <= 0 || viewportSize.height <= 0 || scale <= 0) {
138	    return null;
139	  }
140	
141	  const scaledCellSize = cellSize * scale;
142	  const x = metrics.originX + (-viewportOffset.x / scaledCellSize) * metrics.miniCellSize;
143	  const y = metrics.originY + (-viewportOffset.y / scaledCellSize) * metrics.miniCellSize;
144	  const width = (viewportSize.width / scaledCellSize) * metrics.miniCellSize;
145	  const height = (viewportSize.height / scaledCellSize) * metrics.miniCellSize;
146	
147	  return {
148	    x: clamp(x, metrics.originX, metrics.originX + metrics.gridWidth),
149	    y: clamp(y, metrics.originY, metrics.originY + metrics.gridHeight),
150	    width: Math.max(1, Math.min(width, metrics.gridWidth)),
151	    height: Math.max(1, Math.min(height, metrics.gridHeight)),
152	  };
153	}
154	
155	export function getViewportOffsetFromNavigatorPointer(
156	  pointer: Point,
157	  rows: number,
158	  cols: number,
159	  viewportSize: ViewportSize,
160	  scale: number,
161	  cellSize: number,
162	  metrics: NavigatorMetrics
163	): Point | null {
164	  if (rows <= 0 || cols <= 0 || viewportSize.width <= 0 || viewportSize.height <= 0 || scale <= 0) {
165	    return null;
166	  }
167	
168	  const scaledCellSize = cellSize * scale;
169	  const logicalCenterCol = (pointer.x - metrics.originX) / metrics.miniCellSize;
170	  const logicalCenterRow = (pointer.y - metrics.originY) / metrics.miniCellSize;
171	  const gridPixelWidth = cols * scaledCellSize;
172	  const gridPixelHeight = rows * scaledCellSize;
173	
174	  return {
175	    x: clamp(viewportSize.width / 2 - logicalCenterCol * scaledCellSize, viewportSize.width - gridPixelWidth, 0),
176	    y: clamp(viewportSize.height / 2 - logicalCenterRow * scaledCellSize, viewportSize.height - gridPixelHeight, 0),
177	  };
178	}
179	
```

```json
1	export type RowNumberDirection = 'row1_top' | 'row1_bottom';
2	
3	export const displayRowNumber = (
4	  arrayRow: number,
5	  totalRows: number,
6	  direction: RowNumberDirection
7	) => (direction === 'row1_top' ? arrayRow + 1 : totalRows - arrayRow);
8	
9	export const gridRowFromDisplayRow = (
10	  rowNumber: number,
11	  totalRows: number,
12	  direction: RowNumberDirection
13	) => (direction === 'row1_top' ? rowNumber - 1 : totalRows - rowNumber);
14	
```

```json
6	
7	const isEditableTarget = (target: EventTarget | null) => {
8	  if (!(target instanceof HTMLElement)) {
9	    return false;
10	  }
11	
12	  const tagName = target.tagName.toLowerCase();
13	  return tagName === 'input' || tagName === 'textarea' || tagName === 'select' || target.isContentEditable;
14	};

38	      }
39	    };
40	
41	    const handleKeyDown = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
42	      if (isEditableTarget(event.target)) {
43	        return;
44	      }
45	
46	      if ((event.code === 'ControlLeft' || event.code === 'ControlRight') && !event.repeat) {
47	        cancelCtrlClearTimer();
48	        ctrlClearTimer = window.setTimeout(() => {
49	          clearSelection();
50	          ctrlClearTimer = null;
51	        }, CTRL_CLEAR_DELAY);
52	        return;
53	      }
54	
55	      if (event.code === 'Space' && !event.repeat) {
56	        event.preventDefault();
57	        tempSwitchToPan();
58	        return;
59	      }
60	
61	      const isHistoryShortcut = event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey;
62	      if (isHistoryShortcut && event.code === 'KeyZ') {
63	        event.preventDefault();
64	        cancelCtrlClearTimer();
65	        if (event.shiftKey) {
66	          redo();
67	          return;
68	        }
69	
70	        undo();
71	        return;
72	      }
73	
74	      if (isHistoryShortcut && event.code === 'KeyY') {
75	        event.preventDefault();
76	        cancelCtrlClearTimer();
77	        redo();
78	        return;
79	      }
80	
81	      if (isHistoryShortcut && event.code === 'KeyC') {
82	        event.preventDefault();
83	        cancelCtrlClearTimer();
84	        if (selectedCell) {
85	          copySelection([selectedCell.root], selectedCell.root);
86	        }
87	        return;
88	      }
89	
90	      if (isHistoryShortcut && event.code === 'KeyX') {
91	        event.preventDefault();
92	        cancelCtrlClearTimer();
93	        if (selectedCell && cutSelection([selectedCell.root], selectedCell.root)) {
94	          clearSelection();
95	        }
96	        return;
97	      }
98	
99	      if (isHistoryShortcut && event.code === 'KeyV') {
100	        event.preventDefault();
101	        cancelCtrlClearTimer();
102	        const target = hoverRoot ?? selectedCell?.root;
103	        if (target) {
104	          const pastedRoots = pasteClipboard(target);
105	          if (pastedRoots?.length) {
106	            selectCell({ anchor: pastedRoots[0], root: pastedRoots[0] });
107	          }
108	        }
109	        return;
110	      }
111	
112	      if (event.repeat) {
113	        return;
114	      }
115	
116	      if (event.code === 'KeyV') {
117	        setInteractionMode('SELECT');
118	        return;
119	      }
120	
121	      if (event.code === 'KeyB') {
122	        setInteractionMode('DRAW');
123	        return;
124	      }
125	
126	      if (event.code === 'KeyE') {
127	        setInteractionMode('ERASE');
128	        return;
129	      }
130	
131	      if (event.code === 'KeyH') {
132	        setInteractionMode('PAN');
133	      }
134	    };
135	
136	    const handleKeyUp = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
137	      if (event.code === 'Space') {
138	        event.preventDefault();
139	        restorePreviousMode();
140	      }
141	
142	      if (event.code === 'ControlLeft' || event.code === 'ControlRight') {
143	        cancelCtrlClearTimer();
144	      }
145	    };
146	
147	    const handleWindowBlur = () => {
148	      cancelCtrlClearTimer();
149	      restorePreviousMode();
150	    };
151	
152	    window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
153	    window.addEventListener('keyup', handleKeyUp);
154	    window.addEventListener('blur', handleWindowBlur);
155	
156	    return () => {
157	      window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
158	      window.removeEventListener('keyup', handleKeyUp);
159	      window.removeEventListener('blur', handleWindowBlur);
160	      cancelCtrlClearTimer();
161	    };
162	  }, [
163	    clearSelection,
164	    copySelection,
165	    cutSelection,
166	    hoverRoot,
167	    pasteClipboard,
168	    redo,
169	    restorePreviousMode,
170	    selectCell,
171	    selectedCell,
172	    setInteractionMode,
173	    tempSwitchToPan,
174	    undo,
175	  ]);
176	
177	  return {
178	    interactionMode,
179	    tempSwitchToPan,
180	    restorePreviousMode,
181	  };
182	};
183	
```

```json
12	const SymbolPanel = ({ symbols, selectedSymbolId, onPick }: SymbolPanelProps) => {
13	  const grouped = useMemo(() => {
14	    const map = new Map<string, StitchDefinition[]>();
15	    symbols.forEach((symbol) => {
16	      const key = symbol.category || "other";
17	      if (!map.has(key)) {
18	        map.set(key, []);
19	      }

21	    });
22	    return map;
23	  }, [symbols]);

30	          <div className="symbol-grid">
31	            {list.map((symbol) => {
32	              const span = getSpanRule(symbol.id);
33	              const isMultiCell = span.width > 1;
34	              return (
35	                <button
36	                  type="button"
37	                  key={symbol.id}
38	                  className={`symbol-button ${selectedSymbolId === symbol.id ? "selected" : ""} ${isMultiCell ? "multi-cell" : ""}`}
39	                  style={isMultiCell ? { gridColumn: `span ${Math.min(span.width, 4)}` } : undefined}
40	                  onClick={() => onPick(symbol.id, symbol.svgPath)}
41	                  title={`${symbol.nameZh}${isMultiCell ? ` (${span.width}格)` : ""}`}
42	                >

45	                  </div>
46	                  <span className="symbol-label">{symbol.nameZh}</span>
47	                  {isMultiCell && <span className="span-badge">{span.width}格</span>}
48	                </button>
49	              );
50	            })}
51	          </div>
```

#### Thinking

Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the project. Let me summarize the key findings:

1. The project is a knitting pattern design app (React + TypeScript + Vite + Zustand + react-konva)
2. The bidirectional compilation engine exists in `translator.ts`:
   - `compileGridToText` (grid→text): WORKING, connected to UI
   - `parseTextToGrid` (text→grid): Logic complete, but NOT wired to any UI
3. The TextEditor is read-only - just displays compiled text
4. No Monaco/CodeMirror editor exists yet


5. The user wants to complete the bidirectional compilation engine while preserving the existing diagram→text logic

So my approach is to integrate a proper code editor like Monaco or CodeMirror 6 that supports both directions—displaying compiled output while allowing text edits to flow back into the grid. I'll need to add syntax highlighting for knitting abbreviations, auto-complete based on the stitch registry, and restore the text→grid UI connection that's currently missing.

Before diving in, I should clarify a few things: which editor framework they prefer, whether they want real-time sync or manual apply buttons, and how to handle validation feedback in the UI.


项目状态已经梳理清楚了。核心发现是：

**已完成且运行良好的部分：**
- `compileGridToText`（图解→文字）完整闭环，TextEditor 实时显示
- `parseTextToGrid`（文字→图解）逻辑完整，支持 RS/WS 方向、柔性校验、多语言匹配
- 100+ 针法注册表，含缩写/中英文名/WS 映射/SVG 路径/span 规则

**缺失的关键环节：**
- TextEditor 是只读的，没有任何可编辑入口
- `parseTextToGrid` + `applyTextToGrid` 逻辑存在但完全没有 UI 触发
- 没有接入任何代码编辑器（Monaco / CodeMirror 均未引入）

在动手之前，有几个关键决策想和你确认：

> Read: `D:\aaa-llx\MyKinttingDesign\MyKinttingDesignApp\src\utils\translator.ts`

**Output:**

```json
1	import { stitchRegistry } from '../configs/stitchRegistry';
2	import { CellData } from '../store/projectStore';
3	import { displayRowNumber, type RowNumberDirection } from './rowNumbering';
4	
5	export interface ValidationResult {
6	  valid: boolean;
7	  delta: number;
8	  message: string;
9	}
10	
11	export type TextLocale = 'abbr' | 'en' | 'zh';
12	
13	export interface CompileOptions {
14	  locale?: TextLocale;
15	  rowNumberDirection?: RowNumberDirection;
16	}
17	
18	export interface ParsedRowResult {
19	  rowNumber: number;
20	  cells: CellData[];
21	  validation: ValidationResult;
22	}
23	
24	/**
25	 * 提取连续相同的针法并聚合
26	 */
27	function aggregateStitches(instructions: string[]): string[] {
28	  const aggregated: string[] = [];
29	  let currentStitch = '';
30	  let count = 0;
31	
32	  const flush = () => {
33	    if (count > 0) {
34	      aggregated.push(count === 1 ? currentStitch : `${count} ${currentStitch}`);
35	    }
36	  };
37	
38	  for (const inst of instructions) {
39	    if (inst === currentStitch) {
40	      count++;
41	    } else {
42	      flush();
43	      currentStitch = inst;
44	      count = 1;
45	    }
46	  }
47	  flush();
48	
49	  return aggregated;
50	}
51	
52	function normalizeLabel(label: string) {
53	  return label.trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ').toLowerCase();
54	}
55	
56	function resolveDisplayLabel(stitchId: string, locale: TextLocale, isEvenRow: boolean) {
57	  const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[stitchId];
58	  if (!stitchDef) {
59	    return stitchId;
60	  }
61	
62	  const resolvedId = isEvenRow && stitchDef.wsStitchId ? stitchDef.wsStitchId : stitchId;
63	  const resolvedDef = stitchRegistry[resolvedId] ?? stitchDef;
64	
65	  if (locale === 'zh') {
66	    return resolvedDef.nameZh ?? stitchDef.nameZh ?? stitchId;
67	  }
68	
69	  if (locale === 'en') {
70	    return resolvedDef.nameEn ?? stitchDef.nameEn ?? resolvedDef.nameZh ?? stitchId;
71	  }
72	
73	  return resolvedDef.abbrev ?? stitchDef.abbrev ?? resolvedDef.nameEn ?? resolvedDef.nameZh ?? stitchId;
74	}
75	
76	/**
77	 * 将二维网格编译为自然语言文字说明
78	 */
79	export function compileGridToText(grid: CellData[][], options: CompileOptions = {}): string {
80	  if (!grid || grid.length === 0) return '';
81	  
82	  const locale = options.locale ?? 'abbr';
83	  const rowNumberDirection = options.rowNumberDirection ?? 'row1_top';
84	  const textLines: string[] = [];
85	  const rows = grid.length;
86	  const cols = grid[0].length;
87	
88	  const rowIndices =
89	    rowNumberDirection === 'row1_top'
90	      ? Array.from({ length: rows }, (_, row) => row)
91	      : Array.from({ length: rows }, (_, row) => rows - 1 - row);
92	
93	  for (const r of rowIndices) {
94	    const rowNumber = displayRowNumber(r, rows, rowNumberDirection);
95	    const isEvenRow = rowNumber % 2 === 0;
96	    
97	    // 奇数行（正面 RS）从右向左读图；偶数行（反面 WS）从左向右读图
98	    let colIndices = Array.from({ length: cols }, (_, i) => i);
99	    if (!isEvenRow) {
100	      colIndices = colIndices.reverse();
101	    }
102	    
103	    const rowRawInstructions: string[] = [];
104	    let hasStitchInRow = false;
105	    
106	    for (const c of colIndices) {
107	      const cell = grid[r][c];
108	      
109	      // 跳过没有对应源针法的格子（或是跨格的子节点。因为跨格的主节点通常是在左上或者自身）
110	      // TODO: 此处我们简化，只要是 isSpanChild 就跳过，让 root 单独报告
111	      if (cell.isSpanChild) continue;
112	      
113	      if (!cell.stitchId) {
114	        continue;
115	      }
116	      hasStitchInRow = true;
117	      
118	      const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
119	      if (!stitchDef) continue;
120	      
121	      const displayLabel = resolveDisplayLabel(cell.stitchId, locale, isEvenRow);
122	      
123	      // 针对部分多列针法，比如 c4f 需要占用的针数，这里仅简单视作一个整体指令
124	      rowRawInstructions.push(displayLabel);
125	    }
126	    
127	    if (hasStitchInRow) {
128	      const merged = aggregateStitches(rowRawInstructions);
129	      textLines.push(`Row ${rowNumber}: ${merged.join(', ')}.`);
130	    }
131	  }
132	  
133	  return textLines.join('\n');
134	}
135	
136	/**
137	 * 建立反向字典表，用于将简写映射回 stitchId
138	 */
139	const abbrevToStitchId: Record<string, string> = {};
140	const labelToStitchId: Record<string, string> = {};
141	Object.values(stitchRegistry).forEach(def => {
142	  // 这里我们直接映射为图解符号，因此都是正面视角 (RS) 的原始符号 ID
143	  if (def.abbrev) abbrevToStitchId[normalizeLabel(def.abbrev)] = def.id;
144	  if (def.nameEn) labelToStitchId[normalizeLabel(def.nameEn)] = def.id;
145	  if (def.nameZh) labelToStitchId[normalizeLabel(def.nameZh)] = def.id;
146	});
147	
148	/**
149	 * 解析用户输入的自然语言，转换为对应这行的 Grid Cell 结构。
150	 * Demo 版核心链路：按行解析如 "Row 1: 3 k, 2 p"
151	 */
152	export function parseTextToGrid(text: string, cols: number): ParsedRowResult[] {
153	  const results: ParsedRowResult[] = [];
154	  const lines = text.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim() !== '');
155	  
156	  // Row 匹配正则，例如: "Row 1: 3 k, 2 p." / "Row 1: 3 knit, 2 purl."
157	  const rowRegex = /Row\s+(\d+):(.+)/i;
158	  
159	  for (const line of lines) {
160	    const rowMatch = line.match(rowRegex);
161	    if (!rowMatch) continue;
162	    
163	    const rowNumber = parseInt(rowMatch[1], 10);
164	    const instructionsPart = rowMatch[2];
165	    
166	    // 正面行（奇数行），从右往左布置
167	    // 反面行（偶数行），从左往右布置
168	    const isEvenRow = rowNumber % 2 === 0;
169	    
170	    const cells: CellData[] = [];
171	    let stitchCount = 0; // 这行指令要求的总格子数
172	    
173	    const instructionSegments = instructionsPart.split(',').map(part => part.trim()).filter(Boolean);
174	    for (const segment of instructionSegments) {
175	      const segmentMatch = segment.match(/^(?:(\d+)\s*)?(.+?)\.?$/);
176	      if (!segmentMatch) continue;
177	
178	      const count = segmentMatch[1] ? parseInt(segmentMatch[1], 10) : 1;
179	      const rawLabel = segmentMatch[2].trim();
180	      const normalizedLabel = normalizeLabel(rawLabel);
181	      
182	      // 查反向映射
183	      let targetStitchId = abbrevToStitchId[normalizedLabel] ?? labelToStitchId[normalizedLabel];
184	      
185	      if (!targetStitchId) {
186	        // 如果找不到，直接跳过或者记录个 warning，这里暂跳过
187	        continue;
188	      }
189	      
190	      // 反面行的输入需要反转回去以作为图解在界面上显示。由于图解永远是正面的。
191	      // 如果输入文本说反面(Even Row)要织 p，意味着我们在图纸上它是 k-knit。
192	      if (isEvenRow) {
193	        const potentialTargetStr = Object.values(stitchRegistry).find(
194	          def => def.wsStitchId === targetStitchId
195	        )?.id;
196	        if (potentialTargetStr) targetStitchId = potentialTargetStr;
197	      }
198	      
199	      for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
200	        cells.push({
201	          char: '',
202	          stitchId: targetStitchId
203	        });
204	        
205	        // 简单计算一下针法跨格 (复杂多格针法例如 c4f 可能需要在渲染端另作补全，这里暂按占用首格算)
206	        stitchCount += (stitchRegistry[targetStitchId]?.span?.width || 1);
207	      }
208	    }
209	    
210	    // 柔性校验
211	    let delta = stitchCount - cols;
212	    let valid = delta <= 0; // 只要没超出列宽就算有效，或者你也可以设为严格等于
213	    let message = '✅ 解析成功';
214	    if (delta > 0) {
215	      message = `⚠️ 这行需要 ${stitchCount} 针，但画板宽度仅为 ${cols}，超出了 ${delta} 针。`;
216	    } else if (delta < 0) {
217	      message = `ℹ️ 这行排布后画布剩余 ${Math.abs(delta)} 针空白。`;
218	    }
219	    
220	    results.push({
221	      rowNumber,
222	      cells,
223	      validation: { valid, delta, message }
224	    });
225	  }
226	  
227	  return results;
228	}
229	
```

```json
8	const LOCALES: Array<{ id: TextLocale; label: string }> = [
9	  { id: 'abbr', label: 'Abbr' },
10	  { id: 'en', label: 'EN' },
11	  { id: 'zh', label: '中文' },

14	export const TextEditor: React.FC = () => {
15	  const {
16	    grids,
17	    currentMode,
18	    textLocale,
19	    setTextLocale,
20	    rowNumberDirection,
21	    setRowNumberDirection,
22	  } = useProjectStore();

26	  const rowsInGrid = currentGrid.length;

33	      .filter(Boolean)
34	      .map((line) => {

36	        return { line, rowNumber };
37	      });
38	  }, [currentGrid, rowNumberDirection, textLocale]);
39	
40	  const handleRowClick = (rowNumber: number) => {
41	    const gridRow = gridRowFromDisplayRow(rowNumber, rowsInGrid, rowNumberDirection);
42	    if (gridRow >= 0 && gridRow < rowsInGrid) {
43	      setHighlightedRow(gridRow);
44	    }
45	  };
46	
47	  return (
48	    <div className="text-editor-container instruction-map-panel">

54	      </div>

57	        <button

59	          className={rowNumberDirection === 'row1_top' ? 'locale-chip is-active' : 'locale-chip'}
60	          onClick={() => setRowNumberDirection('row1_top')}
61	        >
62	          Row 1 顶部
63	        </button>
64	        <button
65	          type="button"
66	          className={rowNumberDirection === 'row1_bottom' ? 'locale-chip is-active' : 'locale-chip'}
67	          onClick={() => setRowNumberDirection('row1_bottom')}
68	        >

70	        </button>
71	      </div>

74	        {LOCALES.map((locale) => (
75	          <button
76	            key={locale.id}
77	            type="button"
78	            className={textLocale === locale.id ? 'locale-chip is-active' : 'locale-chip'}
79	            onClick={() => setTextLocale(locale.id)}
80	          >
81	            {locale.label}
82	          </button>
83	        ))}
84	      </div>
85	
86	      <div className="instruction-map-list" aria-label="只读指令映射">
87	        {instructionLines.length ? (
88	          instructionLines.map(({ line, rowNumber }) => (
89	            <button
90	              key={`${rowNumber}-${line}`}
91	              type="button"
92	              className="instruction-map-row"
93	              onClick={() => handleRowClick(rowNumber)}
94	            >
95	              {line}
96	            </button>
97	          ))
98	        ) : (
99	          <p className="instruction-map-empty">画布中暂无可映射的针法。</p>
100	        )}
101	      </div>
102	    </div>
103	  );
104	};
```

```json
176	const storageReplacer = (_key: string, value: unknown) => {
177	  if (value instanceof Map) {
178	    return { __type: 'Map', value: Array.from(value.entries()) };
179	  }
180	  if (value instanceof Set) {
181	    return { __type: 'Set', value: Array.from(value.values()) };
182	  }
183	  if (value instanceof Date) {
184	    return { __type: 'Date', value: value.toISOString() };

190	  if (!isPlainObject(value) || typeof value.__type !== 'string') {
191	    return value;
192	  }
193	
194	  switch (value.__type) {
195	    case 'Map':
196	      return new Map(value.value as Array<[unknown, unknown]>);
197	    case 'Set':
198	      return new Set(value.value as Array<unknown>);
199	    case 'Date':
200	      return new Date(value.value as string);
201	    default:

203	  }

227	const getRootPosition = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number) => {
228	  const cell = grid[row]?.[col];
229	  if (!cell) return null;
230	  if (cell.isSpanChild && cell.parentPos) return cell.parentPos;
231	  return { row, col };

234	const clearStitchAtRoot = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number) => {
235	  const root = getRootPosition(grid, row, col);
236	  if (!root) return false;
237	  const cell = grid[root.row]?.[root.col];
238	  if (!cell?.stitchId) return false;
239	
240	  const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
241	  const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
242	  const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
243	  let changed = false;
244	
245	  for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
246	    for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
247	      const target = grid[root.row + i]?.[root.col + j];
248	      if (target) {
249	        grid[root.row + i][root.col + j] = {};
250	        changed = true;
251	      }
252	    }
253	  }
254	
255	  return changed;
256	};

258	const placeStitchSnapshot = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number, snapshot: CellData) => {
259	  if (!snapshot.stitchId) return false;
260	  const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[snapshot.stitchId];
261	  const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
262	  const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
263	
264	  if (row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > grid.length || col + spanW > (grid[0]?.length ?? 0)) {
265	    return false;
266	  }
267	
268	  for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
269	    for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
270	      if (i === 0 && j === 0) {
271	        grid[row][col] = {
272	          ...snapshot,
273	          isSpanChild: false,
274	          parentPos: undefined,
275	          svgPath: snapshot.svgPath || stitchDef?.svgPath || '',
276	        };
277	      } else {
278	        grid[row + i][col + j] = {
279	          char: '',
280	          svgPath: '',
281	          stitchId: snapshot.stitchId,
282	          isSpanChild: true,
283	          parentPos: { row, col },
284	        };
285	      }
286	    }
287	  }
288	
289	  return true;
290	};

292	// Config localforage
293	const localforageInstance = (localforage as any).default ?? localforage;
294	const storage = localforageInstance.createInstance({
295	  name: 'kintting-design-db',
296	  storeName: 'projects'
```
