```json
300	  .setDriver([localforageInstance.INDEXEDDB, localforageInstance.WEBSQL, localforageInstance.LOCALSTORAGE])
301	  .catch(() => {
302	    console.warn('localforage failed to set preferred drivers; falling back to defaults');
303	  });
304	
305	const forageStorage: StateStorage = {
306	  getItem: async (name: string): Promise<string | null> => {
307	    let val = (await storage.getItem(name)) as string | null;
308	    // Legacy migration step from simple localStorage
309	    if (!val && typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.localStorage) {
310	      val = window.localStorage.getItem(name);
311	      if (val) {
312	        try {
313	          await storage.setItem(name, val);
314	        } catch (e) {
315	          console.warn('Failed to migrate item to localforage', e);
316	        }
317	      }
318	    }
319	    return val || null;
320	  },
321	  setItem: async (name: string, value: string): Promise<void> => {
322	    await storage.setItem(name, value);
323	  },
324	  removeItem: async (name: string): Promise<void> => {
325	    await storage.removeItem(name);
326	  },
327	};
328	
329	// Default autosave debounce delay (ms). Increase to reduce save frequency.
330	const DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS = 10000;
331	const AUTOSAVE_DELAY_STORAGE_KEY = 'kintting:autosaveDelayMs';
332	
333	// Create a debounced wrapper around the forage storage so frequent writes
334	// (e.g., during continuous drawing) are coalesced. Exposes the same
335	// StateStorage async API expected by zustand's persistence layer.
336	const createDebouncedForageStorage = (delay = DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS): StateStorage => {
337	  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return forageStorage;
338	
339	  let timeout: number | undefined;
340	  const pending = new Map<string, string>();
341	  let flushing = false;
342	
343	  const flush = async () => {
344	    if (flushing) return;
345	    flushing = true;
346	    for (const [k, v] of pending) {
347	      try {
348	        await storage.setItem(k, v);
349	      } catch (e) {
350	        // ignore individual write errors
351	        console.warn('debounced storage setItem failed', e);
352	      }
353	    }
354	    pending.clear();
355	    if (typeof timeout !== 'undefined') {
356	      clearTimeout(timeout);
357	      timeout = undefined;
358	    }
359	    flushing = false;
360	  };
361	
362	  try {
363	    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
364	      // flush synchronously where possible
365	      if (pending.size) {
366	        // best-effort flush (no await in beforeunload)
367	        void flush();
368	      }
369	    });
370	  } catch (e) {
371	    // ignore
372	  }
373	
374	  return {
375	    getItem: async (name: string) => {
376	      // If we have a pending value for this key, return it first
377	      if (pending.has(name)) return pending.get(name) as string;
378	      return (await storage.getItem(name)) as string | null;
379	    },
380	    setItem: async (name: string, value: string) => {
381	      pending.set(name, value);
382	      // read current configured delay from localStorage if available
383	      let configured = delay;
384	      try {
385	        const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(AUTOSAVE_DELAY_STORAGE_KEY);
386	        const parsed = raw ? Number(raw) : NaN;
387	        if (!Number.isNaN(parsed) && parsed > 0) configured = parsed;
388	      } catch (e) {
389	        // ignore
390	      }
391	      if (typeof timeout !== 'undefined') clearTimeout(timeout);
392	      timeout = window.setTimeout(() => void flush(), configured) as unknown as number;
393	    },
394	    removeItem: async (name: string) => {
395	      pending.delete(name);
396	      try {
397	        await storage.removeItem(name);
398	      } catch (e) {
399	        console.warn('debounced storage removeItem failed', e);
400	      }
401	    },
402	  };
403	};
404	
405	export const useProjectStore = create<ProjectState>()(
406	  persist(
407	    (set, get) => {
408	      const updateActiveProject = (updater: (project: Project) => Partial<Project>) => {
409	        const state = get();
410	        if (!state.activeProjectId) return;
411	        const project = state.projects[state.activeProjectId];
412	        if (!project) return;
413	        const nextProject = {
414	          ...project,
415	          ...updater(project),
416	          lastModified: Date.now()
417	        };
418	        set({
419	          projects: {
420	            ...state.projects,
421	            [state.activeProjectId]: nextProject
422	          },
423	          ...projectView(nextProject)
424	        });
425	      };
426	
427	      return {
428	        projects: {},
429	        deletedProjects: {},
430	        activeProjectId: null,
431	        ...emptyProjectView(),
432	        clipboard: null,
433	        validationResults: [],
434	
435	        createProject: (name, rows = 20, cols = 20) => {
436	          const newProject = createProjectRecord(name, rows, cols);
437	          set((state) => ({
438	            projects: { ...state.projects, [newProject.id]: newProject },
439	            activeProjectId: newProject.id,
440	            ...projectView(newProject)
441	          }));
442	          return newProject.id;
443	        },
444	
445	        switchProject: (id) => {
446	          const project = get().projects[id];
447	          if (!project) return;
448	          set({ activeProjectId: id, ...projectView(project), validationResults: [] });
449	        },
450	
451	        deleteProject: (id) => {
452	          set((state) => {
453	            const nextProjects = { ...state.projects };
454	            const projectToDelete = nextProjects[id];
455	            if (!projectToDelete) return state;
456	
457	            delete nextProjects[id];
458	            const nextDeletedProjects = {
459	              ...state.deletedProjects,
460	              [id]: { ...projectToDelete, deletedAt: Date.now() },
461	            };
462	
463	            const fallback = Object.values(nextProjects).sort((a, b) => b.lastModified - a.lastModified)[0];
464	            return {
465	              projects: nextProjects,
466	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
467	              activeProjectId: state.activeProjectId === id ? fallback?.id ?? null : state.activeProjectId,
468	              ...(state.activeProjectId === id ? (fallback ? projectView(fallback) : emptyProjectView()) : {})
469	            };
470	          });
471	        },
472	
473	        restoreProject: (id) => {
474	          set((state) => {
475	            const deleted = state.deletedProjects[id];
476	            if (!deleted) return state;
477	
478	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
479	            delete nextDeletedProjects[id];
480	
481	            const restoredProject = {
482	              ...deleted,
483	              deletedAt: undefined,
484	              lastModified: Date.now(),
485	            };
486	
487	            return {
488	              projects: { ...state.projects, [id]: restoredProject },
489	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
490	            };
491	          });
492	        },
493	
494	        deleteProjectPermanently: (id) => {
495	          set((state) => {
496	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
497	            delete nextDeletedProjects[id];
498	            return { deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects };
499	          });
500	        },
501	
502	        emptyRecycleBin: () => {
503	          set({ deletedProjects: {} });
504	        },
505	
506	        purgeExpiredProjects: () => {
507	          set((state) => {
508	            const nextProjects = { ...state.projects };
509	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
510	            let changed = false;
511	
512	            Object.entries(state.projects).forEach(([id, project]) => {
513	              if (state.activeProjectId === id) return;
514	              if (Date.now() - project.lastModified > EXPIRY_SOFT_DELETE_MS) {
515	                nextDeletedProjects[id] = { ...project, deletedAt: Date.now() };
516	                delete nextProjects[id];
517	                changed = true;
518	              }
519	            });
520	
521	            if (!changed) return state;
522	
523	            const fallback = Object.values(nextProjects).sort((a, b) => b.lastModified - a.lastModified)[0];
524	            const nextActiveId = state.activeProjectId && nextProjects[state.activeProjectId] ? state.activeProjectId : fallback?.id ?? null;
525	
526	            return {
527	              projects: nextProjects,
528	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
529	              activeProjectId: nextActiveId,
530	              ...(nextActiveId ? projectView(nextProjects[nextActiveId]) : emptyProjectView()),
531	            };
532	          });
533	        },
534	
535	        renameProject: (id, name) => {
536	          const nextName = name.trim();
537	          if (!nextName) return;
538	          set((state) => {
539	            const project = state.projects[id];
540	            if (!project) return state;
541	            const nextProject = { ...project, name: nextName, lastModified: Date.now() };
542	            return {
543	              projects: {
544	                ...state.projects,
545	                [id]: nextProject,
546	              },
547	              ...(state.activeProjectId === id ? projectView(nextProject) : {}),
548	            };
549	          });
550	        },
551	
552	        duplicateProject: (id) => {
553	          const project = get().projects[id];
554	          if (!project) return null;
555	          const nextProject = cloneProject(project, `${project.name} Copy`);
556	          set((state) => ({
557	            projects: { ...state.projects, [nextProject.id]: nextProject },
558	            activeProjectId: nextProject.id,
559	            ...projectView(nextProject),
560	          }));
561	          return nextProject.id;
562	        },
563	
564	        updateProjectThumbnail: (id, thumbnail) => {
565	          set((state) => {
566	            const project = state.projects[id];
567	            if (!project) return state;
568	            return {
569	              projects: {
570	                ...state.projects,
571	                [id]: { ...project, thumbnail, lastModified: Date.now() }
572	              }
573	            };
574	          });
575	        },
576	
577	        replaceModeGrid: (mode, grid, resetHistory = true) => {
578	          const { activeProjectId } = get();
579	          if (!activeProjectId) {
580	            get().createProject('Untitled Project', grid.length, grid[0]?.length ?? 0);
581	          }
582	
583	          updateActiveProject((project) => ({
584	            grids: { ...project.grids, [mode]: cloneGrid(grid) },
585	            currentMode: mode,
586	            ...(resetHistory ? { undoStack: [], redoStack: [] } : {}),
587	          }));
588	        },
589	
590	        setMode: (mode) => {
591	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ currentMode: mode }));
592	        },
593	
594	        setTextLocale: (locale) => {
595	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ textLocale: locale }));
596	          get().compileToText();
597	        },
598	
599	        setRowNumberDirection: (direction) => {
600	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ rowNumberDirection: direction }));
601	          get().compileToText();
602	        },
603	
604	        initGrid: (rows, cols) => {
605	          if (!get().activeProjectId) {
606	            get().createProject('Untitled Project', rows, cols);
607	            return;
608	          }
609	
610	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ 
611	            grids: { 
612	              knit: createEmptyGrid(rows, cols), 
613	              crochet: createEmptyGrid(rows, cols) 
614	            },
615	            description: '',
616	            undoStack: [], 
617	            redoStack: [] 
618	          }));
619	        },
620	
621	        applyCellChange: (row, col, char, svgPath, stitchId) => {
622	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
623	          if (!activeProjectId) return false;
624	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
625	
626	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
627	          if (!currentGrid[row] || !currentGrid[row][col]) return false;
628	        
629	          const isErasing = !stitchId;
630	          const stitchDef = stitchId ? stitchRegistry[stitchId] : null;
631	        
632	          const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
633	          const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
634	
635	          let needsUpdate = false;
636	          const newGrid = currentGrid.map(r => [...r]);
637	
638	          const clearStitchAt = (r: number, c: number) => {
639	            const cell = newGrid[r]?.[c];
640	            if (!cell) return;
641	            if (cell.isSpanChild && cell.parentPos) {
642	              clearStitchAt(cell.parentPos.row, cell.parentPos.col);
643	              return;
644	            }
645	          
646	            const sDef = cell.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId] : null;
647	            const cSpanW = sDef?.span?.width || 1;
648	            const cSpanH = sDef?.span?.height || 1;
649	          
650	            for (let i = 0; i < cSpanH; i++) {
651	              for (let j = 0; j < cSpanW; j++) {
652	                if (newGrid[r + i] && newGrid[r + i][c + j]) {
653	                  newGrid[r + i][c + j] = { ...newGrid[r + i][c + j], char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: '', isSpanChild: false, parentPos: undefined };
654	                  needsUpdate = true;
655	                }
656	              }
657	            }
658	          };
659	
660	          if (isErasing) {
661	            if (newGrid[row][col].stitchId || newGrid[row][col].isSpanChild) {
662	              clearStitchAt(row, col);
663	            }
664	          } else {
665	            if (row + spanH > currentGrid.length || col + spanW > currentGrid[0].length) {
666	              return false; 
667	            }
668	
669	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
670	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
671	                 const tarR = row + i;
672	                 const tarC = col + j;
673	                 if (newGrid[tarR]?.[tarC] && (newGrid[tarR][tarC].stitchId || newGrid[tarR][tarC].isSpanChild)) {
674	                   clearStitchAt(tarR, tarC);
675	                 }
676	              }
677	            }
678	
679	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
680	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
681	                const tarR = row + i;
682	                const tarC = col + j;
683	                if (newGrid[tarR] && newGrid[tarR][tarC]) {
684	                  if (i === 0 && j === 0) {
685	                    newGrid[tarR][tarC] = { ...newGrid[tarR][tarC], char, svgPath, stitchId, isSpanChild: false, parentPos: undefined };
686	                  } else {
687	                    newGrid[tarR][tarC] = { ...newGrid[tarR][tarC], char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: stitchId, isSpanChild: true, parentPos: { row, col } };
688	                  }
689	                  needsUpdate = true;
690	                }
691	              }
692	            }
693	          }
694	
695	          if (needsUpdate) {
696	            get()._saveSnapshot();
697	            updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid } }));
698	            get().compileToText();
699	            return true;
700	          }
701	
702	          return false;
703	        },
704	
705	        copySelection: (roots, anchor) => {
706	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
707	          if (!activeProjectId || !anchor || roots.length === 0) return false;
708	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
709	
710	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
711	          const seen = new Set<string>();
712	          const items: ClipboardItem[] = [];
713	
714	          for (const root of roots) {
715	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
716	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
717	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
718	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
719	            seen.add(key);
720	
721	            const cell = currentGrid[resolvedRoot.row]?.[resolvedRoot.col];
722	            if (!cell?.stitchId || cell.isSpanChild) continue;
723	
724	            items.push({
725	              dr: resolvedRoot.row - anchor.row,
726	              dc: resolvedRoot.col - anchor.col,
727	              cellSnapshot: { ...cell, parentPos: undefined, isSpanChild: false },
728	            });
729	          }
730	
731	          if (!items.length) return false;
732	          set({ clipboard: { anchor, items } });
733	          return true;
734	        },
735	
736	        cutSelection: (roots, anchor) => {
737	          if (!get().copySelection(roots, anchor)) return false;
738	
739	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
740	          if (!activeProjectId) return false;
741	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
742	
743	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
744	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
745	          let changed = false;
746	
747	          const seen = new Set<string>();
748	          for (const root of roots) {
749	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
750	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
751	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
752	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
753	            seen.add(key);
754	            changed = clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col) || changed;
755	          }
756	
757	          if (!changed) return false;
758	          get()._saveSnapshot();
759	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
760	          get().compileToText();
761	          return true;
762	        },
763	
764	        pasteClipboard: (target) => {
765	          const { activeProjectId, projects, clipboard } = get();
766	          if (!activeProjectId || !clipboard?.items.length) return null;
767	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
768	
769	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
770	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
771	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
772	          const placements = clipboard.items.map((item) => ({
773	            row: target.row + item.dr,
774	            col: target.col + item.dc,
775	            item,
776	          }));
777	
778	          const isOutOfBounds = placements.some(({ row, col, item }) => {
779	            const stitchDef = item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
780	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
781	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
782	            return row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > rows || col + spanW > cols;
783	          });
784	
785	          if (isOutOfBounds) return null;
786	
787	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
788	          for (const placement of placements) {
789	            placeStitchSnapshot(nextGrid, placement.row, placement.col, placement.item.cellSnapshot);
790	          }
791	
792	          get()._saveSnapshot();
793	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
794	          get().compileToText();
795	          return placements.map(({ row, col }) => ({ row, col }));
796	        },
797	
798	        exportSnapshot: () => {
799	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
800	          if (!activeProjectId) return { pages: [] };
801	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
802	
803	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
804	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
805	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
806	
807	          const pageWidth = 595.28;
808	          const pageHeight = 841.89;
809	          const cellSize = 16;
810	          const gridWidth = cols * cellSize;
811	          const gridHeight = rows * cellSize;
812	          const pageScale = Math.min(pageWidth / Math.max(gridWidth, 1), pageHeight / Math.max(gridHeight, 1), 1);
813	
814	          const glyphs = [] as Array<{
815	            id: string;
816	            svgPath: string;
817	            transform: { tx: number; ty: number; scale: number };
818	            bounds: { w: number; h: number };
819	          }>;
820	
821	          for (let row = 0; row < rows; row += 1) {
822	            for (let col = 0; col < cols; col += 1) {
823	              const cell = currentGrid[row]?.[col];
824	              if (!cell?.stitchId || cell.isSpanChild) continue;
825	              const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
826	              if (!stitchDef) continue;
827	
828	              const spanW = stitchDef.span.width || 1;
829	              const spanH = stitchDef.span.height || 1;
830	              glyphs.push({
831	                id: `${row}-${col}-${cell.stitchId}`,
832	                svgPath: stitchDef.svgPath,
833	                transform: {
834	                  tx: col * cellSize * pageScale,
835	                  ty: row * cellSize * pageScale,
836	                  scale: pageScale,
837	                },
838	                bounds: {
839	                  w: spanW * cellSize * pageScale,
840	                  h: spanH * cellSize * pageScale,
841	                },
842	              });
843	            }
844	          }
845	
846	          return {
847	            pages: [
848	              {
849	                width: pageWidth,
850	                height: pageHeight,
851	                glyphs,
852	              },
853	            ],
854	          } as ExportSnapshot;
855	        },
856	
857	        moveSelection: (roots, anchor, target) => {
858	          if (!get().copySelection(roots, anchor)) return null;
859	
860	          const { activeProjectId, projects, clipboard } = get();
861	          if (!activeProjectId || !clipboard?.items.length) return null;
862	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
863	
864	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
865	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
866	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
867	          const placements = clipboard.items.map((item) => ({
868	            row: target.row + item.dr,
869	            col: target.col + item.dc,
870	            item,
871	          }));
872	
873	          const isOutOfBounds = placements.some(({ row, col, item }) => {
874	            const stitchDef = item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
875	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
876	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
877	            return row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > rows || col + spanW > cols;
878	          });
879	
880	          if (isOutOfBounds) return null;
881	
882	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
883	
884	          for (const placement of placements) {
885	            const stitchDef = placement.item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[placement.item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
886	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
887	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
888	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
889	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
890	                clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, placement.row + i, placement.col + j);
891	              }
892	            }
893	          }
894	
895	          const seen = new Set<string>();
896	          for (const root of roots) {
897	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
898	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
899	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
900	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
901	            seen.add(key);
902	            clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
903	          }
904	
905	          for (const placement of placements) {
906	            placeStitchSnapshot(nextGrid, placement.row, placement.col, placement.item.cellSnapshot);
907	          }
908	
909	          get()._saveSnapshot();
910	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
911	          get().compileToText();
912	          return placements.map(({ row, col }) => ({ row, col }));
913	        },
914	
915	        compileToText: () => {
916	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
917	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
918	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
919	
920	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
921	          const text = compileGridToText(currentGrid, { locale: project.textLocale, rowNumberDirection: project.rowNumberDirection });
922	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ description: text }));
923	        },
924	
925	        applyTextToGrid: (text: string) => {
926	          const { activeProjectId, projects, _saveSnapshot } = get();
927	          if (!activeProjectId) return [];
928	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
929	
930	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
931	          const rowsInGrid = currentGrid.length;
932	          const colsInGrid = currentGrid.length > 0 ? currentGrid[0].length : 0;
933	
934	          const parsedRows = parseTextToGrid(text, colsInGrid);
935	
936	          set({ validationResults: parsedRows });
937	
938	          const hasInvalidRows = parsedRows.some((r: any) => !r.validation.valid);
939	
940	          if (hasInvalidRows) {
941	            if (text.trim() === '') {
942	              updateActiveProject(() => ({ description: '' }));
943	            } else {
944	              get().compileToText(); 
945	            }
946	            return parsedRows; 
947	          }
948	
949	          _saveSnapshot(); 
950	
951	          let maxColsFromText = colsInGrid;
952	          parsedRows.forEach((pRow: any) => {
953	            if (pRow.validation.delta > 0) {
954	              maxColsFromText = Math.max(maxColsFromText, colsInGrid + pRow.validation.delta);
955	            }
956	          });
957	
958	          let newGrid = createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText);
959	    
960	          if (rowsInGrid === 0 || text.trim() === '') {
961	            newGrid = createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText); 
962	            updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid }, description: '' }));
963	            return parsedRows;
964	          }
965	
966	          parsedRows.forEach((parsed: any) => {
967	            const gridRowIndex = gridRowFromDisplayRow(parsed.rowNumber, rowsInGrid, project.rowNumberDirection);
968	            if (gridRowIndex >= 0 && gridRowIndex < rowsInGrid) {
969	              const isEvenRow = parsed.rowNumber % 2 === 0;
970	              let currentCol = isEvenRow ? 0 : maxColsFromText - 1;
971	
972	              for (const cell of parsed.cells) {
973	                const stitchId = cell.stitchId!;
974	                const spanW = stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.span?.width || 1;
975	                const dir = isEvenRow ? 1 : -1;
976	
977	                const endCol = currentCol + dir * (spanW - 1);
978	                if (dir === 1 && endCol >= maxColsFromText) continue; 
979	                if (dir === -1 && endCol < 0) continue; 
980	
981	                if (currentCol >= 0 && currentCol < maxColsFromText) {
982	                  newGrid[gridRowIndex][currentCol] = {
983	                    ...cell,
984	                    svgPath: stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.svgPath || '',
985	                    isSpanChild: false,
986	                    parentPos: undefined,
987	                  };
988	                }
989	
990	                for (let k = 1; k < spanW; k++) {
991	                  const childCol = currentCol + dir * k;
992	                  if (childCol >= 0 && childCol < maxColsFromText) {
993	                    newGrid[gridRowIndex][childCol] = {
994	                      char: '',
995	                      svgPath: '',
996	                      stitchId,
997	                      isSpanChild: true,
998	                      parentPos: { row: gridRowIndex, col: currentCol },
999	                    };
1000	                  }
1001	                }
1002	                currentCol = currentCol + dir * spanW;
1003	              }
1004	            }
1005	          });
1006	
1007	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid }, description: text }));
1008	          return parsedRows;
1009	        },
1010	
1011	        resizeGrid: (newCols: number) => {
1012	          const { activeProjectId, projects, _saveSnapshot } = get();
1013	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1014	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1015	
1016	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
1017	          const currentRows = currentGrid.length;
1018	          const currentCols = currentGrid.length > 0 ? currentGrid[0].length : 0;
1019	
1020	          if (newCols === currentCols) return; 
1021	
1022	          _saveSnapshot(); 
1023	
1024	          const newGrid = createEmptyGrid(currentRows, newCols);
1025	
1026	          for (let r = 0; r < currentRows; r++) {
1027	            for (let c = 0; c < Math.min(currentCols, newCols); c++) {
1028	              newGrid[r][c] = currentGrid[r][c];
1029	            }
1030	          }
1031	
1032	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid } }));
1033	          get().compileToText(); 
1034	        },
1035	
1036	        undo: () => {
1037	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1038	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1039	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1040	
1041	          if (project.undoStack.length === 0) return;
1042	        
1043	          const previous = project.undoStack[project.undoStack.length - 1];
1044	          const newUndoStack = project.undoStack.slice(0, -1);
1045	        
1046	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1047	            grids: previous.grids,
1048	            currentMode: previous.currentMode,
1049	            description: previous.description || '',
1050	            undoStack: newUndoStack,
1051	            redoStack: [...project.redoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1052	          }));
1053	        },
1054	
1055	        redo: () => {
1056	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1057	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1058	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1059	
1060	          if (project.redoStack.length === 0) return;
1061	        
1062	          const next = project.redoStack[project.redoStack.length - 1];
1063	          const newRedoStack = project.redoStack.slice(0, -1);
1064	        
1065	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1066	            grids: next.grids,
1067	            currentMode: next.currentMode,
1068	            description: next.description || '',
1069	            undoStack: [...project.undoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1070	            redoStack: newRedoStack,
1071	          }));
1072	        },
1073	
1074	        _saveSnapshot: () => {
1075	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1076	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1077	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1078	
1079	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1080	            undoStack: [...project.undoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1081	            redoStack: []
1082	          }));
1083	        }
1084	      };
1085	    },
1086	    {
1087	      name: 'kintting-design-project',
1088	      storage: createJSONStorage(() => createDebouncedForageStorage(DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS), {
1089	        replacer: storageReplacer,
1090	        reviver: storageReviver,
1091	      }),
1092	      version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
1093	      partialize: (state) => ({
1094	        projects: state.projects,
1095	        deletedProjects: state.deletedProjects,
1096	        activeProjectId: state.activeProjectId,
1097	      }),
1098	      merge: (persistedState: any, currentState) => {
1099	        const merged = { ...currentState, ...(persistedState ?? {}) };
1100	        const activeProject = merged.activeProjectId ? merged.projects?.[merged.activeProjectId] : null;
1101	        return {
1102	          ...merged,
1103	          deletedProjects: merged.deletedProjects ?? {},
1104	          ...(activeProject ? projectView(activeProject) : emptyProjectView()),
1105	          clipboard: null,
1106	          validationResults: [],
1107	        };
1108	      },
1109	      migrate: (persistedState: any, version: number) => {
1110	        if (!persistedState || Object.keys(persistedState).length === 0) {
1111	          return {
1112	            projects: {},
1113	            deletedProjects: {},
1114	            activeProjectId: null,
1115	            clipboard: null,
1116	            validationResults: [],
1117	          };
1118	        }
1119	
1120	        if (version === 0 || typeof persistedState.version !== 'number') {
1121	          if (persistedState.projects && typeof persistedState.projects === 'object') {
1122	            const migratedProjects = Object.fromEntries(
1123	              Object.entries(persistedState.projects).map(([id, project]) => [id, normalizeProject(project)])
1124	            );
1125	
1126	            return {
1127	              projects: migratedProjects,
1128	              deletedProjects: {},
1129	              activeProjectId: persistedState.activeProjectId in migratedProjects ? persistedState.activeProjectId : Object.keys(migratedProjects)[0] ?? null,
1130	              clipboard: null,
1131	              validationResults: [],
1132	            };
1133	          }
1134	
1135	          const id = crypto.randomUUID();
1136	          const grids = persistedState.grids || { knit: [], crochet: [] };
1137	          const currentMode = persistedState.currentMode === 'crochet' ? 'crochet' : 'knit';
1138	
1139	          return {
1140	            projects: {
1141	              [id]: {
1142	                id,
1143	                name: 'Migrated Project',
1144	                lastModified: Date.now(),
1145	                deletedAt: undefined,
1146	                thumbnail: undefined,
1147	                version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
1148	                grids,
1149	                currentMode,
1150	                description: '',
1151	                textLocale: 'abbr' as TextLocale,
1152	                rowNumberDirection: 'row1_top' as RowNumberDirection,
1153	                undoStack: [],
1154	                redoStack: [],
1155	              }
1156	            },
1157	            deletedProjects: {},
1158	            activeProjectId: id,
1159	            clipboard: null,
1160	            validationResults: [],
1161	          };
1162	        }
1163	
1164	        if (version < CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION) {
1165	          if (persistedState.projects && typeof persistedState.projects === 'object') {
1166	            const upgradedProjects = Object.fromEntries(
1167	              Object.entries(persistedState.projects).map(([id, project]) => [id, normalizeProject(project)])
1168	            );
1169	
1170	            return {
1171	              projects: upgradedProjects,
1172	              deletedProjects: {},
1173	              activeProjectId: persistedState.activeProjectId in upgradedProjects ? persistedState.activeProjectId : Object.keys(upgradedProjects)[0] ?? null,
1174	              clipboard: null,
1175	              validationResults: [],
1176	            };
1177	          }
1178	        }
1179	
1180	        return persistedState;
1181	      },
1182	    }
1183	  )
1184	);
1185	
```

```json
318	      rows: Math.max(0, Math.round((parseGaugeValue(gaugeForm.rowsPerTenCm) / 10) * parseGaugeValue(gaugeForm.targetHeightCm))),

322	
323	  const applyGaugeToProject = () => {
324	    const nextCols = Math.max(12, gaugeTotals.stitches);
325	    const nextRows = Math.max(12, gaugeTotals.rows);
326	    initGrid(nextRows, nextCols);
327	    clearSelection();
328	    setCalculatorOpen(false);
329	    setNotice(`针数换算已应用，项目尺寸更新为 ${nextCols} 列 x ${nextRows} 行。`);
330	  };
331	
332	  const handleCreateProject = () => {
333	    const name = window.prompt('项目名称', `Project ${projectList.length + 1}`);
334	    if (!name?.trim()) {
335	      return;
336	    }
337	
338	    createProject(name.trim(), DEFAULT_GRID_ROWS, DEFAULT_GRID_COLS);
339	    clearSelection();
340	    setScale(1);
341	    setIsProjectPanelOpen(false);
342	    setNotice(`已创建项目：${name.trim()}`);
343	  };
344	
345	  const handleRenameProject = () => {
346	    if (!activeProject) {
347	      return;
348	    }
349	
350	    const name = window.prompt('重命名项目', activeProject.name);
351	    if (!name?.trim()) {
352	      return;
353	    }
354	
355	    renameProject(activeProject.id, name.trim());
356	    setNotice(`项目已重命名为：${name.trim()}`);
357	  };
358	
359	  const handleDuplicateProject = () => {
360	    if (!activeProjectId) {
361	      return;
362	    }
363	
364	    const nextId = duplicateProject(activeProjectId);
365	    if (nextId) {
366	      clearSelection();
367	      setIsProjectPanelOpen(false);
368	      setNotice('项目副本已创建。');
369	    }
370	  };
371	
372	  const handleDeleteProject = (id: string) => {
373	    const project = projects[id];
374	    if (!project || !window.confirm(`删除项目“${project.name}”？`)) {
375	      return;
376	    }
377	
378	    deleteProject(id);
379	    clearSelection();
380	    setNotice(`已删除项目：${project.name}`);
381	  };
382	
383	  const handleSwitchProject = (id: string) => {
384	    switchProject(id);
385	    clearSelection();
386	    setIsProjectPanelOpen(false);
387	    setNotice(`已打开项目：${projects[id]?.name ?? id}`);
388	  };
389	
390	  const applyAiPresetToProject = () => {
391	    const knitPreset = createPresetGrid('knit', 32, 32);
392	    replaceModeGrid('knit', knitPreset);
393	    clearSelection();
394	    setScale(1);
395	    setInteractionMode('DRAW');
396	    setActiveSymbolId('c4f');
397	    setActivePage('workspace');
398	    setNotice('AI 纹样映射已应用到棒针工作区，可继续精修。');
399	  };
400	
401	  const confirmExport = async () => {
402	    if (isExporting) {
403	      return;
404	    }
405	
406	    const presetLabel =
407	      exportPreset === 'professional' ? '商用专业版' : exportPreset === 'draft' ? '交流草稿版' : '社交分享版';
408	    setNotice(`${presetLabel} 导出任务正在进行中，水印内容为“${watermarkText || '未设置'}”。`);
409	    setIsExporting(true);
410	
411	    try {
412	      const snapshot = exportSnapshot();
413	      const pdfBlob = await exportProjectAsPDF(snapshot, {
414	        watermarkText,
415	        scale: 1,
416	      });
417	      const url = URL.createObjectURL(pdfBlob);
418	      const anchor = document.createElement('a');
419	      anchor.href = url;
420	      anchor.download = 'mykintting-design.pdf';
421	      document.body.appendChild(anchor);
422	      anchor.click();
423	      document.body.removeChild(anchor);
424	      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
425	      setNotice(`导出完成：已生成 PDF 并自动下载，水印“${watermarkText || '未设置'}”。`);
426	    } catch (error: any) {
427	      setNotice(`导出失败：${error?.message ?? '未知错误'}`);
428	    } finally {
429	      setIsExporting(false);
430	    }
431	  };
432	
433	  const renderSymbolRail = (symbols: StitchDefinition[]) => (
434	    <div className="studio-list">
435	      {symbols.slice(0, 6).map((symbol) => (
436	        <button
437	          key={symbol.id}
438	          type="button"
439	          className={`symbol-button studio-list-item${activeSymbolId === symbol.id ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
440	          onClick={() => handleSymbolPick(symbol.id)}
441	        >
442	          <span className="studio-list-thumb">
443	            <img src={symbol.svgPath} alt={symbol.nameZh} />
444	          </span>
445	          <span className="studio-list-copy">
446	            <strong>{symbol.nameZh}</strong>
447	            <small>{symbol.nameEn ?? (currentMode === 'knit' ? 'Knitting' : 'Crochet')}</small>
448	          </span>
449	        </button>
450	      ))}
451	    </div>
452	  );
453	
454	  const renderWorkspacePage = () => (
455	    <div className="page-stack">
456	      {expiringProjectsCount > 0 && (
457	        <div className="expiration-banner">
458	          <div className="expiration-banner-content">
459	            <span className="expiration-icon">⚠️</span>
460	            <div className="expiration-text">
461	              <strong>注意：{expiringProjectsCount} 个项目即将回收</strong>
462	              <p>最近 7 天未使用的项目将在 10 天后自动移入回收站。请及时查看项目管理面板。</p>
463	            </div>
464	            <button 
465	              type="button" 
466	              className="expiration-action-btn"
467	              onClick={() => setIsProjectPanelOpen(true)}
468	            >
469	              查看项目
470	            </button>
471	          </div>
472	        </div>
473	      )}
474	      <section className="page-hero">
475	        <div>
476	          <div className="text-base font-bold">复杂提花：北极星图案</div>
477	        </div>
478	        <div className="hero-actions">
479	          <span className="hero-pill">Delta: +2</span>
480	          <span className="hero-pill muted">{Math.round(scale * 100)}%</span>

489	            ))}
490	          </div>

494	                <Grid activeSymbolId={activeSymbolId} />
495	              </div>
496	            </div>
497	            <div className="floating-tool-rail">
498	              <button type="button" onClick={() => updateScale(scale + 0.1)}>
499	                +
500	              </button>
501	              <button type="button" onClick={() => updateScale(scale - 0.1)}>
502	                -
503	              </button>
504	              <button type="button" onClick={() => setInteractionMode('SELECT')}>
505	                光标
506	              </button>
507	              <button type="button" onClick={() => setCalculatorOpen(true)}>
508	                换算
509	              </button>
510	            </div>
511	          </div>
512	        </div>
513	
514	        <aside className="workspace-side">
515	          <div className="studio-card compact flush-top">
516	            <div className="studio-card-header">
517	              <div>
518	                <span className="card-kicker">工作台侧栏</span>
519	                <h3>右侧映射面板</h3>
520	              </div>
521	              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
522	                <button
523	                  type="button"
524	                  className="ghost-button"
525	                  onClick={() => {
526	                    const input = window.prompt('设置自动保存间隔（秒）。输入正数，例如 10 表示 10 秒。', String(Math.round(autosaveMs / 1000)));
527	                    if (!input) return;
528	                    const sec = Number(input);
529	                    if (Number.isNaN(sec) || sec <= 0) {
530	                      setNotice('请输入大于 0 的数字。');
531	                      return;
532	                    }
533	                    const ms = Math.round(sec * 1000);
534	                    try {
535	                      window.localStorage.setItem('kintting:autosaveDelayMs', String(ms));
536	                      setAutosaveMs(ms);
537	                      setNotice(`自动保存间隔已设置为 ${sec} 秒。`);
538	                    } catch (e) {
539	                      setNotice('无法保存设置（localStorage 失败）。');
540	                    }
541	                  }}
542	                  title="设置自动保存间隔"
543	                >
544	                  自动保存: {Math.round(autosaveMs / 1000)}s
545	                </button>
546	              </div>
547	            </div>
548	          </div>
549	
550	          <>
551	            {/* Existing right sidebar content */}
552	            <div className="studio-card compact">
553	              <div className="studio-card-header">
554	                <div>
555	                  <span className="card-kicker">当前笔刷</span>
556	                  <h3>{activeSymbol?.nameZh ?? '未选择针法'}</h3>
557	                </div>
558	                <span className="hero-pill muted">{currentMode === 'knit' ? '棒针' : '钩针'}</span>
559	              </div>
560	              <p className="muted-copy">{selectedInfo?.detail ?? '选择任意单元格后，这里会展示当前针法详情。'}</p>
561	              <div className="tool-grid">
562	                {TOOLBAR_TOOLS.map((tool) => (
563	                  <button
564	                    key={tool.id}
565	                    type="button"
566	                    className={`tool-chip${interactionMode === tool.id ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
567	                    data-testid={`tool-${tool.id.toLowerCase()}`}
568	                    onClick={() => setInteractionMode(tool.id)}
569	                  >
570	                    <strong>{tool.short}</strong>
571	                    <span>{tool.label}</span>
572	                  </button>
573	                ))}
574	              </div>
575	              {renderSymbolRail(availableSymbols)}
576	              <div className="studio-range-row">
577	                <label htmlFor="canvas-scale">缩放</label>
578	                <input
579	                  id="canvas-scale"
580	                  type="range"
581	                  min={CANVAS_SCALE_MIN}
582	                  max={CANVAS_SCALE_MAX}
583	                  step={0.05}
584	                  value={scale}
585	                  onChange={(event) => updateScale(Number(event.target.value))}
586	                  aria-label="画布缩放"
587	                />
588	              </div>
589	              <div className="studio-button-row">
590	                <button type="button" className="ghost-button icon-only-button" onClick={undo} disabled={!undoStack.length} aria-label="Undo" title="Undo">
591	                  ↩
592	                </button>
593	                <button type="button" className="ghost-button icon-only-button" onClick={redo} disabled={!redoStack.length} aria-label="Redo" title="Redo">
594	                  ↪
595	                </button>
596	              </div>
597	
598	              <div className="studio-meta-grid">
599	                <span>选择</span>
600	                <strong>{selectedPosition}</strong>
601	                <span>状态</span>
602	                <strong>{previousMode ? `临时 ${interactionMode}` : interactionMode}</strong>
603	              </div>
604	            </div>
605	
606	            <div className="studio-card compact">
607	              <TextEditor />
608	            </div>
609	
610	
611	            <div className="tracker-card">
612	              <span className="card-kicker">进度追踪</span>
613	              <div className="tracker-ring">
614	                <strong>{projectCompletion}%</strong>
615	                <span>已完成</span>
616	              </div>
617	              <div className="tracker-stat">
618	                <strong>
619	                  第 {Math.max(1, Math.ceil(filledCellCount / Math.max(gridCols, 1)))} 行 / 共 {gridRows} 行
620	                </strong>
621	                <span>
622	                  填充 {filledCellCount}/{gridRows * gridCols}
623	                </span>
624	              </div>
625	            </div>
626	          </>
627	        </aside>
628	      </section>
629	    </div>
630	  );

675	                }}

678	              </button>
```

```json
2	
3	export const displayRowNumber = (
4	  arrayRow: number,
5	  totalRows: number,
6	  direction: RowNumberDirection
7	) => (direction === 'row1_top' ? arrayRow + 1 : totalRows - arrayRow);

9	export const gridRowFromDisplayRow = (
10	  rowNumber: number,
11	  totalRows: number,
12	  direction: RowNumberDirection
```

**Output:**

```json
1	import type { languages } from 'monaco-editor';
2	import { stitchRegistry } from '../configs/stitchRegistry';
3	
4	export const KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID = 'knitting-pattern';
5	
6	let registered = false;
7	
8	/**
9	 * Collect all known stitch tokens for auto-completion and highlighting.
10	 * Includes abbreviations, English names, and Chinese names.
11	 */
12	function collectStitchTokens(): { abbrevs: string[]; enNames: string[]; zhNames: string[] } {
13	  const abbrevs: string[] = [];
14	  const enNames: string[] = [];
15	  const zhNames: string[] = [];
16	
17	  for (const def of Object.values(stitchRegistry)) {
18	    if (def.abbrev) abbrevs.push(def.abbrev);
19	    if (def.nameEn) enNames.push(def.nameEn);
20	    if (def.nameZh) zhNames.push(def.nameZh);
21	  }
22	
23	  return { abbrevs, enNames, zhNames };
24	}
25	
26	/**
27	 * Build the Monarch tokenizer grammar for knitting pattern syntax.
28	 *
29	 * Recognized patterns:
30	 *   Row <number>:  — row header (keyword)
31	 *   <number>       — count (number)
32	 *   known abbrev   — stitch token (type)
33	 *   ,  .           — punctuation
34	 *   everything else — plain text
35	 */
36	function buildTokenizer(): languages.IMonarchLanguage {
37	  const { abbrevs, enNames, zhNames } = collectStitchTokens();
38	
39	  // Escape special regex chars in token strings
40	  const escape = (s: string) => s.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
41	
42	  // Build a combined keyword list, longest-first to avoid partial matches
43	  const allKeywords = [...abbrevs, ...enNames, ...zhNames]
44	    .sort((a, b) => b.length - a.length)
45	    .map(escape);
46	
47	  return {
48	    defaultToken: 'source',
49	    keywords: allKeywords,
50	    tokenizer: {
51	      root: [
52	        // Row header: "Row 1:" / "Row 12:"
53	        [/Row\s+(\d+)\s*:/, { token: 'keyword.row-header' }],
54	
55	        // Numbers (stitch counts)
56	        [/\b\d+\b/, 'number'],
57	
58	        // Known stitch tokens (abbreviations, names)
59	        [
60	          new RegExp(`\\b(${allKeywords.join('|')})\\b`),
61	          'type.stitch',
62	        ],
63	
64	        // Chinese stitch names (no word boundary for CJK)
65	        [
66	          new RegExp(`(${zhNames.map(escape).join('|')})`),
67	          'type.stitch',
68	        ],
69	
70	        // Punctuation
71	        [/[,.]/, 'delimiter'],
72	
73	        // Whitespace
74	        [/\s+/, 'white'],
75	      ],
76	    },
77	  };
78	}
79	
80	/**
81	 * Build auto-completion items from the stitch registry.
82	 */
83	function buildCompletionItems(
84	  monaco: typeof import('monaco-editor')
85	): languages.CompletionItem[] {
86	  const items: languages.CompletionItem[] = [];
87	  const seen = new Set<string>();
88	
89	  for (const def of Object.values(stitchRegistry)) {
90	    // Abbreviation completion
91	    if (def.abbrev && !seen.has(def.abbrev)) {
92	      seen.add(def.abbrev);
93	      items.push({
94	        label: def.abbrev,
95	        kind: monaco.languages.CompletionItemKind.Value,
96	        detail: `${def.nameZh} (${def.nameEn ?? def.id})`,
97	        documentation: `针法缩写: ${def.abbrev} → ${def.nameZh}`,
98	        insertText: def.abbrev,
99	      });
100	    }
101	
102	    // English name completion
103	    if (def.nameEn && !seen.has(def.nameEn)) {
104	      seen.add(def.nameEn);
105	      items.push({
106	        label: def.nameEn,
107	        kind: monaco.languages.CompletionItemKind.Value,
108	        detail: `${def.nameZh} [${def.abbrev ?? def.id}]`,
109	        documentation: `${def.nameEn} → ${def.nameZh}`,
110	        insertText: def.nameEn,
111	      });
112	    }
113	
114	    // Chinese name completion
115	    if (def.nameZh && !seen.has(def.nameZh)) {
116	      seen.add(def.nameZh);
117	      items.push({
118	        label: def.nameZh,
119	        kind: monaco.languages.CompletionItemKind.Value,
120	        detail: `${def.nameEn ?? def.id} [${def.abbrev ?? ''}]`,
121	        documentation: `${def.nameZh} → ${def.nameEn ?? def.id}`,
122	        insertText: def.nameZh,
123	      });
124	    }
125	  }
126	
127	  return items;
128	}
129	
130	/**
131	 * Register the knitting-pattern language with Monaco.
132	 * Safe to call multiple times — subsequent calls are no-ops.
133	 */
134	export function registerKnittingLanguage(
135	  monaco: typeof import('monaco-editor')
136	) {
137	  if (registered) return;
138	  registered = true;
139	
140	  // Register language
141	  monaco.languages.register({ id: KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID });
142	
143	  // Set tokenizer
144	  monaco.languages.setMonarchTokensProvider(
145	    KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID,
146	    buildTokenizer()
147	  );
148	
149	  // Register completion provider
150	  monaco.languages.registerCompletionItemProvider(KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID, {
151	    triggerCharacters: [' ', ','],
152	    provideCompletionItems: (model, position) => {
153	      const items = buildCompletionItems(monaco);
154	      const word = model.getWordUntilPosition(position);
155	      const range = {
156	        startLineNumber: position.lineNumber,
157	        endLineNumber: position.lineNumber,
158	        startColumn: word.startColumn,
159	        endColumn: word.endColumn,
160	      };
161	
162	      return {
163	        suggestions: items.map((item) => ({ ...item, range })),
164	      };
165	    },
166	  });
167	
168	  // Define a light theme tailored for knitting patterns
169	  monaco.editor.defineTheme('knitting-light', {
170	    base: 'vs',
171	    inherit: true,
172	    rules: [
173	      { token: 'keyword.row-header', foreground: '8D0B0B', fontStyle: 'bold' },
174	      { token: 'number', foreground: 'B4654A' },
175	      { token: 'type.stitch', foreground: '2E6B4F', fontStyle: 'bold' },
176	      { token: 'delimiter', foreground: '999999' },
177	    ],
178	    colors: {
179	      'editor.background': '#FFF9F5',
180	      'editor.foreground': '#4A3228',
181	      'editorLineNumber.foreground': '#C4A882',
182	      'editorLineNumber.activeForeground': '
```

#### Thinking

All done. Let me summarize what was accomplished.

双向编译引擎的第一阶段已经完成，所有改动已通过构建和测试验证。以下是本次实现的总结：

**新增文件：**

- `src/components/KnittingEditor/knittingLanguage.ts` — 自定义 Monaco 语言定义，包含编织语法的 Monarch 语法高亮（Row 头部、针数、针法缩写/名称分别着色）和基于 stitchRegistry 的自动补全（支持缩写、英文名、中文名三种输入方式）

- `src/components/KnittingEditor/DraggablePanel.tsx` — 可拖拽、可缩放的浮动面板，支持通过标题栏拖动、右下角缩放，位置和尺寸自动持久化到 localStorage

- `src/components/KnittingEditor/KnittingEditor.tsx` — 核心编辑器组件，实现了完整的双向同步逻辑：
  - **图解→文字**：画布变化时自动编译为文字并同步到编辑器（保持原有逻辑不变）
  - **文字→图解**：用户编辑文字后，点击 "Apply" 按钮或按 Ctrl+Enter 触发 `applyTextToGrid`，将解析结果回写到画布
  - 校验反馈：解析后在编辑器中显示错误/信息标记，底部列出每行的校验状态
  - 语言/方向切换工具栏，Reset 按钮可丢弃修改恢复为画布编译结果

- `src/components/KnittingEditor/knitting-editor.css` — 编辑器与浮动面板的完整样式

**修改文件：**

- `App.tsx` — 导入新组件，添加 `isEditorPanelOpen` 状态，在浮动工具栏新增"编辑器"按钮，在页面底部渲染 DraggablePanel + KnittingEditor

**未改动的核心逻辑：** `translator.ts` 中的 `compileGridToText` 和 `parseTextToGrid` 完全保持原样，符合你的要求。

```json
927	          if (!activeProjectId) return [];

935

939

941	            if (text.trim() === '') {

944	              get().compileToText();

953	            if (pRow.validation.delta > 0) {
954	              maxColsFromText = Math.max(maxColsFromText, colsInGrid + pRow.validation.delta);
955	            }
956	          });
957	
958	          let newGrid = createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText);
959	    
960	          if (rowsInGrid === 0 || text.trim() === '') {

966	          parsedRows.forEach((parsed: any) => {
967	            const gridRowIndex = gridRowFromDisplayRow(parsed.rowNumber, rowsInGrid, project.rowNumberDirection);
968	            if (gridRowIndex >= 0 && gridRowIndex < rowsInGrid) {
969	              const isEvenRow = parsed.rowNumber % 2 === 0;
970	              let currentCol = isEvenRow ? 0 : maxColsFromText - 1;
971	
972	              for (const cell of parsed.cells) {
973	                const stitchId = cell.stitchId!;
974	                const spanW = stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.span?.width || 1;
975	                const dir = isEvenRow ? 1 : -1;
976	
977	                const endCol = currentCol + dir * (spanW - 1);
978	                if (dir === 1 && endCol >= maxColsFromText) continue; 
979	                if (dir === -1 && endCol < 0) continue; 
980	
981	                if (currentCol >= 0 && currentCol < maxColsFromText) {
982	                  newGrid[gridRowIndex][currentCol] = {

985	                    isSpanChild: false,

988	                }
```

#### Thinking

Now I can see the bug clearly. At line 958, `createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText)` creates a completely empty grid, then only the parsed rows from the text are filled in (lines 966-1005). Any rows not mentioned in the text input remain empty.

The fix should:
1. Clone the existing grid data into `newGrid` instead of creating an empty grid
2. Only overwrite the rows that are present in the parsed text

#### Thinking

`cloneGrid` exists at line 171. Now I need to fix the `applyTextToGrid` function. The fix is:

1. Instead of `createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText)`, clone the existing grid
2. But we also need to handle column width changes — if the text requires more columns than the current grid, we need to expand; if fewer, we should keep the existing width (or adjust)

Actually, looking more carefully, the approach should be:
- Clone the existing grid (preserving all rows)
- If `maxColsFromText` differs from `colsInGrid`, we need to resize (similar to `resizeGrid` logic)


- Then only overwrite the rows that were parsed from the text

The simplest fix is to clone the current grid first, handle any column width adjustments, and then selectively update only the rows that came from the parsed text.

Now I'm working through the column width logic — if the text requires more columns than the grid currently has, I need to expand all rows to that width. If it needs fewer columns, I should probably keep the existing grid width since the user might just be editing a subset of rows. The key is making sure the new grid can accommodate both the existing data and what's being parsed from the text.

Writing the grid update logic... I'm realizing the logic can be streamlined—the key insight is that I should always preserve the existing grid width unless the parsed text explicitly requires more columns, and I can handle both cloning and resizing in one pass rather than as separate steps.

#### Thinking

The fix is complete. Let me summarize what was done for the user.

问题已修复。根本原因在 `projectStore.ts` 的 `applyTextToGrid` 函数中，之前用 `createEmptyGrid()` 创建了一个全新的空网格，然后只填充文本中提到的行，导致其他行全部丢失。

修改后的逻辑是：先用 `cloneGrid(currentGrid)` 克隆现有网格（保留所有行数据），再只覆盖文本中出现的行。如果文本需要的列数比当前网格多，才会扩展列宽。这样你只编辑 Row 1 时，Row 2、3、4 等都不会受影响。

你可以重新测试一下——在编辑器里只修改某一行的内容然后 Apply，其他行应该保持不变了。

```json
34	  const [editorText, setEditorText] = useState(compiledText);
35	  const [isDirty, setIsDirty] = useState(false);
36	  const [validationResults, setValidationResults] = useState<ValidationInfo[]>([]);
37	  const [lastAppliedText, setLastAppliedText] = useState('');
38	
39	  const editorRef = useRef<editor.IStandaloneCodeEditor | null>(null);
40	  const monacoRef = useRef<typeof import('monaco-editor') | null>(null);
41	
42	  // Sync grid -> editor when compiled text changes externally
43	  // Only sync if user hasn't made local edits
44	  useEffect(() => {
45	    if (!isDirty && compiledText !== editorText) {
46	      setEditorText(compiledText);
47	    }
48	  }, [compiledText, isDirty, editorText]);
49	
50	  const handleEditorMount: OnMount = useCallback((editorInstance, monaco) => {
51	    editorRef.current = editorInstance;
52	    monacoRef.current = monaco;
53	
54	    // Register our custom language
55	    registerKnittingLanguage(monaco);
56	
57	    // Set language
58	    const model = editorInstance.getModel();
59	    if (model) {
60	      monaco.editor.setModelLanguage(model, KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID);
61	    }
62	
63	    // Focus editor for immediate typing
64	    editorInstance.focus();
65	  }, []);
66	
67	  const handleEditorChange = useCallback((value: string | undefined) => {
68	    const newText = value ?? '';
69	    setEditorText(newText);
70	    setIsDirty(newText !== compiledText);
71	
72	    // Clear validation markers when editing
73	    if (monacoRef.current && editorRef.current) {
74	      const model = editorRef.current.getModel();
75	      if (model) {
76	        monacoRef.current.editor.setModelMarkers(model, 'knitting-validation', []);
77	      }
78	    }
79	    setValidationResults([]);
80	  }, [compiledText]);
81	
82	  // Apply text -> grid
83	  const handleApply = useCallback(() => {
84	    if (!editorText.trim()) {
85	      setValidationResults([]);
86	      setIsDirty(false);
87	      return;
88	    }
89	
90	    const parsed = applyTextToGrid(editorText);
91	
92	    // Build validation markers
93	    const markers: ValidationInfo[] = [];
94	    const monacoMarkers: editor.IMarkerData[] = [];
95	
96	    parsed.forEach((row) => {
97	      if (!row.validation.valid || row.validation.delta !== 0) {
98	        const severity = row.validation.valid ? 'info' : 'error';
99	        markers.push({
100	          line: row.rowNumber,
101	          severity,
102	          message: row.validation.message,
103	        });
104	
105	        if (monacoRef.current && editorRef.current) {
106	          const model = editorRef.current.getModel();
107	          if (model) {
108	            const lineContent = model.getLineContent(row.rowNumber) || '';
109	            monacoMarkers.push({
110	              severity: severity === 'error'
111	                ? (monacoRef.current.MarkerSeverity.Error as number)
112	                : (monacoRef.current.MarkerSeverity.Info as number),
113	              message: row.validation.message,
114	              startLineNumber: row.rowNumber,
115	              startColumn: 1,
116	              endLineNumber: row.rowNumber,
117	              endColumn: Math.max(lineContent.length + 1, 2),
118	            });
119	          }
120	        }
121	      }
122	    });
123	
124	    setValidationResults(markers);
125	
126	    // Set Monaco markers
127	    if (monacoRef.current && editorRef.current && monacoMarkers.length > 0) {
128	      const model = editorRef.current.getModel();
129	      if (model) {
130	        monacoRef.current.editor.setModelMarkers(model, 'knitting-validation', monacoMarkers);
131	      }
132	    }
133	
134	    // After applying, sync the editor with freshly compiled text
135	    setLastAppliedText(editorText);
136	    setIsDirty(false);
137	  }, [editorText, applyTextToGrid]);
138	
139	  // Reset editor to compiled text (discard changes)
140	  const handleReset = useCallback(() => {
141	    setEditorText(compiledText);
142	    setIsDirty(false);
143	    setValidationResults([]);
144	
145	    if (monacoRef.current && editorRef.current) {
146	      const model = editorRef.current.getModel();
147	      if (model) {
148	        monacoRef.current.editor.setModelMarkers(model, 'knitting-validation', []);
149	      }
150	    }
151	  }, [compiledText]);
152	
153	  // Sync from editor to grid (Ctrl+Enter shortcut)
154	  useEffect(() => {
155	    const editorInstance = editorRef.current;
156	    if (!editorInstance) return;
157	
158	    const disposable = editorInstance.addAction({
159	      id: 'apply-to-grid',
160	      label: 'Apply text to grid',
161	      keybindings: [2048 | 3], // Ctrl+Enter
162	      run: () => {
163	        handleApply();
164	      },
165	    });
166	
167	    return () => disposable.dispose();
168	  }, [handleApply]);
169	
170	  const errorCount = validationResults.filter(v => v.severity === 'error').length;
171	  const warningCount = validationResults.filter(v => v.severity === 'info').length;
172	
173	  const LOCALES: Array<{ id: TextLocale; label: string }> = [
174	    { id: 'abbr', label: 'Abbr' },
175	    { id: 'en', label: 'EN' },
176	    { id: 'zh', label: '中文' },
177	  ];
178	
179	  return (
180	    <div className="knitting-editor-root">
181	      {/* Toolbar */}
182	      <div className="knitting-editor-toolbar">
183	        <div className="knitting-editor-locale-group">
184	          {LOCALES.map((locale) => (
185	            <button
186	              key={locale.id}
187	              type="button"
188	              className={`knitting-locale-btn${textLocale === locale.id ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
189	              onClick={() => {
190	                setTextLocale(locale.id);
191	                // After locale change, recompile and update editor
192	                setTimeout(() => {
193	                  setEditorText(
194	                    compileGridToText(currentGrid, { locale: locale.id, rowNumberDirection })
195	                  );
196	                  setIsDirty(false);
197	                }, 0);
198	              }}
199	            >
200	              {locale.label}
201	            </button>
202	          ))}
203	        </div>
204	
205	        <div className="knitting-editor-direction-group">
206	          <button
207	            type="button"
208	            className={`knitting-locale-btn${rowNumberDirection === 'row1_top' ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
209	            onClick={() => {
210	              setRowNumberDirection('row1_top');
211	              setTimeout(() => {
212	                setEditorText(
213	                  compileGridToText(currentGrid, { locale: textLocale, rowNumberDirection: 'row1_top' })
214	                );
215	                setIsDirty(false);
216	              }, 0);
217	            }}
218	          >
219	            Row 1 顶
220	          </button>
221	          <button
222	            type="button"
223	            className={`knitting-locale-btn${rowNumberDirection === 'row1_bottom' ? ' is-active' : ''}`}
224	            onClick={() => {
225	              setRowNumberDirection('row1_bottom');
226	              setTimeout(() => {
227	                setEditorText(
228	                  compileGridToText(currentGrid, { locale: textLocale, rowNumberDirection: 'row1_bottom' })
229	                );
230	                setIsDirty(false);
231	              }, 0);
232	            }}
233	          >
234	            Row 1 底
235	          </button>
236	        </div>
237	
238	        <div className="knitting-editor-actions">
239	          <button
240	            type="button"
241	            className="knitting-apply-btn"
242	            onClick={handleApply}
243	            disabled={!isDirty && !editorText.trim()}
244	            title="Apply text to grid (Ctrl+Enter)"
245	          >
246	            Apply
247	          </button>
248	          <button
249	            type="button"
250	            className="knitting-reset-btn"
251	            onClick={handleReset}
252	            disabled={!isDirty}
253	            title="Discard changes and reload from grid"
254	          >
255	            Reset
256	          </button>
257	        </div>
258	      </div>
259	
260	      {/* Validation status bar */}
261	      {(errorCount > 0 || warningCount > 0) && (
262	        <div className="knitting-editor-status">
263	          {errorCount > 0 && (
264	            <span className="validation-error">{errorCount} error(s)</span>
265	          )}
266	          {warningCount > 0 && (
267	            <span className="validation-info">{warningCount} info(s)</span>
268	          )}
269	          {isDirty && <span className="dirty-indicator">Unsaved changes</span>}
270	        </div>
271	      )}
272	
273	      {/* Monaco Editor */}
274	      <div className="knitting-editor-monaco-wrap">
275	        <Editor
276	          height="100%"
277	          language={KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID}
278	          theme="knitting-light"
279	          value={editorText}
280	          onChange={handleEditorChange}
281	          onMount={handleEditorMount}
282	          options={{
283	            minimap: { enabled: false },
284	            fontSize: 13,
285	            fontFamily: '"Consolas", "Monaco", "Courier New", monospace',
286	            lineNumbers: 'on',
287	            scrollBeyondLastLine: false,
288	            wordWrap: 'on',
289	            automaticLayout: true,
290	            padding: { top: 8, bottom: 8 },
291	            renderLineHighlight: 'line',
292	            scrollbar: {
293	              verticalScrollbarSize: 8,
294	              horizontalScrollbarSize: 8,
295	            },
296	            suggest: {
297	              showWords: false,
298	            },
299	            tabCompletion: 'on',
300	            formatOnType: true,
301	          }}
302	        />
303	      </div>
304	
305	      {/* Validation list */}
306	      {validationResults.length > 0 && (
307	        <div className="knitting-editor-validation-list">
308	          {validationResults.map((v, i) => (
309	            <div
310	              key={i}
311	              className={`validation-item validation-${v.severity}`}
312	            >
313	              <span className="validation-row">Row {v.line}</span>
314	              <span className="validation-msg">{v.message}</span>
315	            </div>
316	          ))}
317	        </div>
318	      )}
319	
320	      {/* Footer hint */}
321	      <div className="knitting-editor-footer">
322	        <span>Ctrl+Enter to apply</span>
323	        <span>{colsInGrid} cols</span>
324	      </div>
325	    </div>
326	  );
327	};
328	
```

```json
1	import type { languages } from 'monaco-editor';
2	import { stitchRegistry } from '../../configs/stitchRegistry';
3	
4	export const KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID = 'knitting-pattern';
5	
6	let registered = false;
7	
8	function collectStitchTokens(): { abbrevs: string[]; enNames: string[]; zhNames: string[] } {
9	  const abbrevs: string[] = [];
10	  const enNames: string[] = [];
11	  const zhNames: string[] = [];
12	
13	  for (const def of Object.values(stitchRegistry)) {
14	    if (def.abbrev) abbrevs.push(def.abbrev);
15	    if (def.nameEn) enNames.push(def.nameEn);
16	    if (def.nameZh) zhNames.push(def.nameZh);
17	  }
18	
19	  return { abbrevs, enNames, zhNames };
20	}
21	
22	function buildTokenizer(): languages.IMonarchLanguage {
23	  const { abbrevs, enNames, zhNames } = collectStitchTokens();
24	  const escape = (s: string) => s.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
25	
26	  const allKeywords = [...abbrevs, ...enNames, ...zhNames]
27	    .sort((a, b) => b.length - a.length)
28	    .map(escape);
29	
30	  return {
31	    defaultToken: 'source',
32	    keywords: allKeywords,
33	    tokenizer: {
34	      root: [
35	        [/Row\s+(\d+)\s*:/, { token: 'keyword.row-header' }],
36	        [/\b\d+\b/, 'number'],
37	        [new RegExp(`\\b(${allKeywords.join('|')})\\b`), 'type.stitch'],
38	        [new RegExp(`(${zhNames.map(escape).join('|')})`), 'type.stitch'],
39	        [/[,.]/, 'delimiter'],
40	        [/\s+/, 'white'],
41	      ],
42	    },
43	  };
44	}
45	
46	function buildCompletionItems(
47	  monaco: typeof import('monaco-editor')
48	): languages.CompletionItem[] {
49	  const items: languages.CompletionItem[] = [];
50	  const seen = new Set<string>();
51	
52	  for (const def of Object.values(stitchRegistry)) {
53	    if (def.abbrev && !seen.has(def.abbrev)) {
54	      seen.add(def.abbrev);
55	      items.push({
56	        label: def.abbrev,
57	        kind: monaco.languages.CompletionItemKind.Value,
58	        detail: `${def.nameZh} (${def.nameEn ?? def.id})`,
59	        documentation: `${def.abbrev} - ${def.nameZh}`,
60	        insertText: def.abbrev,
61	      });
62	    }
63	
64	    if (def.nameEn && !seen.has(def.nameEn)) {
65	      seen.add(def.nameEn);
66	      items.push({
67	        label: def.nameEn,
68	        kind: monaco.languages.CompletionItemKind.Value,
69	        detail: `${def.nameZh} [${def.abbrev ?? def.id}]`,
70	        documentation: `${def.nameEn} - ${def.nameZh}`,
71	        insertText: def.nameEn,
72	      });
73	    }
74	
75	    if (def.nameZh && !seen.has(def.nameZh)) {
76	      seen.add(def.nameZh);
77	      items.push({
78	        label: def.nameZh,
79	        kind: monaco.languages.CompletionItemKind.Value,
80	        detail: `${def.nameEn ?? def.id} [${def.abbrev ?? ''}]`,
81	        documentation: `${def.nameZh} - ${def.nameEn ?? def.id}`,
82	        insertText: def.nameZh,
83	      });
84	    }
85	  }
86	
87	  return items;
88	}
89	
90	export function registerKnittingLanguage(
91	  monaco: typeof import('monaco-editor')
92	) {
93	  if (registered) return;
94	  registered = true;
95	
96	  monaco.languages.register({ id: KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID });
97	
98	  monaco.languages.setMonarchTokensProvider(
99	    KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID,
100	    buildTokenizer()
101	  );
102	
103	  monaco.languages.registerCompletionItemProvider(KNITTING_LANGUAGE_ID, {
104	    triggerCharacters: [' ', ','],
105	    provideCompletionItems: (model, position) => {
106	      const items = buildCompletionItems(monaco);
107	      const word = model.getWordUntilPosition(position);
108	      const range = {
109	        startLineNumber: position.lineNumber,
110	        endLineNumber: position.lineNumber,
111	        startColumn: word.startColumn,
112	        endColumn: word.endColumn,
113	      };
114	
115	      return {
116	        suggestions: items.map((item) => ({ ...item, range })),
117	      };
118	    },
119	  });
120	
121	  monaco.editor.defineTheme('knitting-light', {
122	    base: 'vs',
123	    inherit: true,
124	    rules: [
125	      { token: 'keyword.row-header', foreground: '8D0B0B', fontStyle: 'bold' },
126	      { token: 'number', foreground: 'B4654A' },
127	      { token: 'type.stitch', foreground: '2E6B4F', fontStyle: 'bold' },
128	      { token: 'delimiter', foreground: '999999' },
129	    ],
130	    colors: {
131	      'editor.background': '#FFF9F5',
132	      'editor.foreground': '#4A3228',
133	      'editorLineNumber.foreground': '#C4A882',
134	      'editorLineNumber.activeForeground': '#8D0B0B',
135	      'editorCursor.foreground': '#8D0B0B',
136	      'editor.selectionBackground': '#F0D9C8',
137	      'editor.lineHighlightBackground': '#FFF0E6',
138	    },
139	  });
140	}
141
```
