```json
12	  bg?: string;
13	  svgPath?: string;
14	  stitchId?: string; 
15	  isSpanChild?: boolean; 
16	  parentPos?: { row: number; col: number }; 
17	};
18	
19	export interface Snapshot {
20	  grids: { knit: CellData[][]; crochet: CellData[][] };
21	  currentMode: 'knit' | 'crochet';
22	  description?: string;
23	}
24	
25	export interface ClipboardItem {
26	  dr: number;
27	  dc: number;
28	  cellSnapshot: CellData;
29	}
30	
31	export interface ProjectClipboard {
32	  anchor: { row: number; col: number };
33	  items: ClipboardItem[];
34	}
35	
36	export interface Project {
37	  id: string;
38	  name: string;
39	  lastModified: number;
40	  deletedAt?: number;
41	  thumbnail?: string; 
42	  version: number;
43	  grids: { knit: CellData[][]; crochet: CellData[][] };
44	  currentMode: 'knit' | 'crochet';
45	  undoStack: Snapshot[];
46	  redoStack: Snapshot[];
47	  description: string;
48	  textLocale: TextLocale;
49	  rowNumberDirection: RowNumberDirection;
50	}
51	
52	interface ProjectState {
53	  projects: Record<string, Project>;
54	  deletedProjects: Record<string, Project>;
55	  activeProjectId: string | null;
56	
57	  grids: { knit: CellData[][]; crochet: CellData[][] };
58	  currentMode: 'knit' | 'crochet';
59	  description: string;
60	  textLocale: TextLocale;
61	  rowNumberDirection: RowNumberDirection;
62	  undoStack: Snapshot[];
63	  redoStack: Snapshot[];
64	
65	  clipboard: ProjectClipboard | null;
66	  validationResults: ParsedRowResult[];
67	
68	  createProject: (name: string, rows?: number, cols?: number) => string;
69	  switchProject: (id: string) => void;
70	  deleteProject: (id: string) => void;
71	  renameProject: (id: string, name: string) => void;
72	  duplicateProject: (id: string) => string | null;
73	  updateProjectThumbnail: (id: string, thumbnail: string) => void;
74	  restoreProject: (id: string) => void;
75	  deleteProjectPermanently: (id: string) => void;
76	  emptyRecycleBin: () => void;
77	  purgeExpiredProjects: () => void;
78	  replaceModeGrid: (mode: 'knit' | 'crochet', grid: CellData[][], resetHistory?: boolean) => void;
79	
80	  setMode: (mode: 'knit' | 'crochet') => void;
81	  setTextLocale: (locale: TextLocale) => void;
82	  setRowNumberDirection: (direction: RowNumberDirection) => void;
83	  initGrid: (rows: number, cols: number) => void;
84	  applyCellChange: (row: number, col: number, char: string, svgPath?: string, stitchId?: string) => boolean;
85	  copySelection: (roots: Array<{ row: number; col: number }>, anchor: { row: number; col: number } | null) => boolean;
86	  cutSelection: (roots: Array<{ row: number; col: number }>, anchor: { row: number; col: number } | null) => boolean;
87	  pasteClipboard: (target: { row: number; col: number }) => Array<{ row: number; col: number }> | null;
88	  moveSelection: (
89	    roots: Array<{ row: number; col: number }>,
90	    anchor: { row: number; col: number },
91	    target: { row: number; col: number }
92	  ) => Array<{ row: number; col: number }> | null;
93	  
94	  compileToText: () => void;
95	  applyTextToGrid: (text: string) => ParsedRowResult[];
96	  
97	  resizeGrid: (newCols: number) => void;
98	  exportSnapshot: () => ExportSnapshot;
99	
100	  undo: () => void;
101	  redo: () => void;
102	  _saveSnapshot: () => void;
103	}
104	
105	const DAY_MS = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
106	const EXPIRY_SOFT_DELETE_MS = 10 * DAY_MS;
107	const CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION = 1;
108	
109	const normalizeTextLocale = (value: unknown): TextLocale =>
110	  value === 'en' || value === 'zh' || value === 'abbr' ? value : 'abbr';
111	
112	const normalizeRowNumberDirection = (value: unknown): RowNumberDirection =>
113	  value === 'row1_top' || value === 'row1_bottom' ? value : 'row1_top';
114	
115	const createEmptyGrid = (rows: number, cols: number) => 
116	  Array.from({ length: rows }, () => Array.from({ length: cols }, () => ({})));
117	
118	const emptyProjectView = () => ({
119	  grids: { knit: [] as CellData[][], crochet: [] as CellData[][] },
120	  currentMode: 'knit' as const,
121	  description: '',
122	  textLocale: 'abbr' as TextLocale,
123	  rowNumberDirection: 'row1_top' as RowNumberDirection,
124	  undoStack: [] as Snapshot[],
125	  redoStack: [] as Snapshot[],
126	});
127	
128	const createProjectRecord = (name: string, rows: number, cols: number): Project => ({
129	  id: crypto.randomUUID(),
130	  name: name.trim() || 'Untitled Project',
131	  lastModified: Date.now(),
132	  deletedAt: undefined,
133	  thumbnail: undefined,
134	  version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
135	  grids: { knit: createEmptyGrid(rows, cols), crochet: createEmptyGrid(rows, cols) },
136	  currentMode: 'knit',
137	  description: '',
138	  textLocale: 'abbr',
139	  rowNumberDirection: 'row1_top',
140	  undoStack: [],
141	  redoStack: [],
142	});
143	
144	const projectView = (project: Project) => ({
145	  grids: project.grids,
146	  currentMode: project.currentMode,
147	  description: project.description,
148	  textLocale: project.textLocale,
149	  rowNumberDirection: project.rowNumberDirection,
150	  undoStack: project.undoStack,
151	  redoStack: project.redoStack,
152	});
153	
154	const cloneProject = (project: Project, name: string): Project => ({
155	  ...project,
156	  id: crypto.randomUUID(),
157	  name,
158	  lastModified: Date.now(),
159	  deletedAt: undefined,
160	  version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
161	  grids: {
162	    knit: cloneGrid(project.grids.knit),
163	    crochet: cloneGrid(project.grids.crochet),
164	  },
165	  undoStack: [],
166	  redoStack: [],
167	});
168	
169	const rootKey = (row: number, col: number) => `${row},${col}`;
170	
171	const cloneGrid = (grid: CellData[][]) => grid.map((row) => row.map((cell) => ({ ...cell, parentPos: cell.parentPos ? { ...cell.parentPos } : undefined })));
172	
173	const isPlainObject = (value: unknown): value is Record<string, unknown> =>
174	  typeof value === 'object' && value !== null && !Array.isArray(value);
175	
176	const storageReplacer = (_key: string, value: unknown) => {
177	  if (value instanceof Map) {
178	    return { __type: 'Map', value: Array.from(value.entries()) };
179	  }
180	  if (value instanceof Set) {
181	    return { __type: 'Set', value: Array.from(value.values()) };
182	  }
183	  if (value instanceof Date) {
184	    return { __type: 'Date', value: value.toISOString() };
185	  }
186	  return value;
187	};
188	
189	const storageReviver = (_key: string, value: unknown) => {
190	  if (!isPlainObject(value) || typeof value.__type !== 'string') {
191	    return value;
192	  }
193	
194	  switch (value.__type) {
195	    case 'Map':
196	      return new Map(value.value as Array<[unknown, unknown]>);
197	    case 'Set':
198	      return new Set(value.value as Array<unknown>);
199	    case 'Date':
200	      return new Date(value.value as string);
201	    default:
202	      return value;
203	  }
204	};
205	
206	const normalizeProject = (project: any): Project => ({
207	  id: typeof project.id === 'string' ? project.id : crypto.randomUUID(),
208	  name: typeof project.name === 'string' ? project.name : 'Untitled Project',
209	  lastModified: typeof project.lastModified === 'number' ? project.lastModified : Date.now(),
210	  thumbnail: typeof project.thumbnail === 'string' ? project.thumbnail : undefined,
211	  version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
212	  grids:
213	    project?.grids && typeof project.grids === 'object'
214	      ? {
215	          knit: Array.isArray(project.grids.knit) ? project.grids.knit : [],
216	          crochet: Array.isArray(project.grids.crochet) ? project.grids.crochet : [],
217	        }
218	      : { knit: [], crochet: [] },
219	  currentMode: project.currentMode === 'crochet' ? 'crochet' : 'knit',
220	  description: typeof project.description === 'string' ? project.description : '',
221	  textLocale: normalizeTextLocale(project.textLocale),
222	  rowNumberDirection: normalizeRowNumberDirection(project.rowNumberDirection),
223	  undoStack: Array.isArray(project.undoStack) ? project.undoStack : [],
224	  redoStack: Array.isArray(project.redoStack) ? project.redoStack : [],
225	});
226	
227	const getRootPosition = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number) => {
228	  const cell = grid[row]?.[col];
229	  if (!cell) return null;
230	  if (cell.isSpanChild && cell.parentPos) return cell.parentPos;
231	  return { row, col };
232	};
233	
234	const clearStitchAtRoot = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number) => {
235	  const root = getRootPosition(grid, row, col);
236	  if (!root) return false;
237	  const cell = grid[root.row]?.[root.col];
238	  if (!cell?.stitchId) return false;
239	
240	  const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
241	  const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
242	  const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
243	  let changed = false;
244	
245	  for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
246	    for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
247	      const target = grid[root.row + i]?.[root.col + j];
248	      if (target) {
249	        grid[root.row + i][root.col + j] = {};
250	        changed = true;
251	      }
252	    }
253	  }
254	
255	  return changed;
256	};
257	
258	const placeStitchSnapshot = (grid: CellData[][], row: number, col: number, snapshot: CellData) => {
259	  if (!snapshot.stitchId) return false;
260	  const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[snapshot.stitchId];
261	  const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
262	  const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
263	
264	  if (row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > grid.length || col + spanW > (grid[0]?.length ?? 0)) {
265	    return false;
266	  }
267	
268	  for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
269	    for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
270	      if (i === 0 && j === 0) {
271	        grid[row][col] = {
272	          ...snapshot,
273	          isSpanChild: false,
274	          parentPos: undefined,
275	          svgPath: snapshot.svgPath || stitchDef?.svgPath || '',
276	        };
277	      } else {
278	        grid[row + i][col + j] = {
279	          char: '',
280	          svgPath: '',
281	          stitchId: snapshot.stitchId,
282	          isSpanChild: true,
283	          parentPos: { row, col },
284	        };
285	      }
286	    }
287	  }
288	
289	  return true;
290	};
291	
292	// Config localforage
293	const localforageInstance = (localforage as any).default ?? localforage;
294	const storage = localforageInstance.createInstance({
295	  name: 'kintting-design-db',
296	  storeName: 'projects'
297	});
298	
299	localforageInstance
300	  .setDriver([localforageInstance.INDEXEDDB, localforageInstance.WEBSQL, localforageInstance.LOCALSTORAGE])
301	  .catch(() => {
302	    console.warn('localforage failed to set preferred drivers; falling back to defaults');
303	  });
304	
305	const forageStorage: StateStorage = {
306	  getItem: async (name: string): Promise<string | null> => {
307	    let val = (await storage.getItem(name)) as string | null;
308	    // Legacy migration step from simple localStorage
309	    if (!val && typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.localStorage) {
310	      val = window.localStorage.getItem(name);
311	      if (val) {
312	        try {
313	          await storage.setItem(name, val);
314	        } catch (e) {
315	          console.warn('Failed to migrate item to localforage', e);
316	        }
317	      }
318	    }
319	    return val || null;
320	  },
321	  setItem: async (name: string, value: string): Promise<void> => {
322	    await storage.setItem(name, value);
323	  },
324	  removeItem: async (name: string): Promise<void> => {
325	    await storage.removeItem(name);
326	  },
327	};
328	
329	// Default autosave debounce delay (ms). Increase to reduce save frequency.
330	const DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS = 10000;
331	const AUTOSAVE_DELAY_STORAGE_KEY = 'kintting:autosaveDelayMs';
332	
333	// Create a debounced wrapper around the forage storage so frequent writes
334	// (e.g., during continuous drawing) are coalesced. Exposes the same
335	// StateStorage async API expected by zustand's persistence layer.
336	const createDebouncedForageStorage = (delay = DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS): StateStorage => {
337	  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return forageStorage;
338	
339	  let timeout: number | undefined;
340	  const pending = new Map<string, string>();
341	  let flushing = false;
342	
343	  const flush = async () => {
344	    if (flushing) return;
345	    flushing = true;
346	    for (const [k, v] of pending) {
347	      try {
348	        await storage.setItem(k, v);
349	      } catch (e) {
350	        // ignore individual write errors
351	        console.warn('debounced storage setItem failed', e);
352	      }
353	    }
354	    pending.clear();
355	    if (typeof timeout !== 'undefined') {
356	      clearTimeout(timeout);
357	      timeout = undefined;
358	    }
359	    flushing = false;
360	  };
361	
362	  try {
363	    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
364	      // flush synchronously where possible
365	      if (pending.size) {
366	        // best-effort flush (no await in beforeunload)
367	        void flush();
368	      }
369	    });
370	  } catch (e) {
371	    // ignore
372	  }
373	
374	  return {
375	    getItem: async (name: string) => {
376	      // If we have a pending value for this key, return it first
377	      if (pending.has(name)) return pending.get(name) as string;
378	      return (await storage.getItem(name)) as string | null;
379	    },
380	    setItem: async (name: string, value: string) => {
381	      pending.set(name, value);
382	      // read current configured delay from localStorage if available
383	      let configured = delay;
384	      try {
385	        const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(AUTOSAVE_DELAY_STORAGE_KEY);
386	        const parsed = raw ? Number(raw) : NaN;
387	        if (!Number.isNaN(parsed) && parsed > 0) configured = parsed;
388	      } catch (e) {
389	        // ignore
390	      }
391	      if (typeof timeout !== 'undefined') clearTimeout(timeout);
392	      timeout = window.setTimeout(() => void flush(), configured) as unknown as number;
393	    },
394	    removeItem: async (name: string) => {
395	      pending.delete(name);
396	      try {
397	        await storage.removeItem(name);
398	      } catch (e) {
399	        console.warn('debounced storage removeItem failed', e);
400	      }
401	    },
402	  };
403	};
404	
405	export const useProjectStore = create<ProjectState>()(
406	  persist(
407	    (set, get) => {
408	      const updateActiveProject = (updater: (project: Project) => Partial<Project>) => {
409	        const state = get();
410	        if (!state.activeProjectId) return;
411	        const project = state.projects[state.activeProjectId];
412	        if (!project) return;
413	        const nextProject = {
414	          ...project,
415	          ...updater(project),
416	          lastModified: Date.now()
417	        };
418	        set({
419	          projects: {
420	            ...state.projects,
421	            [state.activeProjectId]: nextProject
422	          },
423	          ...projectView(nextProject)
424	        });
425	      };
426	
427	      return {
428	        projects: {},
429	        deletedProjects: {},
430	        activeProjectId: null,
431	        ...emptyProjectView(),
432	        clipboard: null,
433	        validationResults: [],
434	
435	        createProject: (name, rows = 20, cols = 20) => {
436	          const newProject = createProjectRecord(name, rows, cols);
437	          set((state) => ({
438	            projects: { ...state.projects, [newProject.id]: newProject },
439	            activeProjectId: newProject.id,
440	            ...projectView(newProject)
441	          }));
442	          return newProject.id;
443	        },
444	
445	        switchProject: (id) => {
446	          const project = get().projects[id];
447	          if (!project) return;
448	          set({ activeProjectId: id, ...projectView(project), validationResults: [] });
449	        },
450	
451	        deleteProject: (id) => {
452	          set((state) => {
453	            const nextProjects = { ...state.projects };
454	            const projectToDelete = nextProjects[id];
455	            if (!projectToDelete) return state;
456	
457	            delete nextProjects[id];
458	            const nextDeletedProjects = {
459	              ...state.deletedProjects,
460	              [id]: { ...projectToDelete, deletedAt: Date.now() },
461	            };
462	
463	            const fallback = Object.values(nextProjects).sort((a, b) => b.lastModified - a.lastModified)[0];
464	            return {
465	              projects: nextProjects,
466	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
467	              activeProjectId: state.activeProjectId === id ? fallback?.id ?? null : state.activeProjectId,
468	              ...(state.activeProjectId === id ? (fallback ? projectView(fallback) : emptyProjectView()) : {})
469	            };
470	          });
471	        },
472	
473	        restoreProject: (id) => {
474	          set((state) => {
475	            const deleted = state.deletedProjects[id];
476	            if (!deleted) return state;
477	
478	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
479	            delete nextDeletedProjects[id];
480	
481	            const restoredProject = {
482	              ...deleted,
483	              deletedAt: undefined,
484	              lastModified: Date.now(),
485	            };
486	
487	            return {
488	              projects: { ...state.projects, [id]: restoredProject },
489	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
490	            };
491	          });
492	        },
493	
494	        deleteProjectPermanently: (id) => {
495	          set((state) => {
496	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
497	            delete nextDeletedProjects[id];
498	            return { deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects };
499	          });
500	        },
501	
502	        emptyRecycleBin: () => {
503	          set({ deletedProjects: {} });
504	        },
505	
506	        purgeExpiredProjects: () => {
507	          set((state) => {
508	            const nextProjects = { ...state.projects };
509	            const nextDeletedProjects = { ...state.deletedProjects };
510	            let changed = false;
511	
512	            Object.entries(state.projects).forEach(([id, project]) => {
513	              if (state.activeProjectId === id) return;
514	              if (Date.now() - project.lastModified > EXPIRY_SOFT_DELETE_MS) {
515	                nextDeletedProjects[id] = { ...project, deletedAt: Date.now() };
516	                delete nextProjects[id];
517	                changed = true;
518	              }
519	            });
520	
521	            if (!changed) return state;
522	
523	            const fallback = Object.values(nextProjects).sort((a, b) => b.lastModified - a.lastModified)[0];
524	            const nextActiveId = state.activeProjectId && nextProjects[state.activeProjectId] ? state.activeProjectId : fallback?.id ?? null;
525	
526	            return {
527	              projects: nextProjects,
528	              deletedProjects: nextDeletedProjects,
529	              activeProjectId: nextActiveId,
530	              ...(nextActiveId ? projectView(nextProjects[nextActiveId]) : emptyProjectView()),
531	            };
532	          });
533	        },
534	
535	        renameProject: (id, name) => {
536	          const nextName = name.trim();
537	          if (!nextName) return;
538	          set((state) => {
539	            const project = state.projects[id];
540	            if (!project) return state;
541	            const nextProject = { ...project, name: nextName, lastModified: Date.now() };
542	            return {
543	              projects: {
544	                ...state.projects,
545	                [id]: nextProject,
546	              },
547	              ...(state.activeProjectId === id ? projectView(nextProject) : {}),
548	            };
549	          });
550	        },
551	
552	        duplicateProject: (id) => {
553	          const project = get().projects[id];
554	          if (!project) return null;
555	          const nextProject = cloneProject(project, `${project.name} Copy`);
556	          set((state) => ({
557	            projects: { ...state.projects, [nextProject.id]: nextProject },
558	            activeProjectId: nextProject.id,
559	            ...projectView(nextProject),
560	          }));
561	          return nextProject.id;
562	        },
563	
564	        updateProjectThumbnail: (id, thumbnail) => {
565	          set((state) => {
566	            const project = state.projects[id];
567	            if (!project) return state;
568	            return {
569	              projects: {
570	                ...state.projects,
571	                [id]: { ...project, thumbnail, lastModified: Date.now() }
572	              }
573	            };
574	          });
575	        },
576	
577	        replaceModeGrid: (mode, grid, resetHistory = true) => {
578	          const { activeProjectId } = get();
579	          if (!activeProjectId) {
580	            get().createProject('Untitled Project', grid.length, grid[0]?.length ?? 0);
581	          }
582	
583	          updateActiveProject((project) => ({
584	            grids: { ...project.grids, [mode]: cloneGrid(grid) },
585	            currentMode: mode,
586	            ...(resetHistory ? { undoStack: [], redoStack: [] } : {}),
587	          }));
588	        },
589	
590	        setMode: (mode) => {
591	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ currentMode: mode }));
592	        },
593	
594	        setTextLocale: (locale) => {
595	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ textLocale: locale }));
596	          get().compileToText();
597	        },
598	
599	        setRowNumberDirection: (direction) => {
600	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ rowNumberDirection: direction }));
601	          get().compileToText();
602	        },
603	
604	        initGrid: (rows, cols) => {
605	          if (!get().activeProjectId) {
606	            get().createProject('Untitled Project', rows, cols);
607	            return;
608	          }
609	
610	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ 
611	            grids: { 
612	              knit: createEmptyGrid(rows, cols), 
613	              crochet: createEmptyGrid(rows, cols) 
614	            },
615	            description: '',
616	            undoStack: [], 
617	            redoStack: [] 
618	          }));
619	        },
620	
621	        applyCellChange: (row, col, char, svgPath, stitchId) => {
622	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
623	          if (!activeProjectId) return false;
624	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
625	
626	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
627	          if (!currentGrid[row] || !currentGrid[row][col]) return false;
628	        
629	          const isErasing = !stitchId;
630	          const stitchDef = stitchId ? stitchRegistry[stitchId] : null;
631	        
632	          const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
633	          const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
634	
635	          let needsUpdate = false;
636	          const newGrid = currentGrid.map(r => [...r]);
637	
638	          const clearStitchAt = (r: number, c: number) => {
639	            const cell = newGrid[r]?.[c];
640	            if (!cell) return;
641	            if (cell.isSpanChild && cell.parentPos) {
642	              clearStitchAt(cell.parentPos.row, cell.parentPos.col);
643	              return;
644	            }
645	          
646	            const sDef = cell.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId] : null;
647	            const cSpanW = sDef?.span?.width || 1;
648	            const cSpanH = sDef?.span?.height || 1;
649	          
650	            for (let i = 0; i < cSpanH; i++) {
651	              for (let j = 0; j < cSpanW; j++) {
652	                if (newGrid[r + i] && newGrid[r + i][c + j]) {
653	                  newGrid[r + i][c + j] = { ...newGrid[r + i][c + j], char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: '', isSpanChild: false, parentPos: undefined };
654	                  needsUpdate = true;
655	                }
656	              }
657	            }
658	          };
659	
660	          if (isErasing) {
661	            if (newGrid[row][col].stitchId || newGrid[row][col].isSpanChild) {
662	              clearStitchAt(row, col);
663	            }
664	          } else {
665	            if (row + spanH > currentGrid.length || col + spanW > currentGrid[0].length) {
666	              return false; 
667	            }
668	
669	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
670	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
671	                 const tarR = row + i;
672	                 const tarC = col + j;
673	                 if (newGrid[tarR]?.[tarC] && (newGrid[tarR][tarC].stitchId || newGrid[tarR][tarC].isSpanChild)) {
674	                   clearStitchAt(tarR, tarC);
675	                 }
676	              }
677	            }
678	
679	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
680	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
681	                const tarR = row + i;
682	                const tarC = col + j;
683	                if (newGrid[tarR] && newGrid[tarR][tarC]) {
684	                  if (i === 0 && j === 0) {
685	                    newGrid[tarR][tarC] = { ...newGrid[tarR][tarC], char, svgPath, stitchId, isSpanChild: false, parentPos: undefined };
686	                  } else {
687	                    newGrid[tarR][tarC] = { ...newGrid[tarR][tarC], char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: stitchId, isSpanChild: true, parentPos: { row, col } };
688	                  }
689	                  needsUpdate = true;
690	                }
691	              }
692	            }
693	          }
694	
695	          if (needsUpdate) {
696	            get()._saveSnapshot();
697	            updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid } }));
698	            get().compileToText();
699	            return true;
700	          }
701	
702	          return false;
703	        },
704	
705	        copySelection: (roots, anchor) => {
706	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
707	          if (!activeProjectId || !anchor || roots.length === 0) return false;
708	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
709	
710	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
711	          const seen = new Set<string>();
712	          const items: ClipboardItem[] = [];
713	
714	          for (const root of roots) {
715	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
716	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
717	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
718	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
719	            seen.add(key);
720	
721	            const cell = currentGrid[resolvedRoot.row]?.[resolvedRoot.col];
722	            if (!cell?.stitchId || cell.isSpanChild) continue;
723	
724	            items.push({
725	              dr: resolvedRoot.row - anchor.row,
726	              dc: resolvedRoot.col - anchor.col,
727	              cellSnapshot: { ...cell, parentPos: undefined, isSpanChild: false },
728	            });
729	          }
730	
731	          if (!items.length) return false;
732	          set({ clipboard: { anchor, items } });
733	          return true;
734	        },
735	
736	        cutSelection: (roots, anchor) => {
737	          if (!get().copySelection(roots, anchor)) return false;
738	
739	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
740	          if (!activeProjectId) return false;
741	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
742	
743	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
744	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
745	          let changed = false;
746	
747	          const seen = new Set<string>();
748	          for (const root of roots) {
749	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
750	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
751	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
752	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
753	            seen.add(key);
754	            changed = clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col) || changed;
755	          }
756	
757	          if (!changed) return false;
758	          get()._saveSnapshot();
759	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
760	          get().compileToText();
761	          return true;
762	        },
763	
764	        pasteClipboard: (target) => {
765	          const { activeProjectId, projects, clipboard } = get();
766	          if (!activeProjectId || !clipboard?.items.length) return null;
767	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
768	
769	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
770	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
771	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
772	          const placements = clipboard.items.map((item) => ({
773	            row: target.row + item.dr,
774	            col: target.col + item.dc,
775	            item,
776	          }));
777	
778	          const isOutOfBounds = placements.some(({ row, col, item }) => {
779	            const stitchDef = item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
780	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
781	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
782	            return row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > rows || col + spanW > cols;
783	          });
784	
785	          if (isOutOfBounds) return null;
786	
787	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
788	          for (const placement of placements) {
789	            placeStitchSnapshot(nextGrid, placement.row, placement.col, placement.item.cellSnapshot);
790	          }
791	
792	          get()._saveSnapshot();
793	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
794	          get().compileToText();
795	          return placements.map(({ row, col }) => ({ row, col }));
796	        },
797	
798	        exportSnapshot: () => {
799	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
800	          if (!activeProjectId) return { pages: [] };
801	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
802	
803	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
804	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
805	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
806	
807	          const pageWidth = 595.28;
808	          const pageHeight = 841.89;
809	          const cellSize = 16;
810	          const gridWidth = cols * cellSize;
811	          const gridHeight = rows * cellSize;
812	          const pageScale = Math.min(pageWidth / Math.max(gridWidth, 1), pageHeight / Math.max(gridHeight, 1), 1);
813	
814	          const glyphs = [] as Array<{
815	            id: string;
816	            svgPath: string;
817	            transform: { tx: number; ty: number; scale: number };
818	            bounds: { w: number; h: number };
819	          }>;
820	
821	          for (let row = 0; row < rows; row += 1) {
822	            for (let col = 0; col < cols; col += 1) {
823	              const cell = currentGrid[row]?.[col];
824	              if (!cell?.stitchId || cell.isSpanChild) continue;
825	              const stitchDef = stitchRegistry[cell.stitchId];
826	              if (!stitchDef) continue;
827	
828	              const spanW = stitchDef.span.width || 1;
829	              const spanH = stitchDef.span.height || 1;
830	              glyphs.push({
831	                id: `${row}-${col}-${cell.stitchId}`,
832	                svgPath: stitchDef.svgPath,
833	                transform: {
834	                  tx: col * cellSize * pageScale,
835	                  ty: row * cellSize * pageScale,
836	                  scale: pageScale,
837	                },
838	                bounds: {
839	                  w: spanW * cellSize * pageScale,
840	                  h: spanH * cellSize * pageScale,
841	                },
842	              });
843	            }
844	          }
845	
846	          return {
847	            pages: [
848	              {
849	                width: pageWidth,
850	                height: pageHeight,
851	                glyphs,
852	              },
853	            ],
854	          } as ExportSnapshot;
855	        },
856	
857	        moveSelection: (roots, anchor, target) => {
858	          if (!get().copySelection(roots, anchor)) return null;
859	
860	          const { activeProjectId, projects, clipboard } = get();
861	          if (!activeProjectId || !clipboard?.items.length) return null;
862	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
863	
864	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
865	          const rows = currentGrid.length;
866	          const cols = currentGrid[0]?.length ?? 0;
867	          const placements = clipboard.items.map((item) => ({
868	            row: target.row + item.dr,
869	            col: target.col + item.dc,
870	            item,
871	          }));
872	
873	          const isOutOfBounds = placements.some(({ row, col, item }) => {
874	            const stitchDef = item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
875	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
876	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
877	            return row < 0 || col < 0 || row + spanH > rows || col + spanW > cols;
878	          });
879	
880	          if (isOutOfBounds) return null;
881	
882	          const nextGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
883	
884	          for (const placement of placements) {
885	            const stitchDef = placement.item.cellSnapshot.stitchId ? stitchRegistry[placement.item.cellSnapshot.stitchId] : null;
886	            const spanW = stitchDef?.span?.width || 1;
887	            const spanH = stitchDef?.span?.height || 1;
888	            for (let i = 0; i < spanH; i++) {
889	              for (let j = 0; j < spanW; j++) {
890	                clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, placement.row + i, placement.col + j);
891	              }
892	            }
893	          }
894	
895	          const seen = new Set<string>();
896	          for (const root of roots) {
897	            const resolvedRoot = getRootPosition(currentGrid, root.row, root.col);
898	            if (!resolvedRoot) continue;
899	            const key = rootKey(resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
900	            if (seen.has(key)) continue;
901	            seen.add(key);
902	            clearStitchAtRoot(nextGrid, resolvedRoot.row, resolvedRoot.col);
903	          }
904	
905	          for (const placement of placements) {
906	            placeStitchSnapshot(nextGrid, placement.row, placement.col, placement.item.cellSnapshot);
907	          }
908	
909	          get()._saveSnapshot();
910	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: nextGrid } }));
911	          get().compileToText();
912	          return placements.map(({ row, col }) => ({ row, col }));
913	        },
914	
915	        compileToText: () => {
916	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
917	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
918	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
919	
920	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
921	          const text = compileGridToText(currentGrid, { locale: project.textLocale, rowNumberDirection: project.rowNumberDirection });
922	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ description: text }));
923	        },
924	
925	        applyTextToGrid: (text: string) => {
926	          const { activeProjectId, projects, _saveSnapshot } = get();
927	          if (!activeProjectId) return [];
928	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
929	
930	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
931	          const rowsInGrid = currentGrid.length;
932	          const colsInGrid = currentGrid.length > 0 ? currentGrid[0].length : 0;
933	
934	          const parsedRows = parseTextToGrid(text, colsInGrid);
935	
936	          set({ validationResults: parsedRows });
937	
938	          const hasInvalidRows = parsedRows.some((r: any) => !r.validation.valid);
939	
940	          if (hasInvalidRows) {
941	            if (text.trim() === '') {
942	              updateActiveProject(() => ({ description: '' }));
943	            } else {
944	              get().compileToText(); 
945	            }
946	            return parsedRows; 
947	          }
948	
949	          _saveSnapshot(); 
950	
951	          // Determine target column count: keep existing width unless text needs more
952	          let maxColsFromText = colsInGrid;
953	          parsedRows.forEach((pRow: any) => {
954	            if (pRow.validation.delta > 0) {
955	              maxColsFromText = Math.max(maxColsFromText, colsInGrid + pRow.validation.delta);
956	            }
957	          });
958	
959	          // Edge case: empty grid or empty text → create fresh
960	          if (rowsInGrid === 0 || text.trim() === '') {
961	            const emptyGrid = createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText);
962	            updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: emptyGrid }, description: '' }));
963	            return parsedRows;
964	          }
965	
966	          // Clone existing grid to preserve rows not mentioned in the text input
967	          let newGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
968	
969	          // If text requires more columns than current grid, expand all rows
970	          if (maxColsFromText > colsInGrid) {
971	            newGrid = newGrid.map(row => {
972	              const newRow = [...row];
973	              for (let c = colsInGrid; c < maxColsFromText; c++) {
974	                newRow.push({ char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: undefined });
975	              }
976	              return newRow;
977	            });
978	          }
979	
980	          // Only overwrite rows that are present in the parsed text
981	          parsedRows.forEach((parsed: any) => {
982	            const gridRowIndex = gridRowFromDisplayRow(parsed.rowNumber, rowsInGrid, project.rowNumberDirection);
983	            if (gridRowIndex >= 0 && gridRowIndex < rowsInGrid) {
984	              const isEvenRow = parsed.rowNumber % 2 === 0;
985	              const colOffset = parsed.colOffset || 0;
986	              // 使用列偏移确定起始位置：
987	              // 偶数行（WS, 从左到右）：从 colOffset 开始
988	              // 奇数行（RS, 从右到左）：从 (maxColsFromText - 1 - colOffset) 开始
989	              let currentCol = isEvenRow ? colOffset : (maxColsFromText - 1 - colOffset);
990	
991	              // 清除该行中将要写入的区域，避免残留旧数据（如旧的 spanChild 标记）
992	              const totalSpanWidth = parsed.cells.reduce((sum: number, c: any) =>
993	                sum + (stitchRegistry[c.stitchId]?.span?.width || 1), 0);
994	              const clearStart = isEvenRow ? colOffset : Math.max(0, maxColsFromText - 1 - colOffset - totalSpanWidth + 1);
995	              const clearEnd = isEvenRow ? Math.min(maxColsFromText - 1, colOffset + totalSpanWidth - 1) : (maxColsFromText - 1 - colOffset);
996	              for (let c = clearStart; c <= clearEnd; c++) {
997	                newGrid[gridRowIndex][c] = { char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: undefined };
998	              }
999	
1000	              for (const cell of parsed.cells) {
1001	                const stitchId = cell.stitchId!;
1002	                const spanW = stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.span?.width || 1;
1003	                const dir = isEvenRow ? 1 : -1;
1004	
1005	                const endCol = currentCol + dir * (spanW - 1);
1006	                if (dir === 1 && endCol >= maxColsFromText) continue; 
1007	                if (dir === -1 && endCol < 0) continue; 
1008	
1009	                if (currentCol >= 0 && currentCol < maxColsFromText) {
1010	                  newGrid[gridRowIndex][currentCol] = {
1011	                    ...cell,
1012	                    svgPath: stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.svgPath || '',
1013	                    isSpanChild: false,
1014	                    parentPos: undefined,
1015	                  };
1016	                }
1017	
1018	                for (let k = 1; k < spanW; k++) {
1019	                  const childCol = currentCol + dir * k;
1020	                  if (childCol >= 0 && childCol < maxColsFromText) {
1021	                    newGrid[gridRowIndex][childCol] = {
1022	                      char: '',
1023	                      svgPath: '',
1024	                      stitchId,
1025	                      isSpanChild: true,
1026	                      parentPos: { row: gridRowIndex, col: currentCol },
1027	                    };
1028	                  }
1029	                }
1030	                currentCol = currentCol + dir * spanW;
1031	              }
1032	            }
1033	          });
1034	
1035	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid }, description: text }));
1036	          return parsedRows;
1037	        },
1038	
1039	        resizeGrid: (newCols: number) => {
1040	          const { activeProjectId, projects, _saveSnapshot } = get();
1041	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1042	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1043	
1044	          const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
1045	          const currentRows = currentGrid.length;
1046	          const currentCols = currentGrid.length > 0 ? currentGrid[0].length : 0;
1047	
1048	          if (newCols === currentCols) return; 
1049	
1050	          _saveSnapshot(); 
1051	
1052	          const newGrid = createEmptyGrid(currentRows, newCols);
1053	
1054	          for (let r = 0; r < currentRows; r++) {
1055	            for (let c = 0; c < Math.min(currentCols, newCols); c++) {
1056	              newGrid[r][c] = currentGrid[r][c];
1057	            }
1058	          }
1059	
1060	          updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid } }));
1061	          get().compileToText(); 
1062	        },
1063	
1064	        undo: () => {
1065	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1066	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1067	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1068	
1069	          if (project.undoStack.length === 0) return;
1070	        
1071	          const previous = project.undoStack[project.undoStack.length - 1];
1072	          const newUndoStack = project.undoStack.slice(0, -1);
1073	        
1074	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1075	            grids: previous.grids,
1076	            currentMode: previous.currentMode,
1077	            description: previous.description || '',
1078	            undoStack: newUndoStack,
1079	            redoStack: [...project.redoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1080	          }));
1081	        },
1082	
1083	        redo: () => {
1084	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1085	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1086	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1087	
1088	          if (project.redoStack.length === 0) return;
1089	        
1090	          const next = project.redoStack[project.redoStack.length - 1];
1091	          const newRedoStack = project.redoStack.slice(0, -1);
1092	        
1093	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1094	            grids: next.grids,
1095	            currentMode: next.currentMode,
1096	            description: next.description || '',
1097	            undoStack: [...project.undoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1098	            redoStack: newRedoStack,
1099	          }));
1100	        },
1101	
1102	        _saveSnapshot: () => {
1103	          const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
1104	          if (!activeProjectId) return;
1105	          const project = projects[activeProjectId];
1106	
1107	          updateActiveProject(() => ({
1108	            undoStack: [...project.undoStack, { grids: project.grids, currentMode: project.currentMode, description: project.description }],
1109	            redoStack: []
1110	          }));
1111	        }
1112	      };
1113	    },
1114	    {
1115	      name: 'kintting-design-project',
1116	      storage: createJSONStorage(() => createDebouncedForageStorage(DEFAULT_AUTOSAVE_DELAY_MS), {
1117	        replacer: storageReplacer,
1118	        reviver: storageReviver,
1119	      }),
1120	      version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
1121	      partialize: (state) => ({
1122	        projects: state.projects,
1123	        deletedProjects: state.deletedProjects,
1124	        activeProjectId: state.activeProjectId,
1125	      }),
1126	      merge: (persistedState: any, currentState) => {
1127	        const merged = { ...currentState, ...(persistedState ?? {}) };
1128	        const activeProject = merged.activeProjectId ? merged.projects?.[merged.activeProjectId] : null;
1129	        return {
1130	          ...merged,
1131	          deletedProjects: merged.deletedProjects ?? {},
1132	          ...(activeProject ? projectView(activeProject) : emptyProjectView()),
1133	          clipboard: null,
1134	          validationResults: [],
1135	        };
1136	      },
1137	      migrate: (persistedState: any, version: number) => {
1138	        if (!persistedState || Object.keys(persistedState).length === 0) {
1139	          return {
1140	            projects: {},
1141	            deletedProjects: {},
1142	            activeProjectId: null,
1143	            clipboard: null,
1144	            validationResults: [],
1145	          };
1146	        }
1147	
1148	        if (version === 0 || typeof persistedState.version !== 'number') {
1149	          if (persistedState.projects && typeof persistedState.projects === 'object') {
1150	            const migratedProjects = Object.fromEntries(
1151	              Object.entries(persistedState.projects).map(([id, project]) => [id, normalizeProject(project)])
1152	            );
1153	
1154	            return {
1155	              projects: migratedProjects,
1156	              deletedProjects: {},
1157	              activeProjectId: persistedState.activeProjectId in migratedProjects ? persistedState.activeProjectId : Object.keys(migratedProjects)[0] ?? null,
1158	              clipboard: null,
1159	              validationResults: [],
1160	            };
1161	          }
1162	
1163	          const id = crypto.randomUUID();
1164	          const grids = persistedState.grids || { knit: [], crochet: [] };
1165	          const currentMode = persistedState.currentMode === 'crochet' ? 'crochet' : 'knit';
1166	
1167	          return {
1168	            projects: {
1169	              [id]: {
1170	                id,
1171	                name: 'Migrated Project',
1172	                lastModified: Date.now(),
1173	                deletedAt: undefined,
1174	                thumbnail: undefined,
1175	                version: CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION,
1176	                grids,
1177	                currentMode,
1178	                description: '',
1179	                textLocale: 'abbr' as TextLocale,
1180	                rowNumberDirection: 'row1_top' as RowNumberDirection,
1181	                undoStack: [],
1182	                redoStack: [],
1183	              }
1184	            },
1185	            deletedProjects: {},
1186	            activeProjectId: id,
1187	            clipboard: null,
1188	            validationResults: [],
1189	          };
1190	        }
1191	
1192	        if (version < CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION) {
1193	          if (persistedState.projects && typeof persistedState.projects === 'object') {
1194	            const upgradedProjects = Object.fromEntries(
1195	              Object.entries(persistedState.projects).map(([id, project]) => [id, normalizeProject(project)])
1196	            );
1197	
1198	            return {
1199	              projects: upgradedProjects,
1200	              deletedProjects: {},
1201	              activeProjectId: persistedState.activeProjectId in upgradedProjects ? persistedState.activeProjectId : Object.keys(upgradedProjects)[0] ?? null,
1202	              clipboard: null,
1203	              validationResults: [],
1204	            };
1205	          }
1206	        }
1207	
1208	        return persistedState;
1209	      },
1210	    }
1211	  )
1212	);
1213	
```

#### Tool: Read

> Read: `D:\aaa-llx\MyKinttingDesign\MyKinttingDesignApp\src\components\Grid\grid.css`

```json
19	  width: 100%;
20	  height: 100%;
21	}
```

```json
61	    if (state.interactionMode === 'PAN') {
62	      return state;
63	    }
64

69	      return state;
70	    }
71	
72	    return {
```

```json
25	export function screenToGrid(
26	  screenPoint: Point,
27	  viewportOffset: Point,
28	  scale: number,
29	  cellSize: number
30	): { row: number; col: number } {
31	  const gridX = (screenPoint.x - viewportOffset.x) / scale;
32	  const gridY = (screenPoint.y - viewportOffset.y) / scale;
33	
34	  return {
35	    col: Math.floor(gridX / cellSize),
36	    row: Math.floor(gridY / cellSize),
37	  };
38	}
39	
40	export function gridToScreen(
41	  row: number,
42	  col: number,
43	  viewportOffset: Point,
44	  scale: number,
45	  cellSize: number
46	): Point {
47	  return {
48	    x: col * cellSize * scale + viewportOffset.x,
49	    y: row * cellSize * scale + viewportOffset.y,
50	  };
51	}
52	
53	export function calculateZoomOffset(
54	  currentOffset: Point,
55	  currentScale: number,
56	  newScale: number,
57	  mousePoint: Point
58	): Point {
59	  const logicalX = (mousePoint.x - currentOffset.x) / currentScale;
60	  const logicalY = (mousePoint.y - currentOffset.y) / currentScale;
61	
62	  return {
63	    x: mousePoint.x - logicalX * newScale,
64	    y: mousePoint.y - logicalY * newScale,
65	  };
66	}
67	
68	export function resolveGridCell(
69	  grid: CellData[][],
70	  row: number,
71	  col: number
72	): ResolvedGridCell | null {
73	  if (!grid[row] || !grid[row][col]) {
74	    return null;
75	  }
76	
77	  const anchor = { row, col };
78	  const cell = grid[row][col];
79	
80	  if (cell.isSpanChild && cell.parentPos) {
81	    const root = cell.parentPos;
82	    return {
83	      anchor,
84	      root,
85	      cell: grid[root.row]?.[root.col] ?? null,
86	    };
87	  }
88	
89	  return {
90	    anchor,
91	    root: anchor,
92	    cell,
93	  };
94	}
95	
96	export function toSelectedCellState(resolved: ResolvedGridCell): SelectedCellState {
97	  return {
98	    anchor: resolved.anchor,
99	    root: resolved.root,
100	  };
101	}
102	
103	export function getNavigatorMetrics(
104	  rows: number,
105	  cols: number,
106	  _viewportSize: ViewportSize,
107	  _scale: number,
108	  navigatorSize: number,
109	  _cellSize: number,
110	  padding: number
111	): NavigatorMetrics {
112	  const safeRows = Math.max(rows, 1);
113	  const safeCols = Math.max(cols, 1);
114	  const contentSize = Math.max(1, navigatorSize - padding * 2);
115	  const miniCellSize = Math.min(contentSize / safeCols, contentSize / safeRows);
116	  const gridWidth = cols * miniCellSize;
117	  const gridHeight = rows * miniCellSize;
118	
119	  return {
120	    miniCellSize,
121	    gridWidth,
122	    gridHeight,
123	    originX: (navigatorSize - gridWidth) / 2,
124	    originY: (navigatorSize - gridHeight) / 2,
125	  };
126	}
127	
128	export function getNavigatorViewportRect(
129	  rows: number,
130	  cols: number,
131	  viewportOffset: Point,
132	  viewportSize: ViewportSize,
133	  scale: number,
134	  cellSize: number,
135	  metrics: NavigatorMetrics
136	) {
137	  if (rows <= 0 || cols <= 0 || viewportSize.width <= 0 || viewportSize.height <= 0 || scale <= 0) {
138	    return null;
139	  }
140	
141	  const scaledCellSize = cellSize * scale;
142	  const x = metrics.originX + (-viewportOffset.x / scaledCellSize) * metrics.miniCellSize;
143	  const y = metrics.originY + (-viewportOffset.y / scaledCellSize) * metrics.miniCellSize;
144	  const width = (viewportSize.width / scaledCellSize) * metrics.miniCellSize;
145	  const height = (viewportSize.height / scaledCellSize) * metrics.miniCellSize;
146	
147	  return {
148	    x: clamp(x, metrics.originX, metrics.originX + metrics.gridWidth),
149	    y: clamp(y, metrics.originY, metrics.originY + metrics.gridHeight),
150	    width: Math.max(1, Math.min(width, metrics.gridWidth)),
151	    height: Math.max(1, Math.min(height, metrics.gridHeight)),
152	  };
153	}
154	
155	export function getViewportOffsetFromNavigatorPointer(
156	  pointer: Point,
157	  rows: number,
158	  cols: number,
159	  viewportSize: ViewportSize,
160	  scale: number,
161	  cellSize: number,
162	  metrics: NavigatorMetrics
163	): Point | null {
164	  if (rows <= 0 || cols <= 0 || viewportSize.width <= 0 || viewportSize.height <= 0 || scale <= 0) {
165	    return null;
166	  }
167	
168	  const scaledCellSize = cellSize * scale;
169	  const logicalCenterCol = (pointer.x - metrics.originX) / metrics.miniCellSize;
170	  const logicalCenterRow = (pointer.y - metrics.originY) / metrics.miniCellSize;
171	  const gridPixelWidth = cols * scaledCellSize;
172	  const gridPixelHeight = rows * scaledCellSize;
173	
174	  return {
175	    x: clamp(viewportSize.width / 2 - logicalCenterCol * scaledCellSize, viewportSize.width - gridPixelWidth, 0),
176	    y: clamp(viewportSize.height / 2 - logicalCenterRow * scaledCellSize, viewportSize.height - gridPixelHeight, 0),
177	  };
178	}
```

#### Thinking

Now I see the issue! Look at `updateActiveProject`:

```javascript
const updateActiveProject = (updater: (project: Project) => Partial<Project>) => {
  const state = get();
  if (!state.activeProjectId) return;
  const project = state.projects[state.activeProjectId];
  if (!project) return;
  const nextProject = {
    ...project,
    ...updater(project),
    lastModified: Date.now()
  };
  set({
    projects: {
      ...state.projects,
      [state.activeProjectId]: nextProject
    },
    ...projectView(nextProject)
  });
};
```

And `projectView`:
```javascript
const projectView = (project: Project) => ({
  grids: project.grids,
  currentMode: project.currentMode,
  description: project.description,
  textLocale: project.textLocale,
  rowNumberDirection: project.rowNumberDirection,
  undoStack: project.undoStack,
  redoStack: project.redoStack,
});
```

So when `applyTextToGrid` calls `updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid }, description: text }))`, the updater returns an object with the updated grids and description, which gets merged into the next project state along with the timestamp.

The `set()` call then spreads both the updated projects map and the flattened project view into the store, so `grids` ends up with the new grid data and `description` gets set to the raw text. The Grid component should pick up this change since it's reading `grids` from the store, but I'm wondering if there's a selector issue or if the component isn't actually re-rendering when the state updates.

Let me trace through the Grid component more carefully—it's destructuring `grids` and `currentMode` directly from `useProjectStore()`, which means it's subscribing to the entire store state. When `set()` is called with new values, Zustand should trigger a re-render for any component that accessed those properties. The `grids` object reference changes because we're creating a new object with the spread operator, so the component should detect that change and re-render with the updated grid data.

But wait, I'm realizing the real issue might not be in the Grid component at all. The user mentioned the editor shows updated text after clicking Apply, but the grid itself doesn't reflect those changes. That suggests the problem could be in how the text is being parsed and applied to the grid state in the first place, not in how the grid is being rendered.

Let me trace through what happens when text is applied: the editor text gets parsed into rows, and if any row fails validation, the entire apply operation aborts and the grid stays unchanged. The validation checks whether the effective width (column offset plus stitch count) exceeds the grid's column count. So if the parsed text has rows that are too wide, nothing gets applied at all.

Looking at the specific rows in the screenshot, they all seem to fit within the 40-column limit, but I should verify this more carefully by checking each row's actual width calculation. I'm verifying the column calculations for the remaining rows—Row 10 checks out at 18 total, and Row 11 comes to 24, both well within the 40-column limit. So the validation should pass for all rows, which means the issue must be elsewhere. Let me reconsider whether the problem is actually in the `applyTextToGrid` function itself rather than the validation logic.

Actually, I'm wondering if the real culprit is the editor sync logic. But if that effect isn't firing or isn't working correctly, the editor might not reflect the actual grid state.
```javascript
compileToText: () => {
  const { activeProjectId, projects } = get();
  if (!activeProjectId) return;
  const project = projects[activeProjectId];
  const currentGrid = project.grids[project.currentMode];
  const text = compileGridToText(currentGrid, { locale: project.textLocale, rowNumberDirection: project.rowNumberDirection });


```

```json
3	export const displayRowNumber = (

9	export const gridRowFromDisplayRow = (
```

#### Thinking

I see the issue now! Look at `updateActiveProject`:

```javascript
const updateActiveProject = (updater: (project: Project) => Partial<Project>) => {
  const state = get();
  if (!state.activeProjectId) return;
  const project = state.projects[state.activeProjectId];
  if (!project) return;
  const nextProject = {
    ...project,
    ...updater(project),
    lastModified: Date.now()
  };
  set({
    projects: {
      ...state.projects,
      [state.activeProjectId]: nextProject
    },
    ...projectView(nextProject)
  });
};
```

And `projectView`:
```javascript
const projectView = (project: Project) => ({
  grids: project.grids,
  currentMode: project.currentMode,
  description: project.description,
  textLocale: project.textLocale,
  rowNumberDirection: project.rowNumberDirection,
  undoStack: project.undoStack,
  redoStack: project.redoStack,
});
```

So when `applyTextToGrid` calls `updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: newGrid } }))`, the updater returns an object with the updated grids, which gets merged into the next project state along with the timestamp, then the whole thing gets spread into the store update.

The `set()` call creates a new `projects` object with the updated project, and `projectView(nextProject)` flattens out the grid data so it's accessible at the top level of the state. This means `state.grids` should now reference the new grid object with the updated mode.

Since the Grid component reads `grids` directly from the store and the reference has changed, it should trigger a re-render. But I'm wondering if there's something about how Zustand's `persist` middleware handles state updates that might be interfering with the reactivity here.

```json
949	          _saveSnapshot(); 
950	
951	          // Determine target column count: keep existing width unless text needs more
952	          let maxColsFromText = colsInGrid;
953	          parsedRows.forEach((pRow: any) => {
954	            if (pRow.validation.delta > 0) {
955	              maxColsFromText = Math.max(maxColsFromText, colsInGrid + pRow.validation.delta);
956	            }
957	          });
958	
959	          // Edge case: empty grid or empty text → create fresh
960	          if (rowsInGrid === 0 || text.trim() === '') {
961	            const emptyGrid = createEmptyGrid(rowsInGrid, maxColsFromText);
962	            updateActiveProject(() => ({ grids: { ...project.grids, [project.currentMode]: emptyGrid }, description: '' }));
963	            return parsedRows;
964	          }
965	
966	          // Clone existing grid to preserve rows not mentioned in the text input
967	          let newGrid = cloneGrid(currentGrid);
968	
969	          // If text requires more columns than current grid, expand all rows
970	          if (maxColsFromText > colsInGrid) {
971	            newGrid = newGrid.map(row => {
972	              const newRow = [...row];
973	              for (let c = colsInGrid; c < maxColsFromText; c++) {
974	                newRow.push({ char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: undefined });
975	              }
976	              return newRow;
977	            });
978	          }
979	
980	          // Only overwrite rows that are present in the parsed text
981	          parsedRows.forEach((parsed: any) => {
982	            const gridRowIndex = gridRowFromDisplayRow(parsed.rowNumber, rowsInGrid, project.rowNumberDirection);
983	            if (gridRowIndex >= 0 && gridRowIndex < rowsInGrid) {
984	              const isEvenRow = parsed.rowNumber % 2 === 0;
985	              const colOffset = parsed.colOffset || 0;
986	              // 使用列偏移确定起始位置：
987	              // 偶数行（WS, 从左到右）：从 colOffset 开始
988	              // 奇数行（RS, 从右到左）：从 (maxColsFromText - 1 - colOffset) 开始
989	              let currentCol = isEvenRow ? colOffset : (maxColsFromText - 1 - colOffset);
990	
991	              // 清除该行中将要写入的区域，避免残留旧数据（如旧的 spanChild 标记）
992	              const totalSpanWidth = parsed.cells.reduce((sum: number, c: any) =>
993	                sum + (stitchRegistry[c.stitchId]?.span?.width || 1), 0);
994	              const clearStart = isEvenRow ? colOffset : Math.max(0, maxColsFromText - 1 - colOffset - totalSpanWidth + 1);
995	              const clearEnd = isEvenRow ? Math.min(maxColsFromText - 1, colOffset + totalSpanWidth - 1) : (maxColsFromText - 1 - colOffset);
996	              for (let c = clearStart; c <= clearEnd; c++) {
997	                newGrid[gridRowIndex][c] = { char: '', svgPath: '', stitchId: undefined };
998	              }
999	
1000	              for (const cell of parsed.cells) {
1001	                const stitchId = cell.stitchId!;
1002	                const spanW = stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.span?.width || 1;
1003	                const dir = isEvenRow ? 1 : -1;
1004	
1005	                const endCol = currentCol + dir * (spanW - 1);
1006	                if (dir === 1 && endCol >= maxColsFromText) continue; 
1007	                if (dir === -1 && endCol < 0) continue; 
1008	
1009	                if (currentCol >= 0 && currentCol < maxColsFromText) {
1010	                  newGrid[gridRowIndex][currentCol] = {
1011	                    ...cell,
1012	                    svgPath: stitchRegistry[stitchId]?.svgPath || '',
1013	                    isSpanChild: false,
1014	                    parentPos: undefined,
1015	                  };
1016	                }
1017	
1018	                for (let k = 1; k < spanW; k++) {
1019	                  const childCol = currentCol + dir * k;
1020	                  if (childCol >= 0 && childCol < maxColsFromText) {
1021	                    newGrid[gridRowIndex][childCol] = {
1022	                      char: '',
1023	                      svgPath: '',
1024	                      stitchId,
1025	                      isSpanChild: true,
1026	                      parentPos: { row: gridRowIndex, col: currentCol },
1027	                    };
```
